## ⭐ 及格论文详细分析

### 1. Neuroimaging subtypes of adolescent sleep insufficiency stratify natural short sleepers from comorbi

**作者**: Yiwei Chen, Miaoxiu Li, Zhenfeng Zheng, Xinyi Xu, Yongquan Huang, Ruike Chen, Ruoke Zhao, Guanghai Wang, F Jiang, Dan Wu
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70135-6](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70135-6)

**评分**: 21.0 / 14.0 ✅

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 8.0/10 | 8.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 8.0/10 | 8.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 5.0/10 | 5.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文使用脑部MRI数据（medical imaging）通过SuStaIn模型进行神经影像亚型分析（medical image analysis），与这两个关键词高度相关（8分）。虽然涉及机器学习模型，但未明确使用深度学习技术，与deep learning medical imaging有一定关联但非核心（5分）。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    The SuStaIn model deciphers the heterogeneous neurobiology of insufficient sleep and offers a framework for stratified interventions.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过脑部MRI分析识别了青少年睡眠不足的三种神经影像亚型，揭示了不同亚型与遗传、环境或精神疾病的关联，为分层干预提供了框架。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 睡眠不足（青少年少于8小时）具有异质性的神经生物学基础。通过对ABCD研究的脑部MRI数据应用SuStaIn模型，我们识别出三种不同的皮层厚度减小子类型，其起始部位分别位于中央后回、距周皮层和内嗅皮层。这些亚型在睡眠相关决定因素上存在差异。中央后回亚型在睡眠行为和睡眠环境方面与充足睡眠的对照组相似，且未表现出精神共病，这与自然短睡眠者特征一致（尽管睡眠时间短但表型正常）。值得注意的是，该亚型显示出显著超前的大脑年龄，多基因评分分析揭示了其具有短睡眠的遗传易感性。距周皮层亚型与环境因素（如光/噪音污染）相关，睡眠时长在环境因素对皮层变薄的影响中起中介作用。内嗅皮层亚型则表现出更高的精神疾病风险、更年轻的大脑年龄，以及与精神病相关神经递质系统更强的空间相关性。本研究解析了睡眠不足的异质性神经生物学机制，并为分层干预提供了框架。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Insufficient sleep (less than 8 hours for adolescents) has heterogeneous neurobiological underpinnings. Using the SuStaIn model on brain MRI from ABCD Study, we identified three distinct subtypes with reduced cortical thickness, starting from the postcentral, pericalcarine, and entorhinal cortices. The subtypes diverged in sleep-related determinants. The postcentral subtype mirrored the controls of sufficient sleep in sleep behavior and sleep environment and showed no psychiatric comorbidities, which aligned with natural short sleepers (phenotypically normal despite short sleep). Notably, this subtype displayed significantly advanced brain age, and polygenetic score analysis revealed a genetic predisposition for short sleep. The pericalcarine subtype was linked to environmental factors (e.g., light/noise pollution), with sleep duration mediating environmental effects on cortical thinning. The entorhinal subtype showed elevated psychiatric risk, younger brain age, and larger spatial correlations with psychosis-related neurotransmitter systems. This work deciphers the heterogeneous neurobiology of insufficient sleep and offers a framework for stratified interventions.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: neuroimaging, sleep insufficiency, brain MRI, cortical thickness, SuStaIn model, adolescent sleep, neurobiological subtypes, stratified interventions

**深度分析**:

#### 青少年睡眠不足的神经影像亚型：区分自然短睡眠者与共病或环境驱动的睡眠不足

**摘要**:

> 本研究针对青少年睡眠不足（定义为每晚睡眠少于8小时）的异质性神经生物学基础展开研究。研究利用美国青少年脑认知发展（ABCD）研究中的脑部MRI数据，采用亚型与阶段推断（SuStaIn）模型，基于皮层厚度变化识别出三种不同的睡眠不足亚型：后中央皮层亚型、距状旁皮层亚型和内嗅皮层亚型。研究发现，后中央皮层亚型在睡眠行为和环境上与睡眠充足对照组相似，无精神共病，符合自然短睡眠者特征，且显示出显著的大脑年龄提前和短睡眠遗传倾向；距状旁皮层亚型主要与环境因素（如光/噪音污染）相关，睡眠时长在环境因素导致皮层变薄中起中介作用；内嗅皮层亚型则与精神疾病风险升高、大脑年龄更年轻以及与精神病相关神经递质系统的空间相关性更强相关。该研究为理解睡眠不足的异质性神经机制提供了新见解，并为分层干预提供了框架。

**创新点**:
- 首次利用神经影像数据（皮层厚度）对青少年睡眠不足进行客观亚型分类，揭示了其异质性神经基础。
- 结合SuStaIn模型，不仅识别亚型，还模拟了各亚型大脑变化的进展轨迹，增强了动态理解。
- 将神经影像亚型与多维度社会生态因素（环境、遗传、精神共病）关联，实现了跨层次机制阐释。
- 区分了自然短睡眠者与病理/环境驱动的睡眠不足，为精准干预提供了潜在生物标志物。

<details>
<summary>方法</summary>

!!! info

    研究基于ABCD纵向队列，选取客观睡眠时长（Fitbit测量）少于8小时的青少年为睡眠不足组。首先通过全脑皮层厚度（CT）比较识别睡眠相关易感脑区；随后采用SuStaIn模型，以皮层厚度z分数为指标，通过贝叶斯模型选择确定最佳亚型数量（3类），并分配每个个体到最可能的亚型和进展阶段；利用纵向MRI数据计算皮层厚度变化（ΔCT），验证亚型特异性变化模式；最后通过社会生态问卷、大脑年龄计算、多基因风险评分（PRS）、神经递质图谱空间相关分析等，综合表征各亚型的临床、环境和生物学特征。

</details>
<br>

**关键结果**:
- 识别出三种睡眠不足神经影像亚型：后中央皮层亚型（20.86%）、距状旁皮层亚型（48.89%）和内嗅皮层亚型（30.25%）。
- 后中央亚型特征：睡眠行为/环境与对照组相似，无精神共病，大脑年龄显著提前，具有短睡眠遗传倾向。
- 距状旁亚型特征：与环境因素（光/噪音污染）强相关，睡眠时长中介环境对皮层变薄的影响。
- 内嗅亚型特征：精神疾病风险高，大脑年龄更年轻，与精神病相关神经递质系统空间相关性更强。
- 纵向数据显示各亚型皮层厚度变化模式与SuStaIn模拟的进展轨迹高度一致。

**技术栈**: 算法/模型：亚型与阶段推断（SuStaIn）模型、贝叶斯模型选择、线性混合效应模型、中介分析、空间相关分析。, 神经影像处理：FreeSurfer（皮层厚度提取）、Desikan-Killiany图谱、Destrieux图谱。, 数据来源：ABCD研究（MRI、Fitbit睡眠数据、社会生态问卷）、独立自采数据集（验证）。, 分析工具：多基因风险评分（PRS）计算、大脑年龄预测模型、神经递质图谱（受体密度图）。, 统计方法：Bonferroni校正、Cohen's d效应量、交叉验证、Euclidean距离计算。

<details>
<summary>优点</summary>

- 研究设计严谨：基于大样本纵向队列（ABCD），结合客观睡眠测量与多时间点MRI，增强了可靠性。
- 方法先进：采用SuStaIn模型实现亚型与进展阶段同步推断，优于传统聚类方法。
- 多维数据整合：融合神经影像、遗传、环境、临床问卷数据，全面揭示睡眠不足异质性机制。
- 临床转化潜力：亚型分类为区分自然短睡眠与病理性睡眠不足提供了客观影像标志物，有助于个性化干预。
- 验证充分：使用纵向数据和独立数据集验证亚型稳定性与生物学一致性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>局限</summary>

- 睡眠测量依赖Fitbit，虽为客观设备，但仍可能受佩戴依从性影响，且未涵盖睡眠质量多维指标（如睡眠结构）。
- 研究样本主要为美国青少年，文化与环境因素可能限制结论的普适性。
- 亚型分类基于横断面数据推断进展轨迹，虽经纵向验证，但因果机制仍需前瞻性实验进一步确认。
- 环境因素（如光污染）依赖问卷自报，可能存在回忆偏倚或测量误差。
- 未深入探讨各亚型与特定认知功能或长期健康结局的关联。

</details>
<br>

**与研究方向的相关性**:

> 本研究与'医学图像分析'高度相关：核心方法基于脑部MRI图像的定量分析（皮层厚度提取），并采用先进的计算模型（SuStaIn）进行图像驱动的亚型发现。研究展示了神经影像在揭示疾病（睡眠不足）异质性中的关键作用，体现了医学图像分析从描述性统计向模式识别与机制解释的深化，是影像组学在睡眠医学领域的典型应用。

---

### 2. Clusters of vascular aging manifestations predict incident cardiovascular events in the community

**作者**: Thomas T. van Sloten, P. Boutouyrie, Mouad Abouqateb, RM Bruno, RE Climie, F. Zhu, Shuyue Yang, Ali Farzaneh, O. Guedj, N. Danchin, Bruno Pannier, S. Laurent, M. Kamran Ikram, F. Mattace-Raso, M. Kavousi, Xavier Jouven, Christian Spaulding
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-05
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70137-4](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70137-4)

**评分**: 18.0 / 14.0 ✅

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 8.0/10 | 8.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 8.0/10 | 8.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 2.0/10 | 2.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文使用颈动脉超声方法非侵入性地评估血管老化表现，这属于医学影像分析（medical image analysis）和医学成像（medical imaging）的应用范畴，因此这两个关键词相关度较高（8分）。然而，论文摘要和标题中未提及深度学习技术，研究主要基于传统超声成像和统计分析，因此“deep learning medical imaging”相关度较低（2分）。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    It is found that arteriosclerosis and atherosclerosis compared to HVA clusters are independent predictors of CVD, and improve risk stratification for stroke among those at intermediate risk.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过颈动脉超声识别了三种血管老化模式，发现动脉硬化和动脉粥样硬化相比健康血管老化能独立预测心血管事件并改善中风风险分层。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 血管衰老是血管在整个生命周期中功能和结构变化的累积。尽管早期研究表明血管衰老的单一表现与心血管疾病（CVD）风险增加相关，但尚不清楚血管衰老的不同表现在个体层面如何聚集，以及具有不同血管衰老模式的个体是否具有不同的显性CVD进展风险。本研究识别了三种血管衰老模式，包括健康血管衰老（HVA）、动脉硬化和动脉粥样硬化。血管衰老表现通过颈动脉超声方法进行无创评估。主要分析和验证分析分别在两个独立的前瞻性队列中的8360名和2086名参与者中进行。我们发现，与HVA集群相比，动脉硬化和动脉粥样硬化集群是CVD的独立预测因子，并能改善中风险人群的卒中风险分层。血管衰老评估可能有助于识别CVD风险升高的人群。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Vascular aging is the accumulation of functional and structural changes of vessels throughout life. While earlier studies have shown that single manifestation of vascular aging is associated with an increased risk of cardiovascular disease (CVD), it is unknown how the different manifestations of vascular aging cluster at the individual level, and whether individuals with different vascular aging patterns have different risk of progression to overt CVD. Here, we identify three patterns of vascular aging including healthy vascular aging (HVA), arteriosclerosis and atherosclerosis. Vascular aging manifestations were evaluated non-invasively by carotid ultrasound methods. The main and the validation analysis were conducted on 8360 and 2086 participants in two separate prospective cohorts. We find that arteriosclerosis and atherosclerosis compared to HVA clusters are independent predictors of CVD, and improve risk stratification for stroke among those at intermediate risk. Vascular aging evaluation may help identify those at increased risk of CVD.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: vascular aging, cardiovascular disease, carotid ultrasound, arteriosclerosis, atherosclerosis, risk stratification, prospective cohort

**深度分析**:

#### 血管老化表现集群预测社区心血管事件

**摘要**:

> 本研究探讨了血管老化多种表现如何集群化并预测心血管疾病（CVD）。血管老化是血管功能和结构随年龄累积的变化，以往研究多关注单一表现，而本研究通过高分辨率颈动脉超声非侵入性测量多种血管老化参数（如动脉粥样硬化斑块、内膜中层厚度、动脉僵硬度等），在巴黎前瞻性研究III（PPS3，8360名参与者）和鹿特丹研究（2086名参与者）两个独立前瞻性队列中，识别出三种血管老化模式：健康血管老化、动脉硬化主导型和动脉粥样硬化主导型。研究发现，与健康血管老化集群相比，动脉硬化集群与卒中风险独立相关，动脉粥样硬化集群与冠心病风险独立相关，且两种集群均与复合心血管事件及全因死亡率相关。外部验证证实了集群的普适性。在中等风险个体中，加入血管老化集群信息可显著改善卒中风险分层。

**创新点**:
- 首次在人群水平系统识别并验证了血管老化的三种集群模式（健康、动脉硬化型、动脉粥样硬化型）
- 揭示了不同血管老化集群与特定心血管结局（卒中 vs. 冠心病）的差异关联
- 证明了血管老化集群在传统风险因素基础上对卒中风险分层的增量预测价值
- 采用多队列设计（发现队列+外部验证队列）增强结果可靠性
- 利用颈动脉超声一站式评估多种血管老化参数，实现非侵入性综合测量

<details>
<summary>方法</summary>

!!! info

    研究采用前瞻性队列设计。在PPS3发现队列中，对8360名无CVD参与者进行颈动脉超声检查，测量动脉粥样硬化参数（斑块、IMT）、动脉僵硬度参数（DC、YEM、局部PWV等）及动脉重构参数（直径）。使用聚类分析识别血管老化模式。通过Cox比例风险模型评估集群与结局（卒中、冠心病、复合事件、全因死亡）的关联，调整传统风险因素。采用内部验证（Bootstrap）和外部验证（鹿特丹研究）检验稳健性。在中等风险亚组中，通过C统计量评估集群对传统风险评分（SCORE2、美国汇总风险方程）的增量预测价值。

</details>
<br>

**关键结果**:
- 识别出三种血管老化集群：健康血管老化（47.8%）、动脉硬化型（25.2%）、动脉粥样硬化型（27.0%）
- 动脉硬化集群与卒中风险显著相关（HR 1.76），动脉粥样硬化集群与冠心病风险显著相关（HR 1.53）
- 两种异常集群均与复合心血管事件（HR约1.5）及全因死亡率（HR约1.5）相关
- 外部验证证实集群模式可跨人群推广，关联一致
- 在中等风险个体中，加入集群信息使卒中风险区分度显著提升（SCORE2模型提升7.8%）

**技术栈**: 聚类分析（未指定具体算法，可能为k-means或层次聚类）, Cox比例风险回归模型, Kaplan-Meier生存曲线, Bootstrap内部验证, C统计量（AUC）用于模型区分度评估, 竞争风险模型（敏感性分析）, 多重插补处理缺失数据

<details>
<summary>优点</summary>

- 大样本前瞻性设计（超万人队列）提供统计效力
- 多队列验证（发现+外部验证）增强结果普适性
- 综合评估多种血管老化参数，全面反映血管状态
- 临床转化价值明确，展示了风险分层的实际应用潜力
- 方法学严谨，包括多重敏感性分析和亚组分析

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>局限</summary>

- 研究人群主要为欧洲中老年，结果外推至其他种族/年龄组需谨慎
- 颈动脉超声参数可能受操作者及设备差异影响
- 未纳入其他血管床（如冠状动脉、股动脉）评估
- 残余混杂可能（如未测量的生活方式因素）
- 中等风险亚组样本量相对较小，增量预测结果需进一步验证

</details>
<br>

**与研究方向的相关性**:

> 论文与'医学图像分析'高度相关：核心数据来源于颈动脉超声图像分析，通过超声测量IMT、斑块、动脉直径等结构参数，并基于图像衍生功能参数（如僵硬度指标）。研究本质上是将医学图像（超声）提取的定量特征用于表型分型（聚类）和预后预测，体现了医学图像分析在心血管风险分层中的关键应用。

---

### 3. Assessing the micromechanical architecture of joint tissues with speckle rheological microscopy

**作者**: Nichaluk Leartprapun, Fernando P. S. Guastaldi, Mark A. Randolph, Robert W. Redmond, Seemantini K. Nadkarni
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70248-y](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70248-y)

**评分**: 15.0 / 14.0 ✅

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 7.0/10 | 7.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 8.0/10 | 8.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文开发了一种名为SHEAR的非接触式成像技术，用于评估关节组织的粘弹性行为，属于医学成像领域，因此与'medical imaging'高度相关（8分），与'medical image analysis'有一定相关性（7分）。然而，论文未提及深度学习技术，因此'deep learning medical imaging'完全无关（0分）。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    Speckle rHEologicAl micRoscopy (SHEAR) is presented, offering a promising non-destructive imaging tool for assessing mechanical function in degenerative joint disease, and has the potential to provide a powerful tool for biomechanical analysis of joint structures.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究开发了一种非接触式成像技术SHEAR，用于评估关节组织的粘弹性行为，并在猪和人类关节组织中验证了其有效性，为退行性关节疾病的诊断和治疗提供了新工具。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 关节组织依赖其固态（弹性）与液态（黏性）成分之间精细调控的相互作用来维持机械功能。疾病或创伤导致的成分降解会破坏关节组织的弹性和黏性响应特性，直接损害关节功能。本研究提出散斑流变显微成像技术（Speckle rHEologicAl micRoscopy, SHEAR），用于在不接触或干扰样本的情况下研究完整关节组织的黏弹性行为，为评估退行性关节疾病的机械功能提供了一种前景广阔的无损成像工具。在健康猪膝关节组织中，SHEAR与传统流变仪的测量结果呈现高度相关性。在具有局灶性损伤的猪软骨组织以及接受膝关节置换术的人类患者手术切除的软骨标本中，SHEAR揭示了组织弹性和黏性特征的双重转变。SHEAR技术有望为关节结构的生物力学分析提供强大工具，并为改进退行性关节疾病的诊断与治疗开辟新路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Joint tissues rely on a finely tuned interplay between solid (elastic) and fluid (viscous) constituents to support their mechanical function. Degradation of these constituents due to disease or trauma disrupts the elastic and viscous susceptibility of joint tissues, directly impairing joint function. We present Speckle rHEologicAl micRoscopy (SHEAR) to investigate the viscoelastic behavior of intact joint tissues without making contact or otherwise manipulating the sample, offering a promising non-destructive imaging tool for assessing mechanical function in degenerative joint disease. SHEAR demonstrated strong correlation to conventional rheometer in healthy swine knee joint tissues. In swine cartilage with focal lesions and surgically excised cartilage specimens from human patients undergoing knee replacement, SHEAR revealed transformation in both the elastic and viscous landscape of the tissue. SHEAR has the potential to provide a powerful tool for biomechanical analysis of joint structures and pave new paths for improved diagnosis and therapy of degenerative joint disease.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: speckle rheological microscopy, viscoelastic behavior, joint tissues, non-destructive imaging, degenerative joint disease, biomechanical analysis, SHEAR

**深度分析**:

#### 利用散斑流变显微技术评估关节组织的微机械结构

**摘要**:

> 本研究针对骨关节炎等退行性关节疾病中关节组织机械性能退化的问题，开发了一种名为散斑流变显微技术（SHEAR）的非接触式光学成像方法。该方法通过分析组织内源性散射结构的布朗运动引起的散斑波动，无需对样本施加机械变形或破坏，即可实现完整关节组织的高分辨率粘弹性映射。研究在健康猪膝关节组织上验证了SHEAR与传统流变仪的相关性，并在猪软骨局灶性病变及人类膝关节置换术切除的软骨样本中，成功揭示了组织弹性与粘性景观的转变。SHEAR为关节结构的生物力学分析提供了有力工具，有望推动退行性关节疾病的诊断与治疗。

**创新点**:
- 开发了非接触、非破坏性的散斑流变显微技术（SHEAR），可直接在完整组织上映射粘弹性
- 首次实现了关节组织微环境中弹性与粘性模量的频率依赖性三维（2D+频率）映射
- 通过分析组织内源性散射结构的布朗运动，避免了传统方法所需的样本机械变形或几何制备
- 在退行性关节疾病模型中揭示了组织粘弹性景观的转变，超越了单一弹性测量的局限
- 技术简单易用，具备未来临床转化潜力，适用于关节镜手术和组织工程应用

<details>
<summary>方法</summary>

!!! info

    SHEAR基于扩散波光谱学原理，利用相干光照射组织产生散斑图案，通过高速CMOS相机记录散斑强度随时间波动。数据处理包括：1）计算散斑强度自相关函数；2）通过扩散波光谱公式推导组织超微结构的均方位移（MSD）；3）分析MSD的幂律标度指数α；4）应用广义斯托克斯-爱因斯坦关系（GSER）计算频率依赖的复剪切模量G*(ω)=G′(ω)+iG″(ω)，从而分离弹性模量G′和粘性模量G″。

</details>
<br>

**关键结果**:
- SHEAR在健康猪膝关节组织（软骨、半月板、肌腱、韧带）中表现出与传统流变仪的良好相关性
- 在猪软骨局灶性病变模型中，SHEAR检测到弹性与粘性模量的显著变化
- 在人类膝关节置换术切除的退行性软骨样本中，SHEAR揭示了组织粘弹性景观的转变
- 频率依赖性映射显示，退行性组织在特定频率下弹性与粘性行为发生特征性改变
- SHEAR能够区分组织微环境中固体样（负载支撑）与流体样（减震）机械特性的贡献

**技术栈**: 算法：散斑强度自相关分析、扩散波光谱学（DWS）、广义斯托克斯-爱因斯坦关系（GSER）, 数学方法：均方位移（MSD）计算、幂律标度指数α分析、复剪切模量分解, 工具：线性偏振单色光源、高速CMOS相机、直立显微镜, 数据处理：像素级时间序列分析、频率依赖性粘弹性重建

<details>
<summary>优点</summary>

- 非接触、非破坏性测量，保持样本原始状态，适用于脆弱组织或工程化构建体
- 高空间分辨率，能够映射组织微环境的局部粘弹性异质性
- 同时量化弹性与粘性行为，提供比单一弹性测量更全面的机械特性表征
- 无需复杂样本制备或机械加载装置，操作简便
- 在退行性关节疾病模型中显示出诊断潜力，具备临床转化前景

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>局限</summary>

- 目前仅适用于离体组织样本，尚未在活体或体内环境中验证
- 深度整合信号可能限制对特定深度的分辨率，需进一步优化层析能力
- 依赖于组织内源性散射结构，对于高度透明或低散射组织可能灵敏度不足
- 研究样本量有限，需更大规模验证以确认临床适用性
- 技术对运动伪影敏感，在活体应用中可能需运动补偿算法

</details>
<br>

**与研究方向的相关性**:

> 本研究与'医学图像分析'高度相关：SHEAR本质上是一种基于光学成像的生物力学映射技术，通过分析散斑波动图像序列，重建组织粘弹性参数的空间分布图。它扩展了医学图像分析的传统范畴（如结构或功能成像），引入了微机械特性定量成像的新维度，为退行性关节疾病的早期诊断、治疗评估及组织工程提供了新型图像分析工具。

---

### 4. Multimodal evidence for hippocampal engagement and modulation by functional connectivity-guided pari

**作者**: Zhuoran Li, Nicholas T. Trapp, J. Bruss, Xianqing Liu, Kang Wu, Ziyan Chen, Amit Etkin, Matthew A. Howard, Aaron D. Boes, Jing Jiang
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-08
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70346-x](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70346-x)

**评分**: 14.0 / 14.0 ✅

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 6.0/10 | 6.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 8.0/10 | 8.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文使用功能磁共振成像（fMRI）作为主要神经影像技术来研究海马体活动，与'medical imaging'高度相关（8分）。研究涉及神经影像数据分析，与'medical image analysis'有一定关联（6分）。但论文未提及深度学习技术，与'deep learning medical imaging'完全无关（0分）。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    These findings provide multimodal causal neural evidence and important mechanistic insights supporting the development of personalized neuromodulation strategies aimed at improving hippocampus-dependent functions.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过结合经颅磁刺激与颅内脑电图和功能磁共振成像，提供了海马体参与和调节的多模态因果神经证据，支持个性化神经调节策略的发展。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 海马体活动支撑记忆及诸多其他脑功能。基于海马体功能连接（FC）引导的经颅磁刺激（TMS）在改善记忆方面展现出潜力，但尚缺乏其能够有效介入并调节海马体活动的直接神经证据。本研究结合了两种方法：在8名神经外科患者中采用TMS与颅内脑电图（iEEG）同步记录，并在79名神经健康的参与者中采用TMS与功能磁共振成像（fMRI）结合。我们发现：（1）基于海马体-FC个体化定位的顶叶皮层单脉冲TMS，优先在海马体内诱发出具有特异性的时域与频域活动模式；（2）TMS诱发的海马体反应差异与个体顶叶-海马体FC强度差异相关；（3）针对海马体-FC引导的顶叶皮层进行重复性TMS，能够选择性抑制海马体theta振荡。这些发现提供了多模态因果神经证据及重要的机制性见解，为开发旨在改善海马体依赖功能的个体化神经调控策略提供了支持。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Hippocampal activity supports memory and many other brain functions. Transcranial magnetic stimulation (TMS) guided by hippocampal functional connectivity (FC) shows promise in improving memory, but direct neural evidence of its capacity to engage and modulate hippocampal activity is lacking. Here we combined TMS with intracranial electroencephalography (iEEG) in 8 neurosurgical patients and with functional magnetic resonance imaging (fMRI) in 79 neurologically healthy participants. We identified that (1) single-pulse TMS to individualized parietal cortex guided by hippocampal-FC preferentially evoked distinct temporal and spectral activity patterns in the hippocampus, (2) variability in TMS-evoked hippocampal responses related to individual differences in parietal-hippocampus FC strength, and (3) repetitive TMS to hippocampal-FC-guided parietal cortex selectively suppressed hippocampal theta oscillations. These findings provide multimodal causal neural evidence and important mechanistic insights supporting the development of personalized neuromodulation strategies aimed at improving hippocampus-dependent functions.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: hippocampal activity, transcranial magnetic stimulation, functional magnetic resonance imaging, functional connectivity, intracranial electroencephalography, personalized neuromodulation, theta oscillations, parietal cortex

**深度分析**:

#### 功能连接引导的顶叶经颅磁刺激对海马体参与和调节的多模态证据

**摘要**:

> 本研究针对海马体功能连接引导的经颅磁刺激（TMS）在改善记忆方面缺乏直接神经证据的问题，通过多模态方法探究了个性化顶叶TMS对海马体活动的因果性影响。研究结合了8名神经外科患者的颅内脑电图（iEEG）和79名健康参与者的功能磁共振成像（fMRI），采用功能连接引导的个性化TMS定位技术。研究发现：（1）基于海马体功能连接引导的顶叶单脉冲TMS能特异性诱发海马体独特的时域和频域活动模式；（2）TMS诱发的海马体反应变异与个体顶叶-海马体功能连接强度相关；（3）重复性TMS能选择性抑制海马体θ振荡。这些发现为开发针对海马体依赖性功能的个性化神经调控策略提供了多模态因果神经证据和机制性见解。

**创新点**:
- 首次结合TMS-iEEG和TMS-fMRI多模态技术，直接验证功能连接引导的顶叶TMS对海马体活动的因果性调控
- 开发了个性化功能连接引导的TMS定位方法，实现基于个体脑网络特征的精准神经调控
- 揭示了TMS诱发的海马体反应与顶叶-海马体功能连接强度的个体化关联机制
- 发现重复性TMS能特异性调节海马体θ振荡，为记忆相关神经振荡调控提供了新证据

<details>
<summary>方法</summary>

!!! info

    研究采用双模态实验设计：1）在8名植入颅内电极的癫痫患者中，实施基于静息态fMRI功能连接引导的个性化顶叶单脉冲TMS，同步记录iEEG数据；2）在79名健康参与者中，进行相同的TMS干预并采集fMRI数据。技术路线包括：个性化TMS靶点定位（基于海马体功能连接图谱）、TMS参数优化、多模态数据采集（iEEG/fMRI）、信号预处理（FieldTrip、fMRIPrep）、时频分析、功能连接分析、统计检验（非参数置换检验）等。

</details>
<br>

**关键结果**:
- 单脉冲TMS能特异性诱发海马体早期（<100ms）和高频（>30Hz）神经活动
- 个体顶叶-海马体功能连接强度正向预测TMS诱发的海马体反应幅度
- 重复性TMS（10Hz）显著抑制海马体θ波段（4-8Hz）振荡功率
- 多模态证据一致显示功能连接引导的TMS能有效调控海马体神经活动

**技术栈**: 神经影像技术：fMRI（3T）、颅内脑电图（iEEG）, 神经调控技术：经颅磁刺激（TMS）、重复性TMS（rTMS）, 分析工具：FieldTrip（EEG分析）、fMRIPrep（fMRI预处理）、ANTs（图像配准）、EEGLAB, 数学方法：功能连接分析（静息态fMRI）、时频分析（小波变换）、非参数统计检验（置换检验）, 编程语言：MATLAB、Python

<details>
<summary>优点</summary>

- 创新性地结合了侵入性和非侵入性多模态技术，提供了因果性神经证据
- 采用个性化功能连接引导的TMS定位，提高了神经调控的精准性
- 样本量较大（iEEG患者8人，fMRI健康人79人），增强了结果的可靠性
- 方法学严谨，包括严格的数据预处理流程和多重比较校正
- 研究结果具有明确的临床转化价值，为个性化神经调控提供了新思路

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>局限</summary>

- iEEG样本量较小（n=8），且患者群体（癫痫）可能影响结果的普适性
- TMS对海马体的影响是间接通过顶叶皮层介导的，直接机制仍需进一步验证
- 研究主要关注神经生理效应，缺乏行为学结果（如记忆表现）的直接关联
- fMRI的时间分辨率有限，难以捕捉TMS诱发的快速神经动态变化
- 未系统比较不同TMS参数（如频率、强度）对海马体调控的差异化影响

</details>
<br>

**与研究方向的相关性**:

> 本研究与'医学图像分析'高度相关：1）核心数据来源于fMRI和iEEG等医学影像模态；2）采用先进的医学图像处理流程（fMRIPrep、ANTs配准）进行数据预处理；3）基于静息态fMRI的功能连接分析是研究的关键方法；4）个性化TMS靶点定位依赖于fMRI脑网络图谱分析；5）研究结果展示了多模态医学影像在神经调控疗效评估中的重要作用。

## 📋 所有论文列表

### 1. ✅ Neuroimaging subtypes of adolescent sleep insufficiency stratify natural short sleepers from comorbidity or environment driven insufficiency

**作者**: Yiwei Chen, Miaoxiu Li, Zhenfeng Zheng, Xinyi Xu, Yongquan Huang, Ruike Chen, Ruoke Zhao, Guanghai Wang, F Jiang, Dan Wu
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70135-6](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70135-6)

**评分**: 21.0 / 14.0 ✅

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 8.0/10 | 8.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 8.0/10 | 8.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 5.0/10 | 5.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文使用脑部MRI数据（medical imaging）通过SuStaIn模型进行神经影像亚型分析（medical image analysis），与这两个关键词高度相关（8分）。虽然涉及机器学习模型，但未明确使用深度学习技术，与deep learning medical imaging有一定关联但非核心（5分）。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    The SuStaIn model deciphers the heterogeneous neurobiology of insufficient sleep and offers a framework for stratified interventions.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过脑部MRI分析识别了青少年睡眠不足的三种神经影像亚型，揭示了不同亚型与遗传、环境或精神疾病的关联，为分层干预提供了框架。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 睡眠不足（青少年少于8小时）具有异质性的神经生物学基础。通过对ABCD研究的脑部MRI数据应用SuStaIn模型，我们识别出三种不同的皮层厚度减小子类型，其起始部位分别位于中央后回、距周皮层和内嗅皮层。这些亚型在睡眠相关决定因素上存在差异。中央后回亚型在睡眠行为和睡眠环境方面与充足睡眠的对照组相似，且未表现出精神共病，这与自然短睡眠者特征一致（尽管睡眠时间短但表型正常）。值得注意的是，该亚型显示出显著超前的大脑年龄，多基因评分分析揭示了其具有短睡眠的遗传易感性。距周皮层亚型与环境因素（如光/噪音污染）相关，睡眠时长在环境因素对皮层变薄的影响中起中介作用。内嗅皮层亚型则表现出更高的精神疾病风险、更年轻的大脑年龄，以及与精神病相关神经递质系统更强的空间相关性。本研究解析了睡眠不足的异质性神经生物学机制，并为分层干预提供了框架。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Insufficient sleep (less than 8 hours for adolescents) has heterogeneous neurobiological underpinnings. Using the SuStaIn model on brain MRI from ABCD Study, we identified three distinct subtypes with reduced cortical thickness, starting from the postcentral, pericalcarine, and entorhinal cortices. The subtypes diverged in sleep-related determinants. The postcentral subtype mirrored the controls of sufficient sleep in sleep behavior and sleep environment and showed no psychiatric comorbidities, which aligned with natural short sleepers (phenotypically normal despite short sleep). Notably, this subtype displayed significantly advanced brain age, and polygenetic score analysis revealed a genetic predisposition for short sleep. The pericalcarine subtype was linked to environmental factors (e.g., light/noise pollution), with sleep duration mediating environmental effects on cortical thinning. The entorhinal subtype showed elevated psychiatric risk, younger brain age, and larger spatial correlations with psychosis-related neurotransmitter systems. This work deciphers the heterogeneous neurobiology of insufficient sleep and offers a framework for stratified interventions.

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过颈动脉超声识别了三种血管老化模式，发现动脉硬化和动脉粥样硬化相比健康血管老化能独立预测心血管事件并改善中风风险分层。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 血管衰老是血管在整个生命周期中功能和结构变化的累积。尽管早期研究表明血管衰老的单一表现与心血管疾病（CVD）风险增加相关，但尚不清楚血管衰老的不同表现在个体层面如何聚集，以及具有不同血管衰老模式的个体是否具有不同的显性CVD进展风险。本研究识别了三种血管衰老模式，包括健康血管衰老（HVA）、动脉硬化和动脉粥样硬化。血管衰老表现通过颈动脉超声方法进行无创评估。主要分析和验证分析分别在两个独立的前瞻性队列中的8360名和2086名参与者中进行。我们发现，与HVA集群相比，动脉硬化和动脉粥样硬化集群是CVD的独立预测因子，并能改善中风险人群的卒中风险分层。血管衰老评估可能有助于识别CVD风险升高的人群。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Vascular aging is the accumulation of functional and structural changes of vessels throughout life. While earlier studies have shown that single manifestation of vascular aging is associated with an increased risk of cardiovascular disease (CVD), it is unknown how the different manifestations of vascular aging cluster at the individual level, and whether individuals with different vascular aging patterns have different risk of progression to overt CVD. Here, we identify three patterns of vascular aging including healthy vascular aging (HVA), arteriosclerosis and atherosclerosis. Vascular aging manifestations were evaluated non-invasively by carotid ultrasound methods. The main and the validation analysis were conducted on 8360 and 2086 participants in two separate prospective cohorts. We find that arteriosclerosis and atherosclerosis compared to HVA clusters are independent predictors of CVD, and improve risk stratification for stroke among those at intermediate risk. Vascular aging evaluation may help identify those at increased risk of CVD.

</details>
<br>

### 3. ✅ Assessing the micromechanical architecture of joint tissues with speckle rheological microscopy

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    Speckle rHEologicAl micRoscopy (SHEAR) is presented, offering a promising non-destructive imaging tool for assessing mechanical function in degenerative joint disease, and has the potential to provide a powerful tool for biomechanical analysis of joint structures.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究开发了一种非接触式成像技术SHEAR，用于评估关节组织的粘弹性行为，并在猪和人类关节组织中验证了其有效性，为退行性关节疾病的诊断和治疗提供了新工具。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 关节组织依赖其固态（弹性）与液态（黏性）成分之间精细调控的相互作用来维持机械功能。疾病或创伤导致的成分降解会破坏关节组织的弹性和黏性响应特性，直接损害关节功能。本研究提出散斑流变显微成像技术（Speckle rHEologicAl micRoscopy, SHEAR），用于在不接触或干扰样本的情况下研究完整关节组织的黏弹性行为，为评估退行性关节疾病的机械功能提供了一种前景广阔的无损成像工具。在健康猪膝关节组织中，SHEAR与传统流变仪的测量结果呈现高度相关性。在具有局灶性损伤的猪软骨组织以及接受膝关节置换术的人类患者手术切除的软骨标本中，SHEAR揭示了组织弹性和黏性特征的双重转变。SHEAR技术有望为关节结构的生物力学分析提供强大工具，并为改进退行性关节疾病的诊断与治疗开辟新路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Joint tissues rely on a finely tuned interplay between solid (elastic) and fluid (viscous) constituents to support their mechanical function. Degradation of these constituents due to disease or trauma disrupts the elastic and viscous susceptibility of joint tissues, directly impairing joint function. We present Speckle rHEologicAl micRoscopy (SHEAR) to investigate the viscoelastic behavior of intact joint tissues without making contact or otherwise manipulating the sample, offering a promising non-destructive imaging tool for assessing mechanical function in degenerative joint disease. SHEAR demonstrated strong correlation to conventional rheometer in healthy swine knee joint tissues. In swine cartilage with focal lesions and surgically excised cartilage specimens from human patients undergoing knee replacement, SHEAR revealed transformation in both the elastic and viscous landscape of the tissue. SHEAR has the potential to provide a powerful tool for biomechanical analysis of joint structures and pave new paths for improved diagnosis and therapy of degenerative joint disease.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: speckle rheological microscopy, viscoelastic behavior, joint tissues, non-destructive imaging, degenerative joint disease, biomechanical analysis, SHEAR

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    These findings provide multimodal causal neural evidence and important mechanistic insights supporting the development of personalized neuromodulation strategies aimed at improving hippocampus-dependent functions.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过结合经颅磁刺激与颅内脑电图和功能磁共振成像，提供了海马体参与和调节的多模态因果神经证据，支持个性化神经调节策略的发展。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 海马体活动支撑记忆及诸多其他脑功能。基于海马体功能连接（FC）引导的经颅磁刺激（TMS）在改善记忆方面展现出潜力，但尚缺乏其能够有效介入并调节海马体活动的直接神经证据。本研究结合了两种方法：在8名神经外科患者中采用TMS与颅内脑电图（iEEG）同步记录，并在79名神经健康的参与者中采用TMS与功能磁共振成像（fMRI）结合。我们发现：（1）基于海马体-FC个体化定位的顶叶皮层单脉冲TMS，优先在海马体内诱发出具有特异性的时域与频域活动模式；（2）TMS诱发的海马体反应差异与个体顶叶-海马体FC强度差异相关；（3）针对海马体-FC引导的顶叶皮层进行重复性TMS，能够选择性抑制海马体theta振荡。这些发现提供了多模态因果神经证据及重要的机制性见解，为开发旨在改善海马体依赖功能的个体化神经调控策略提供了支持。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Hippocampal activity supports memory and many other brain functions. Transcranial magnetic stimulation (TMS) guided by hippocampal functional connectivity (FC) shows promise in improving memory, but direct neural evidence of its capacity to engage and modulate hippocampal activity is lacking. Here we combined TMS with intracranial electroencephalography (iEEG) in 8 neurosurgical patients and with functional magnetic resonance imaging (fMRI) in 79 neurologically healthy participants. We identified that (1) single-pulse TMS to individualized parietal cortex guided by hippocampal-FC preferentially evoked distinct temporal and spectral activity patterns in the hippocampus, (2) variability in TMS-evoked hippocampal responses related to individual differences in parietal-hippocampus FC strength, and (3) repetitive TMS to hippocampal-FC-guided parietal cortex selectively suppressed hippocampal theta oscillations. These findings provide multimodal causal neural evidence and important mechanistic insights supporting the development of personalized neuromodulation strategies aimed at improving hippocampus-dependent functions.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: hippocampal activity, transcranial magnetic stimulation, functional magnetic resonance imaging, functional connectivity, intracranial electroencephalography, personalized neuromodulation, theta oscillations, parietal cortex

### 5. ❌ Cryo-ET comparison of the hierarchical ultrastructure of silkworm, spider, and artificial silk fibers

**作者**: Kai Song, Haonan Zhang, Xueli Zhang, Yan Li, Ping Zhu
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70477-1](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70477-1)

**评分**: 4.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 2.0/10 | 2.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 2.0/10 | 2.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文使用cryo-electron tomography（冷冻电子断层扫描）分析丝纤维的超微结构，这是一种成像技术，与'medical imaging'和'medical image analysis'有微弱关联（评分2分），因为医学影像分析也涉及图像处理和解剖结构可视化，但本文研究对象是材料科学中的丝纤维，而非医学或临床图像。'deep learning medical imaging'完全无关（评分0分），因为论文未涉及深度学习或人工智能方法。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    本研究应用冷冻电子断层扫描比较了蚕丝、蜘蛛丝和人工丝纤维的层次超微结构，揭示了天然丝中纳米纤维的排列模式差异，为理解丝形成和仿生纤维设计提供了结构基础。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 蜘蛛丝与蚕丝以其卓越的机械性能而闻名，这源于其超微结构的有序组织。然而，这种结构尚未被完全理解。本研究采用冷冻电子断层扫描技术（cryo-ET）来解析蚕丝、蜘蛛丝及人工丝的多层级结构。在蚕丝中，我们观察到直径约3.6纳米的纳米原纤，它们通过大量桥接结构相互连接，代表了目前冷冻电子断层扫描技术所能解析的最小原纤特征。这些纳米原纤沿纤维轴方向排列，并组织成鱼骨状图案，通过层层堆叠构建出微米尺度的丝纤维。蜘蛛丝则呈现出紧密排列的纳米原纤，具有近乎完美的轴向排列和极少的空隙。相比之下，蚕丝显示出区域性异质的间隙，而人工丝则缺乏天然材料特有的有序堆积特征。这些发现为理解丝蛋白的形成机制提供了结构基础，并可能指导未来的仿生纤维设计。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Spider and silkworm silks are renowned for their exceptional mechanical properties, which arises from their ultrastructural organization. However, this architecture remains incompletely understood. Here, we apply cryo-electron tomography to examine the hierarchical organization of silkworm, spider, and artificial silks. In silkworm silk, we observe nanofibrils of ~3.6 nm in diameter, interconnected by abundant bridges and representing the smallest fibrillar features currently accessible by cryo-ET. These nanofibrils align with the fiber axis and are organized into a herringbone pattern, with stacked layers building the micron-scale filament. Spider silk displays densely packed nanofibrils with near-perfect axial alignment and minimal voids. In contrast, silkworm silk shows regionally heterogeneous gaps, whereas artificial silk lacks the ordered packing characteristic of natural materials. These observations provide a structural basis for understanding silk formation and may guide future biomimetic fiber design.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: cryo-electron tomography, silkworm silk, spider silk, artificial silk, hierarchical ultrastructure, nanofibrils, biomimetic fiber design, mechanical properties

### 6. ❌ NF-κB activation in astrocytes impairs wound healing after traumatic brain injury in male mice

**作者**: Tabea Hein, Ester Nespoli, Marsela Hakani, Heinrich Wendt, Stephanie Nadine May, Jasmin Jorzik, Duygu Yagdiran, Judith Stefanie Schlett, Konstantinos Tsesmelis, Miltiadis Tsesmelis, V Prex, Melanie Mettang, Alireza Abaei, Volker Rasche, Michael Lattke, Franz Oswald, Markus Huber-Lang, Leda Dimou, Thomas Wirth, Bernd Baumann
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70304-7](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70304-7)

**评分**: 4.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 2.0/10 | 2.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 2.0/10 | 2.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究创伤性脑损伤（TBI）后星形胶质细胞中NF-κB激活对伤口愈合的影响，属于神经科学和分子病理学领域。虽然涉及脑损伤模型，但未使用医学图像分析技术（如MRI、CT图像处理），也未提及深度学习在医学成像中的应用。因此，与'medical image analysis'和'medical imaging'仅有微弱关联（因涉及脑损伤研究背景），与'deep learning medical imaging'完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    It is shown that TBI-mediated NF-κB activation in astrocytes impairs their homeostatic functions, amplifies the post-traumatic neuroimmune response and disturbs the multicellular CNS scar development in a male mouse model of TBI.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究发现创伤性脑损伤后星形胶质细胞中NF-κB的激活会损害其稳态功能，放大神经免疫反应并阻碍中枢神经系统疤痕的良性修复，从而恶化损伤预后。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 创伤性脑损伤（TBI）是一种复杂的疾病状态，多种病理生理机制共同影响其病程发展。在初始机械性损伤后，神经胶质细胞与外周浸润免疫细胞的神经炎症反应共同决定了整体临床结局。然而，这些继发性过程及其导致有益或有害结果的分子决定因素尚未明确。本研究通过雄性小鼠TBI模型揭示，星形胶质细胞中TBI介导的核因子κB（NF-κB）激活会损害其稳态功能，放大创伤后神经免疫反应，并扰乱中枢神经系统多细胞瘢痕的形成。我们的结果进一步证实了胶质界膜边界形成的特异性缺陷，并证实NF-κB激活的星形胶质细胞诱导的旁分泌信号通路会阻碍TBI后中枢神经系统完整性的有益修复。这些发现深化了我们对NF-κB介导的创伤后病理生理机制的理解，为未来开发改善TBI预后的靶向治疗策略提供了依据。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Traumatic brain injury (TBI) is a complex condition in which multiple pathophysiological mechanisms influence the course of the disease. After the initial mechanical impact, neuroinflammatory reactions of glial cells along with infiltrating peripheral immune cells determine the overall clinical outcome. However, these secondary processes and their molecular determinants promoting either beneficial or detrimental consequences are not well-defined. Here, we show that TBI-mediated NF-κB activation in astrocytes impairs their homeostatic functions, amplifies the post-traumatic neuroimmune response and disturbs the multicellular CNS scar development in a male mouse model of TBI. Our results further demonstrate a specific deficit in the formation of the glial limitans border and establish that paracrine signaling pathways induced by NF-κB-activated astrocytes can prevent a beneficial restoration of the CNS integrity after TBI. These findings enhance our understanding on the NF-κB-mediated post-traumatic pathophysiology and provide information on future targeted therapies to improve TBI outcome.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: traumatic brain injury, NF-κB activation, astrocytes, neuroimmune response, glial limitans, CNS scar development, paracrine signaling, mouse model

### 7. ❌ Nonequilibrium ordering dynamics of confined soft alginate hydrogel colloids driven by time-evolving electrostatic interactions

**作者**: In Hwan Jung, Chetan Revadekar, Hag Sung Lee, Hyerim Hwang, Hyosung An, Bum Jun Park

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 阐明非平衡胶体系统中排斥相互作用如何演化形成有序结构仍是一个核心挑战，部分原因是极少有实验平台能提供粒子尺度的结构演化观测途径。本文表明，限制于溴化环己烷（CHB）乳液液滴内的海藻酸盐水凝胶胶体可形成一个可控模型系统，其中静电相互作用随时间演化并驱动有序化。从周围水相扩散的Ba²⁺离子逐步交联海藻酸胶滴，增加其表面电荷，同时浮力使其在CHB相内压实成局部的准二维层状结构。随着静电排斥增强，组装体从无序态演化为六方有序结构。通过将布朗动力学模拟与实验测得的晶格弹性常数进行校准，我们将有效德拜屏蔽长度限定在≈2.5–3 μm范围内。定量成像进一步表明，当无量纲相互作用参数（定义为静电相互作用能与热能之比）达到≈117–149时，有序结构开始形成。该有序态在机械和磁扰动下表现出可逆的无序-有序转变行为，这为研究受限条件下电荷调控的胶体有序化提供了一个稳健的非平衡实验平台。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Abstract Elucidating how repulsive interactions evolve to generate ordered structures in nonequilibrium colloidal systems remains a central challenge, partly because few experimental platforms provide particle-resolved access to their structural evolution. Here we show that alginate hydrogel colloids confined within cyclohexyl bromide (CHB) emulsion droplets form a controllable model system in which electrostatic interactions evolve in time and drive ordering. Ba 2+ ions diffusing from the surrounding aqueous phase progressively crosslink the alginate droplets, increasing their surface charge, while buoyancy compacts them into locally quasi-two-dimensional layers within the CHB phase. As electrostatic repulsion strengthens, the assembly evolves from a disordered state to a hexagonally ordered structure. By calibrating Brownian dynamics simulations to the experimentally measured lattice spring constant, we constrain the effective Debye screening length to ≈2.5–3 μm. Quantitative imaging further shows that ordering emerges once a dimensionless interaction parameter—defined as the ratio of electrostatic interaction energy to thermal energy—reaches values of ≈117–149. The ordered state exhibits reversible disordered–order behavior under mechanical and magnetic perturbations, demonstrating a robust nonequilibrium platform for probing charge-regulated colloidal ordering under confinement.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: alginate hydrogel colloids, nonequilibrium ordering dynamics, electrostatic interactions, colloidal assembly, Brownian dynamics simulations, confinement, Debye screening length, hexagonally ordered structure

---

### 8. ❌ Lyn governs the establishment and maintenance of B cell anergy by suppressing PI3K signaling

**作者**: Brigita E. Fiske, Scott M. Wemlinger, Bergren W. Crute, Andrew Getahun
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    It is shown that Ars/A1 B cells require Lyn to establish and maintain B cell unresponsiveness via restricting PI3K-dependent signaling pathways, and that the autoimmunity associated with dysregulated Lyn function may, in part, be due to an inability of these autoreactive B cells to become tolerized.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究发现Lyn激酶通过限制PI3K依赖的信号通路来建立和维持自身反应性B细胞的无反应状态，揭示了Lyn功能失调可能导致自身免疫的部分机制。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> Src家族激酶Lyn已知参与外周B细胞耐受的诱导与维持；然而，在机制层面将其致耐受功能与Lyn在B细胞及髓系细胞发育活化中的作用进行区分具有挑战性。本研究采用他莫昔芬诱导型、B细胞特异性Lyn基因敲除系统，实现了仅在B细胞中急性消除Lyn，从而最大程度减少混杂因素。该遗传工具与携带自身反应性外周B细胞的免疫球蛋白转基因小鼠联用，以DNA为靶标的Ars/A1 B细胞需要持续的抑制性信号传导（由肌醇磷酸酶SHIP-1和酪氨酸磷酸酶SHP-1介导）来维持无反应（失能）状态。本研究表明，Ars/A1 B细胞需要依赖Lyn通过限制PI3K依赖性信号通路来建立并维持B细胞无反应性。这种Lyn依赖性机制与mIgM B细胞受体（BCR）表达降低的效应相互补充，共同限制Ars/A1 B细胞中的BCR信号传导。因此，我们的研究结果提示，一部分自身反应性B细胞需要Lyn来实现失能状态，而与Lyn功能失调相关的自身免疫可能部分源于这类自身反应性B细胞无法被有效耐受化。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The Src family kinase Lyn is known to be involved in the induction and maintenance of peripheral B cell tolerance; however, mechanistic separation of tolerogenic functions from the role of Lyn in B cell and myeloid cell development and activation is challenging. Here we utilize a system in which Lyn deletion is tamoxifen inducible and B cell restricted, which allows acute elimination of Lyn in B cells only, minimizing confounding factors. This genetic tool is employed in conjunction with immunoglobulin transgenic mice in which peripheral B cells are autoreactive. DNA reactive Ars/A1 B cells require continuous inhibitory signaling, mediated by the inositol phosphatase SHIP-1 and the tyrosine phosphatase SHP-1, to maintain an unresponsive (anergic) state. Here we show that Ars/A1 B cells require Lyn to establish and maintain B cell unresponsiveness via restricting PI3K-dependent signaling pathways. This Lyn-dependent mechanism complements the impact of reduced mIgM B cell receptor (BCR) expression to restrict BCR signaling in Ars/A1 B cells. Our findings thus suggest that a subset of autoreactive B cells requires Lyn to become anergic and that the autoimmunity associated with dysregulated Lyn function may, in part, be due to an inability of these autoreactive B cells to become tolerized.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Lyn, B cell anergy, PI3K signaling, autoreactive B cells, B cell tolerance, Src family kinase, BCR signaling, autoimmunity

### 9. ❌ High-voltage and stable co-free LiNiO2 positive electrode for sulfide-based all-solid-state batteries

**作者**: Yue Wang, Dixing Ni, Huan Li, Bernt Johannessen, Chao Chao Ye, Shi-Zhang Qiao
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-08

|------|------|------|------|

| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是全固态锂离子电池的高电压钴酸锂正极材料，通过异相重构策略改善结构稳定性和界面兼容性。论文内容完全属于材料科学、电化学和电池技术领域，与医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像没有任何关联。所有关键词均与论文主题无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了高电压钴酸锂正极在全固态电池中的结构和界面降解问题，通过W和Al共掺杂的异相重构策略，实现了稳定、高容量和长循环寿命的钴酸锂正极材料。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 高电压LiNiO2正极材料的开发对于实现高能量密度全固态锂离子电池至关重要。然而，其实际应用受到结构疲劳以及与固态电解质界面不相容性的阻碍。本文提出了一种普适性的异相重构策略，以设计稳定的LiNiO2基正极材料（LiNi0.964Al0.03W0.006O2）。在该结构中，高价态W促进了与硫化物电解质具有良好界面相容性的坚固表面尖晶石相的形成，而低价态Al则通过强Al-O键抑制Li/Ni阳离子混排，从而稳定层状结构。W与Al的协同作用强化了具有增强机械与化学完整性的稳定层状-尖晶石框架，减轻了晶格应变，并抑制了有害的岩盐相和微裂纹的产生。该材料在高达4.5 V的电压下工作，在0.5 C倍率下可提供187.6 mAh g-1的高容量，并在720次循环后仍能保持122.1 mAh g-1的容量。这一异相重构策略概念在基于LiNiO2的其他体系（LiNi0.964Al0.03Mo0.006O2、LiNi0.964B0.03W0.006O2和LiNi0.964B0.03Nb0.006O2）中得到了进一步验证，证实了这是一种普适且可扩展的设计原则，可用于推进无钴、高能量、长寿命全固态锂离子电池的发展。用于全固态电池的高电压无钴LiNiO2正极材料长期受结构和界面退化问题困扰。本研究报道了一种通用的掺杂策略，可稳定正极并实现耐用的高电压全固态电池。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The development of high-voltage LiNiO2 is critical for achieving high-energy-density all-solid-state Lithium-ion batteries. However, their practical application is hindered by structural fatigue and interfacial incompatibility with solid electrolytes. Here, a universal heterophase reconstruction strategy is proposed to engineer a stable LiNiO2-based positive electrode (LiNi0.964Al0.03W0.006O2). In this architecture, high-valence W facilitates the formation of a robust surface spinel phase that exhibits good interfacial compatibility with sulfide electrolytes, while low-valence Al suppresses Li/Ni cation disorder through strong Al–O bonding, stabilizing the layered structure. The synergy of W and Al reinforces a stable layered-spinel framework with enhanced mechanical and chemical integrity, mitigates lattice strain and suppresses the detrimental rock-salt phase and microcracks. Operating up to 4.5 V, LiNi0.964Al0.03W0.006O2 delivers a high capacity of 187.6 mAh g-1 at 0.5 C and maintains 122.1 mAh g-1 even after 720 cycles. This heterophase reconstruction strategy concept is further validated in LiNiO2-based systems (LiNi0.964Al0.03Mo0.006O2, LiNi0.964B0.03W0.006O2, and LiNi0.964B0.03Nb0.006O2), confirming a general, scalable design rule for advancing cobalt-free, high-energy and long-life all-solid-state Lithium-ion batteries. High-voltage Co-free LiNiO2 positive electrode for all-solid-state batteries suffers from structural and interfacial degradation. Here, the authors report a general doping strategy that stabilizes the cathode and enables durable, high-voltage all-solid-state batteries.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: all-solid-state batteries, LiNiO2 cathode, heterophase reconstruction, high-voltage, cobalt-free, sulfide electrolytes, structural stability, long cycle life

### 10. ❌ Direct oxidative carbonylation of methane to acetic acid via high-valent iron-oxo mediated water activation

**作者**: Hailong Zhang, Richard J. Lewis, A. Iulian Dugulan, Yang Li, Shuai Wang, Zhenxing Wang, Jianrong Zeng, Nicholas F. Dummer, Yanyan Xi, Yunyun Li, Thomas E. Davies, Mingbo Wu, Graham J. Hutchings, Wenting Wu
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70339-w](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70339-w)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文标题和摘要明确表明这是一篇关于甲烷直接氧化羰基化合成乙酸（CH₃COOH）的催化化学研究，涉及Rh-O-Fe活性位点、高价金属介导的机理、水活化、自由基解耦等化学工程和催化科学概念。全文未提及任何医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习在医学成像中的应用，与所有评分关键词完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究解决了甲烷直接转化为高附加值化学品（如乙酸）的挑战，通过设计Rh-O-Fe双位点催化剂实现高价金属介导的水活化和自由基解耦机制，在连续操作中实现了高选择性（92%）和稳定的乙酸合成。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 甲烷（CH<sub>4</sub>）直接转化为高附加值化学品受限于其惰性的C-H键及低效的C-C偶联过程。本文报道了一种空间分离的Rh-O-Fe活性位点结构，该结构通过高价金属介导的自由基机制，实现了CH<sub>4</sub>与H<sub>2</sub>O活化过程的解耦，从而能够选择性合成乙酸（CH<sub>3</sub>COOH）。原位红外光谱、操作条件下穆斯堡尔谱以及准原位高场电子顺磁共振（EPR）分析表明，O<sub>2</sub>将Rh与Fe氧化至高价位态。Rh<sup>(III)</sup>活化CH<sub>4</sub>生成•CH<sub>3</sub>自由基，而Fe<sup>(IV)</sup> = O则通过截短的水煤气变换路径将H<sub>2</sub>O解离为•OH自由基。•OH迅速与CO反应形成•COOH中间体，该中间体在沸石内与•CH<sub>3</sub>发生偶联，最终生成CH<sub>3</sub>COOH。这种双位点策略规避了传统水煤气变换反应与CO插入步骤的动力学限制。该催化剂在连续运行中实现了18.2 mmol g<sub>cat</sub><sup>-1</sup> h<sup>-1</sup>的乙酸生成速率，选择性达92%，并保持100小时的稳定性。本研究确立了由高价金属位点实现的自由基解耦机制，为选择性烷烃氧化提供了一种设计原则。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Direct conversion of CH<sub>4</sub> into value-added chemicals is impeded by the inert C-H bonds and inefficient C-C coupling. We report a spatially separated Rh-O-Fe active-site architecture that decouples CH<sub>4</sub> and H<sub>2</sub>O activation through a high-valent-metal mediated radical mechanism, enabling selective CH<sub>3</sub>COOH synthesis. In-situ infrared, operando Mössbauer spectroscopy, and quasi in-situ high-field EPR reveal that O<sub>2</sub> oxidizes Rh and Fe to high valence states. Rh<sup>(III)</sup> activates CH<sub>4</sub> to •CH<sub>3</sub>, while Fe<sup>(IV)</sup> = O dissociates H<sub>2</sub>O into •OH through a truncated water-gas shift pathway. •OH rapidly reacts with CO to form •COOH intermediates, which couples with •CH<sub>3</sub> within the zeolite to yield CH<sub>3</sub>COOH. This dual-site strategy circumvents kinetic limits of conventional water-gas shift and CO insertion steps. The catalyst achieves 18.2 mmol g<sub>cat</sub><sup>-1</sup> h<sup>-1</sup> CH<sub>3</sub>COOH with 92% selectivity and 100-hour stability in continuous operation. This study establishes radical decoupling enabled by high-valent metal sites as a design principle for selective alkane oxidation.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: methane conversion, acetic acid synthesis, Rh-O-Fe catalyst, high-valent metal, water activation, radical mechanism, selective oxidation, zeolite catalyst

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过CCTG PA.7临床试验发现，在转移性胰腺导管腺癌患者中，DNA损伤修复基因（如BRCA1、POLE、ATM、FANCA）的并发突变与接受免疫治疗的患者总生存期显著改善相关（中位生存期26.2 vs. 9.7个月）。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> CCTG PA.7研究是一项随机II期临床试验，旨在比较单纯化疗与化疗联合双重免疫检查点抑制剂治疗转移性胰腺导管腺癌（metastatic pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma, mPDAC）患者的疗效。继已发表的试验主要结果之后，本次分析聚焦于长期生存数据及探索性分析。血浆测序分析发现，在173例患者中有18例（10.40%）存在DNA损伤修复基因（BRCA1、POLE、ATM和FANCA）的共突变；携带两个或以上此类基因突变的患者在接受免疫治疗时显示出总生存获益（中位总生存期26.2个月对比9.7个月；风险比0.34；95%置信区间0.16-0.68；p=0.001；交互作用p=0.003）。在免疫治疗组中，伴有DNA损伤修复基因共突变的11例患者中有7例（63.64%）观察到部分缓解。作为一项在PDAC领域的前瞻性研究，本结果识别出一种超越错配修复缺陷的潜在生物标志物，可预测免疫治疗获益，这些数据揭示了一个具有治疗可行性的mPDAC亚组。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The CCTG PA.7 study was a randomized phase II trial comparing chemotherapy with and without dual immune checkpoint inhibition in patients with metastatic pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma (mPDAC). In follow-up to the published primary results of the trial, the analysis herein focused on long-term survival and exploratory analysis.Plasma sequencing analysis identified concurrent mutations in DNA damage repair genes BRCA1, POLE, ATM and FANCA in 18/173 (10.40%) of patients, and presence of two or more mutations in these genes was associated with overall survival benefit for patients receiving immunotherapy (median overall survival 26.2 vs. 9.7 months; hazard ratio, 0.34; 95% CI, 0.16-0.68; p = 0.001; interaction p = 0.003). Partial response was observed in 7/11 (63.64%) patients with concurrent DNA damage repair gene mutations in the immunotherapy arm. As a prospective study in PDAC identifying a potential biomarker beyond mismatch repair deficiency for benefit from immunotherapy, these data highlight an actionable subgroup of mPDAC.

</details>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究报道了一种三核氰桥FeCo化合物通过电子转移耦合自旋跃迁机制实现光热诱导铁电相变，并展示了通过冷却速率变化和溶剂分子吸附/脱附可逆调控铁电性的多态开关能力。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 基于极性分子的多态转换磁性材料因其在下一代存储设备、传感器及能量转换领域的应用潜力而备受关注。其中，表现出电子转移耦合自旋跃迁（ETCST）行为的普鲁士蓝类似物因其独特的转换特性尤为突出。本研究报道了一种三核氰基桥联的FeCo化合物（1），该化合物通过ETCST机制表现出光诱导与热诱导的铁电相变。值得注意的是，该FeCo配合物还展现出淬灭效应，即非极性态在低温下被捕获为亚稳态，从而允许通过改变冷却速率来控制极化。此外，研究观察到通过溶剂分子的脱附与吸收可实现可逆的单晶到单晶转变。移除EtOH后的FeCo化合物（1'）失去了铁电性，这表明铁电相变可通过客体分子的动态脱附/吸附进行调控。这些发现推进了具有多态转换功能的新型铁电材料的设计，为未来在非接触式存储设备等领域的应用提供了潜力。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Polar molecule-based magnetic materials capable of multistate switching have garnered significant interest for their potential applications in next-generation memory devices, sensors, and energy conversion. Among such materials, Prussian blue analogs that exhibit electron transfer-coupled spin transition (ETCST) behavior stand out due to their unique switching properties. In this study, we report a trinuclear cyanide-bridged FeCo compound (1) that exhibits photo- and thermo-induced ferroelectric phase transition via ETCST mechanism. Notably, this FeCo complex also demonstrates a quenching effect, whereby a non-polar state is trapped as a metastable state at low temperature, allowing the polarization control via the cooling rate variations. In addition, reversible single-crystal-to-single-crystal transformation via the desorption and absorption of solvent molecules are observed. The EtOH-removed FeCo compound (1') loses its ferroelectricity, revealing that the ferroelectric phase transition can be modulated by dynamic desorption/adsorption of the guest molecule. These findings advance the design of functional ferroelectric materials with multistate switching capabilities, offering potential for future applications in contactless memory devices and beyond.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: ferroelectric switching, Prussian blue analogue, FeCo complex, electron transfer-coupled spin transition, photo-thermo-induced phase transition, single-crystal transformation, multistate switching, molecular magnetic materials

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文开发了一种基于资产级数据的自下而上方法，用于评估全球钢铁企业的碳排放轨迹与净零目标的（不）对齐情况，发现企业2030年的预计排放量超过国际能源署净零排放情景的10%-22%，且超过企业自身设定的减排目标。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们开发了一种自下而上的方法，用于评估企业相对于净零排放情景的（偏离）一致性。该方法基于单个生产单元的资产层面数据，能够详细估算企业的排放轨迹。我们将此方法应用于全球钢铁行业，发现根据对钢铁生产排放因子未来演变的不同假设，企业2030年的预计排放量将超出国际能源署（IEA）净零排放情景所隐含水平的10%至22%。此外，即使在电力供应脱碳速度遵循净零情景的乐观假设下，2030年的预计排放量仍将超过企业集体声明的减排目标，而这一差距主要由大型钢铁企业驱动。我们的研究结果表明，自下而上的资产层面方法能够切实检验企业对国家脱碳计划的贡献度。这进而对制定更具针对性的工业脱碳政策及监管信息披露至关重要。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We develop a bottom-up methodology to estimate companies' (mis)alignment to net-zero scenarios. The approach relies on asset-level data for individual production units, enabling a detailed estimation of corporate emissions trajectories. We apply the methodology to the steel sector globally and find that companies' projected emissions for 2030 exceed those implied by the International Energy Agency's (IEA) Net Zero Emissions (NZE) scenario by between 10% and 22%, depending on the assumptions about the future evolution of emission factors of steel production. Further, we find that projected emissions for 2030 exceed companies' aggregate stated targets, even under the optimistic assumption of electricity supply decarbonization rate following the net-zero scenario, with the gap primarily driven by the largest steel companies. Our results show that a bottom-up asset-level approach allows for a reality check of companies' contributions to national decarbonization plans. This, in turn, is crucial to inform more targeted industrial policies for decarbonization, and regulatory disclosure.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: net-zero alignment, asset-level data, corporate emissions, steel sector, bottom-up methodology, decarbonization, emissions trajectories, IEA NZE scenario

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    A machine-learning-guided workflow along with an algorithm named parallelized hybrid-space Bayesian optimization (PHBO) to accelerate the discovery of nanocarriers for specific enzymes and reactions and demonstrates that data-efficient optimization can substantially accelerate the discovery of enzyme nanohybrids with high catalytic activity across diverse enzymatic systems.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究开发了一种基于并行化混合空间贝叶斯优化的机器学习工作流，用于高效发现具有高催化活性的酶纳米杂化物，在有限实验中实现了对多种酶的高活性恢复。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 人工智能（AI）已显著推动蛋白质工程的发展，能够为多样化应用实现快速的酶定向进化。然而，生物大分子的脆弱性要求对酶进行固定化，以在苛刻的工业条件下保持催化活性，但这通常限制了底物扩散并降低了酶活性。这一挑战需要通过大量试错实验来优化不同酶的高活性固定化载体。本文展示了一种机器学习引导的工作流程，以及一种名为并行化混合空间贝叶斯优化（parallelized hybrid-space Bayesian optimization, PHBO）的算法，以加速发现适用于特定酶和反应的纳米载体。该工作流程利用先验知识、机器学习和迭代反馈，在有限次数的实验中探索了超过10<sup>7</sup>次实验的反应空间，并分别实现了葡萄糖氧化酶、过氧化氢酶和南极假丝酵母脂肪酶B（Candida Antarctica lipase B）100%、90%和79%的活性恢复。这些结果表明，数据高效优化能够大幅加速发现具有高催化活性的酶纳米杂化材料，并适用于多种酶系统。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Artificial intelligence (AI) has significantly advanced protein engineering, enabling rapid enzyme evolution for diverse applications. However, the fragile nature of biomacromolecules requires enzyme immobilization to preserve catalytic activity under harsh industrial conditions, which often restricts substrate diffusion and reduces enzymatic activity. This challenge demands extensive trial-and-error experiments to optimize immobilized carriers with high activity for different enzymes. Here we show a machine-learning-guided workflow along with an algorithm named parallelized hybrid-space Bayesian optimization (PHBO) to accelerate the discovery of nanocarriers for specific enzymes and reactions. Leveraging prior knowledge, machine learning and iterative feedback, within limited number of experiments, this workflow explores the reaction space of over 10<sup>7</sup> experiments and achieves activity recovery of 100%, 90%, and 79% for glucose oxidase, catalase, and Candida Antarctica lipase B, respectively. These results demonstrate that data-efficient optimization can substantially accelerate the discovery of enzyme nanohybrids with high catalytic activity across diverse enzymatic systems.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: enzyme nanohybrids, Bayesian optimization, machine learning, protein engineering, enzyme immobilization, catalytic activity, parallelized optimization, nanocarriers

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    It is proposed that early-stage AD-related synaptic pathophysiology is focused at population-coupled synapses, with molecular measures implicating abnormal synaptic processing as an early-stage feature in parvalbumin-positive interneurons.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过体内成像和分子分析发现，在阿尔茨海默病早期淀粉样蛋白病理中，突触功能障碍并非全局性，而是特异性地发生在与群体活动耦合的GABA能突触上，并涉及小清蛋白阳性中间神经元的基因表达改变。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 阿尔茨海默病（AD）中的突触功能障碍可能导致突触丧失与认知损伤。AD相关的突触病理生理变化是全局性发生，还是局限于特定突触，目前尚不明确。本研究在App<sup>NL-G-F</sup>小鼠早期淀粉样蛋白病变阶段，对AD相关的突触功能障碍进行了活体研究。我们发现，在c-Fos阳性兴奋性神经元处，突触前GABA能蛋白减少，而兴奋性与抑制性神经元集群的钙介导活动增强。活体突触结构与功能成像显示，GABA能轴突终扣的密度及其钙介导活动降低。突触活动的减弱并非全局性，而是集中于淀粉样微环境中与群体活动紧密耦合的GABA能终扣。这种群体耦合突触活动的选择性减弱同样出现在兴奋性树突棘中。空间转录组学分析发现，在疾病早期，小清蛋白（parvalbumin）阳性抑制性神经元已出现差异基因表达，这些基因与GABA能突触传递下调相关。我们认为，早期AD相关的突触病理生理变化集中于群体耦合突触，其分子指标提示突触处理异常是小清蛋白阳性中间神经元在疾病早期的特征性表现。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Synaptic dysfunction in Alzheimer's disease (AD) may drive synapse loss and cognitive impairment. Whether AD-related synaptic pathophysiology occurs globally, or in specific synapses, is unclear. We investigate in vivo AD-related synaptic dysfunction during early-stage amyloidosis in App<sup>NL-G-F</sup> mice. We find reduced presynaptic GABAergic proteins at c-Fos-positive excitatory neurons and increased calcium-mediated activity at excitatory and inhibitory neuronal assemblies. In vivo synaptic structure/function imaging finds reduced density and calcium-mediated activity of GABAergic axonal boutons. Rather than occurring globally, reduced synaptic activity is focused at GABAergic boutons strongly coupled to population activity in the amyloid microenvironment. The selective weakening of population-coupled synaptic activity also occurs in excitatory dendritic spines. Spatial transcriptomics finds parvalbumin-positive inhibitory neurons show differential gene expression associated with downregulated GABAergic synaptic transmission at early stages. We propose that early-stage AD-related synaptic pathophysiology is focused at population-coupled synapses, with molecular measures implicating abnormal synaptic processing as an early-stage feature in parvalbumin-positive interneurons.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Alzheimer's disease, synaptic dysfunction, amyloid-beta pathology, in vivo imaging, GABAergic synapses, population-coupled activity, parvalbumin interneurons, spatial transcriptomics

### 16. ❌ Diel and eddy driven changes in microbial gene expression and biogeochemistry in the oceanic chlorophyll maximum

**作者**: Logan M. Peoples, John M. Eppley, Benedetto Barone, Brett W. Hobson, David M. Karl, Brian Kieft, Roman Marin, Christina M. Preston, Anna E. Romano, John Ryan, Christopher A. Scholin, Samuel T. Wilson, Yanwu Zhang, Matthew J. Church, Edward F. DeLong
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70228-2](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70228-2)

| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究海洋微生物在叶绿素最大层中对昼夜变化和中尺度涡旋扰动的响应，涉及微生物转录组学、生物地球化学和物理海洋学，完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像等医疗领域内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过自主水下航行器和船基测量，揭示了海洋叶绿素最大层中微生物群落如何快速响应昼夜周期变化和中尺度涡旋扰动，导致浮游植物代谢和氨氧化古菌转录活动的动态变化。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 海洋微生物能够快速响应环境变化。确定物理与生物过程如何调控微生物的分布、丰度及代谢动态是一项挑战。本研究利用具备拉格朗日特征追踪与原位采样能力的自主水下航行器，结合船基观测，分析了中尺度气旋式涡旋中深层叶绿素最大值（Deep Chlorophyll Maximum, DCM）内微生物转录活动与生物地球化学过程在日际至周尺度上的变化。近20%的总转录表达显示出昼夜周期性，凸显了在DCM弱光环境下昼夜循环对浮游植物代谢的重要性。涡旋引起的等密度面抬升增加了营养盐浓度，并导致DCM位置上移，从而驱动微微型真核细胞丰度增加，并提升了利用硝酸盐的光合自养生物的转录活性。随着涡旋减弱，DCM深度加深，转录活动转向化能自养氨氧化古菌。观测到的时间动态表明，浮游生物群落如何快速响应昼夜变化与随机的中尺度扰动。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Oceanic microorganisms can rapidly respond to environmental variability. Determining how physical and biological processes control microbial distributions, abundances, and metabolic dynamics is challenging. Here, we used autonomous underwater vehicles capable of Lagrangian feature tracking and in situ sampling, in combination with ship-based measurements, to examine diel to weekly scale changes in microbial transcription and biogeochemistry in the deep chlorophyll maximum (DCM) of a mesoscale cyclonic eddy. Nearly 20% of total transcript expression showed diel periodicity, highlighting the importance of the diurnal cycle on phytoplankton metabolism in the dim waters of the DCM. Eddy-induced isopycnal uplift increased nutrient concentrations and caused upward displacement of the DCM, driving increased picoeukaryotic cell abundances and transcriptional activity of nitrate-incorporating photoautotrophs. As the eddy weakened, the DCM deepened and transcriptional activity shifted towards chemolithoautotrophic ammonia-oxidizing archaea. The temporal dynamics observed demonstrate how plankton communities rapidly respond to both diel variation and stochastic mesoscale disturbances.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: microbial gene expression, biogeochemistry, oceanic chlorophyll maximum, diel periodicity, mesoscale eddy, phytoplankton metabolism, autonomous underwater vehicles, transcriptional activity

### 17. ❌ Modeling roles and trade-offs in multiplex networks

**作者**: Nikolaos Nakis, Sune Lehmann, Nicholas A. Christakis, Morten Mørup
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**arXiv链接**: [https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.05488](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.05488)
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-68896-1](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-68896-1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是多路复用网络（multiplex networks）中的角色建模和权衡分析，应用于社会、健康和经济网络层，属于网络科学和社会科学领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像技术，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    This work introduces the Multiplex Latent Trade-off Model, MLT, a framework for identifying roles in multiplex networks that incorporates independence, dependence, and interdependence, and identifies core principles of social exchange that reveal multi-scale communities.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了多路复用潜在权衡模型（MLT）来识别多路网络中的角色，通过分析社会、健康和经济网络层揭示了社会交换的核心原则和多尺度社区结构。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 多重社会网络捕捉了同一人群间的多种关系类型。其结构反映了交换如何产生于与独立性相关的个体属性、与他人地位或资源相关的依赖性，以及相互关联的互依性。理解这些系统具有挑战性，因为网络各层可能扮演着不同却互补的角色。我们提出了多重潜在权衡模型（Multiplex Latent Trade-off Model, MLT），这是一个用于识别多重网络中角色的框架，该框架整合了独立性、依赖性与互依性。MLT将角色表征为权衡过程，要求每个节点在各层间分配源角色与目标角色，同时在层级结构内分配社区成员身份。将MLT应用于176个多重网络（包括来自洪都拉斯西部村庄的社会、健康与经济层面数据），我们识别出社会交换的核心原则并揭示了多尺度社区结构。链接预测分析表明，对互依性的建模最能提升社会关系的预测准确性，而健康与经济关系则更多地受个体地位与行为的影响。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Multiplex social networks capture multiple types of relations among the same people. Their structure reflects how exchanges arise from individual attributes related to independence, the status or resources of others related to dependence, and mutual influence related to interdependence. Understanding these systems is challenging because layers can play distinct yet complementary roles. We introduce the Multiplex Latent Trade-off Model, MLT, a framework for identifying roles in multiplex networks that incorporates independence, dependence, and interdependence. MLT represents roles as trade-offs, requiring each node to distribute source and target roles across layers while allocating community memberships within hierarchical structures. Applying MLT to 176 multiplex networks, including social, health, and economic layers from villages in western Honduras, we identify core principles of social exchange and reveal multi-scale communities. Link-prediction analyses show that modeling interdependence most improves predictions for social ties, whereas health and economic ties are shaped more strongly by individual status and behavior.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: multiplex networks, role modeling, trade-offs, social exchange, link prediction, community detection, interdependence, hierarchical structures

---

### 18. ❌ High-efficiency electrochemical air capture enabled by thiadiazole redox carrier with tunable gas-selective channels

**作者**: Jing Hou, Yingying Cheng, Tao Yan, Zhikun Liu, Peng Kang
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70444-w](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70444-w)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是电化学直接空气CO₂捕获技术，涉及电化学、材料科学、气体分离和分子动力学模拟，与医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像完全无关。论文内容聚焦于CO₂捕获材料、气体选择性通道和电化学性能，没有任何医学图像或医学成像相关内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了使用噻二唑氧化还原载体和可调气体选择性通道的高效电化学空气CO₂捕获技术，通过BPT-GPL复合电极系统实现了高CO₂捕获容量和优异的O₂耐受性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 利用氧化还原载体的电化学直接空气CO<sub>2</sub>捕集（eDAC）技术可实现可持续脱碳，但存在因氧诱导副反应（如氧还原和载体氧化）导致的效率损失。本研究通过将2,5-双(4-吡啶基)-1,3,4-噻二唑（BPT）与富含醚氧基（-O-）的气体渗透层（GPL）结合，构建了一种复合电极BPT-GPL，其形成了可调控的气体传输通道，在促进CO<sub>2</sub>扩散的同时限制O<sub>2</sub>渗透。在大气条件（约400 ppm CO<sub>2</sub>，21% O<sub>2</sub>）下，BPT-GPL体系在48次循环中表现出3.3 ± 0.2 mmol g<sup>-1</sup><sub>BPT</sub>的高eDAC容量，且氧化还原载体降解可忽略不计。基于噻二唑环的BPT分子增加了电子离域性，表现出适中的CO<sub>2</sub>结合强度与高耐氧性。此外，GPL在允许CO<sub>2</sub>扩散的同时抑制O<sub>2</sub>渗透，形成了低氧微环境，从而抑制副反应并维持循环稳定性。分子动力学（MD）模拟表明，醚氧基对CO<sub>2</sub>的亲和力强于O<sub>2</sub>，这提高了CO<sub>2</sub>在GPL内的溶解度，导致CO<sub>2</sub>优先渗透。BPT-GPL体系有利于CO<sub>2</sub>传输并限制O<sub>2</sub>输送，实现了高效eDAC，并凸显了其实际应用的潜力。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Electrochemical direct air CO<sub>2</sub> capture (eDAC) using redox carriers enables sustainable decarbonization but suffers efficiency losses from O<sub>2</sub>-induced side reactions such as oxygen reduction and carrier oxidation. We introduce a composite electrode BPT-GPL by integrating 2,5-bis(4-pyridyl)-1,3,4-thiadiazole (BPT) with ether oxygen (-O-) enriched gas permeation layer (GPL), forming a tunable gas transport channel that facilitates CO<sub>2</sub> diffusion while limiting O<sub>2</sub> penetration. Under atmospheric conditions (~400 ppm CO<sub>2</sub>, 21% O<sub>2</sub>), the BPT - GPL system demonstrates high eDAC capacity of 3.3 ± 0.2 mmol g<sup>-1</sup><sub>BPT</sub> across 48 cycles with negligible redox carrier degradation. The thiadiazole ring-based BPT molecules increase electron delocalization, exhibiting moderate CO<sub>2</sub> binding strength and high O<sub>2</sub> tolerance. Moreover, GPL allows CO<sub>2</sub> diffusion and suppresses O<sub>2</sub> permeation creating low-O<sub>2</sub> microenvironment that inhibits side reactions and maintains cycling stability. Molecular dynamics (MD) simulations suggest that ether oxygen's stronger affinity for CO<sub>2</sub> than O<sub>2</sub> increases CO<sub>2</sub> solubility within GPL, resulting in preferential CO<sub>2</sub> permeation. The BPT - GPL system favors CO<sub>2</sub> delivery and restricts O<sub>2</sub> transport, enabling efficient eDAC and highlighting the potential for practical implementation.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: electrochemical CO₂ capture, redox carrier, thiadiazole, gas-selective channels, oxygen tolerance, molecular dynamics simulation, BPT-GPL composite, direct air capture

**作者**: Yan Ping, Zhewen Qin, Xingxiao Huang, Qiuli Sun, Tao Yao, Siqi Li, Xin Tian, Xintong Xia, Bowen Diao, Lin Zhao, Xinyuan Zhang, Danni Wei, Long Wang, Ying Wu, Ying Wu, Jinyu Huang, Bo Shan
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    It is demonstrated that perivascular MSCs enhance arterial immune response by facilitating recruitment of ST2-expressing reparative macrophages in male mice, and an IL33-ST2-OPN axis that mediates functional crosstalk between perivascular MSCs and reparative macrophages is defined, orchestrating immune-mediated reparative responses.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究揭示了血管周围间充质干细胞通过IL33-ST2-OPN轴促进ST2+修复性巨噬细胞招募和表型转换，从而驱动血管平滑肌细胞增殖和新内膜增生，为预防血管再狭窄提供了潜在治疗靶点。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 组织驻留间充质基质细胞（MSC）在损伤部位指导免疫细胞活化，这是组织修复的关键环节。然而，驱动损伤响应性免疫-基质细胞相互作用的完整免疫调节机制尚未被充分探索。本研究利用血管内损伤小鼠模型，证明在雄性小鼠中，血管周围MSC通过促进表达ST2的修复性巨噬细胞募集，从而增强动脉免疫反应。时间分辨单细胞测序揭示了MSC介导的巨噬细胞表型转换，这对血管再生至关重要。机制上，损伤激活了MSC中NFκB依赖的IL-33产生，其作为旁分泌信号驱动ST2+巨噬细胞产生骨桥蛋白（Osteopontin, OPN/SPP1），并刺激血管平滑肌细胞（VSMC）增殖和新内膜形成。局部水凝胶介导的靶向Il33或Spp1的siRNA递送有效减轻了损伤诱导的新内膜增生，这提示了一种预防再狭窄及其他血管疾病的潜在治疗策略。我们的研究结果界定了一条IL33-ST2-OPN轴，该轴介导了血管周围MSC与修复性巨噬细胞之间的功能性交互对话，从而协调免疫介导的修复反应。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Tissue-resident mesenchymal stromal cells (MSC) instruct immune cell activation at injury sites, a key event in tissue repair. However, the full array of immunomodulatory mechanisms driving injury-responsive immune-stromal cell interactions is underexplored. Here, using an endovascular injury mouse model, we demonstrate that perivascular MSCs enhance arterial immune response by facilitating recruitment of ST2-expressing reparative macrophages in male mice. Time-resolved single-cell sequencing reveals an MSC-mediated, macrophage phenotypic switch, essential for vascular regeneration. Mechanistically, injury activates NFκB-dependent IL-33 production in MSCs, which acts as a paracrine signal that drives Osteopontin (OPN/SPP1) production in ST2+ macrophages and stimulates vascular smooth muscle cell (VSMC) proliferation and neointima formation. Local hydrogel-mediated delivery of siRNAs targeting Il33 or Spp1 effectively alleviates injury-induced neointimal hyperplasia, suggesting a potential therapeutic strategy to prevent restenosis and other vascular diseases. Our findings define an IL33-ST2-OPN axis that mediates functional crosstalk between perivascular MSCs and reparative macrophages, orchestrating immune-mediated reparative responses.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: perivascular mesenchymal cells, ST2+ reparative macrophages, neointimal hyperplasia, IL33-ST2-OPN axis, vascular injury, single-cell sequencing, hydrogel-mediated siRNA delivery, vascular regeneration

    该研究提出了一个多目标土地利用规划框架，以平衡生物多样性保护与农业和可再生能源发展需求，全球应用表明无规划的发展将威胁近100万平方公里高优先级保护区，而多部门协调规划可减少冲突和碳损失。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 日益增长的粮食需求与减少排放的气候承诺，将推动农业和可再生能源领域的土地开发。与此同时，为生物多样性及自然对人类的贡献（Nature's contributions to people, NCP）保护土地，对于实现国际气候、可持续发展及生物多样性目标至关重要。要达成这些相互关联的目标，需要跨部门的高效土地配置。本文提出一个灵活的多目标框架，用于在气候变化背景下战略性分配土地，以减轻对生物多样性和NCP的威胁，同时支持发展需求。通过国家层面目标在全球尺度应用该框架表明，若未来发展规划不考虑自然因素，土地需求可能影响近100万平方公里的高优先级保护区。多部门协同规划能够缓解潜在冲突，减少碳损失和物种暴露风险。我们的研究结果强调，必须保护对自然至关重要的区域，降低粮食和能源的土地需求，并有意识地协调跨部门土地利用。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Growing demand for food coupled with climate commitments to reduce emissions will result in more land development for agriculture and renewable energy. Simultaneously, conserving land for biodiversity and nature's contributions to people (NCP) is imperative for achieving international climate, sustainable development, and biodiversity goals. Meeting these interconnected objectives requires efficient land allocation across sectors. Here, we present a flexible, multiple-objective framework for strategically allocating land to mitigate threats to biodiversity and NCP under climate change while supporting development. Application of this framework at a global scale through country-level targets shows that if future development is planned without consideration of nature, demands for land could impact nearly 1 million km<sup>2</sup> of high-priority conservation areas. Multi-sector planning can mitigate potential conflict, reducing carbon loss and species exposure. Our findings underscore the need to conserve critical areas for nature, reduce land demand for food and energy, and intentionally coordinate land use across sectors.

</details>

    该研究利用人类大脑类器官建立了西尼罗河病毒脑炎模型，发现类器官能模拟急性和长期感染，并揭示了病毒感染动力学和免疫反应特征。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 西尼罗河病毒（WNV）作为一种全球关注的新发虫媒病毒，可导致人类神经侵袭性疾病。目前，针对人类WNV脑炎尚无保护性疫苗或特异性治疗方法。该病毒会诱导神经元细胞死亡，而星形胶质细胞和小胶质细胞被认为参与了WNV的病理过程。因此，理解它们的作用对于未来的治疗策略至关重要。本研究利用男性诱导多能干细胞（iPSCs）生成的人脑类器官，建立了一个WNV脑炎模型。感染呈现出异质性的动力学特征：早期强烈的病毒复制可能导致病毒清除，而晚期的感染高峰则与更长期的感染相关。病毒灶出现在富含神经元和星形胶质细胞的皮质样区域，但该区域缺乏小胶质细胞。促炎细胞因子（IL-6、TNF-α、IL-18）、趋化因子（CXCL10、CCL17、CX3CL1、CCL2）和生物标志物（IL-1RA、sTREM-1、sRAGE、BDNF）的释放量均有所增加。综上所述，人脑类器官是研究急性和长期WNV感染的合适模型，具有重要价值。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> West Nile virus (WNV), an arbovirus of emerging global interest, can cause neuroinvasive disease in humans. Currently, no protective vaccine or specific treatment is available for human WNV encephalitis. The virus induces neuronal cell death, while astrocytes and microglia cells are suspected to contribute to WNV pathology. Hence, understanding their role is crucial for future treatment approaches. In this study, we establish a WNV encephalitis model using human cerebral organoids, generated with male iPSCs. Infection results in heterogeneous kinetics with an early strong replication potentially leading to viral clearance, while a late peak was associated with more long-term infection. Viral foci are seen in cortical-like areas, rich in neurons and astrocytes, however void of microglia. Pro-inflammatory cytokines (IL-6, TNF-α, IL-18), chemokines (CXCL10, CCL17, CX3CL1, CCL2) and biomarkers (IL-1RA, sTREM-1, sRAGE, BDNF) are increasingly released. Conclusively, human cerebral organoids make suitable WNV encephalitis models with valuable properties to study acute and long-term infection.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: West Nile virus, encephalitis, human cerebral organoids, neuroinvasive disease, viral infection kinetics, pro-inflammatory cytokines, innate immunocompetency, iPSCs

### 22. ❌ Accurate atomic resolution XFEL structures of a metalloenzyme reveal key insights into its catalytic mechanism*

**作者**: Samuel L. Rose, Daniel P. Donnelly, Felix F. Ferroni, Hiroshi Sugimoto, Keitaro Yamashita, Kunio Hirata, Hideo Ago, Go Ueno, Hironori Murakami, Robert R. Eady, Takehiko Tosha, Mari Yamamoto, S. Samar Hasnain
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70261-1](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70261-1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究铜亚硝酸盐还原酶（CuNiRs）的原子分辨率结构，使用X射线自由电子激光（XFEL）技术解析其氧化、还原和底物结合状态下的结构，以揭示其催化机制。该研究属于结构生物学、生物化学和酶学领域，与医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像完全无关。论文未涉及任何医学图像处理、诊断或分析技术。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究利用XFEL技术解析了铜亚硝酸盐还原酶在多种状态下的原子分辨率结构，揭示了其催化中心的结构变化和反应机制。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 金属蛋白构成了蛋白质王国的主要组成部分，常利用过渡金属的氧化还原化学驱动涉及质子与电子转移的关键生物过程。铜是最广泛使用的过渡金属之一，其氧化还原特性被应用于电子传递和化学底物的催化。铜亚硝酸还原酶（CuNiRs）利用两种类型的铜中心，已成为研究氧化还原酶反应机制（包括质子耦合电子转移和底物门控）背后复杂生物过程的模型体系。我们利用SACLA X射线自由电子激光（XFEL）提供的较高X射线能量（13 keV）及SHELXL精修方法，获得了来自三种生物的CuNiR在氧化态（低pH与高pH）、还原态及底物结合态下约1 Å精度的原子分辨率结构。通过观察发现，在所有情况下氧化态催化型二价铜中心（T2Cu<sup>2+</sup>）均呈现五配位构型，这一结果揭示了一致的结构图景。同时，我们还捕获了具有单一溶剂配体的四配位还原态一价铜位点（T2Cu<sup>+</sup>），为以有序路径为主导的随机序贯反应机制提供了结构支持。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Metalloproteins represent a major fraction of the protein kingdom and often exploit the redox chemistry of transition metals to drive key biological events involving proton and electron transfer. Copper is one of the most widely used transition metals whose redox properties are utilised in both electron transfer and catalysis of chemical substrates. Copper nitrite reductases (CuNiRs) utilise two types of copper centres and have become a model system for studying complex biological events that underpin the reaction mechanisms of redox enzymes, including proton-coupled electron transfer and substrate gating. We utilised the higher X-ray energy (13 keV) available at the SACLA X-ray Free Electron Laser (XFEL) and SHELXL refinement to obtain accurate atomic resolution structures of CuNiRs at ~1 Å from three organisms - in the oxidised (low and high pH), reduced and substrate-bound states. A consistent picture now emerges with the observation of a pentacoordinated oxidised catalytic type-2 Cu (T2Cu<sup>2+</sup>) centre in all cases. A tetracoordinated reduced T2Cu<sup>+</sup> site with a single solvent ligand has also been captured, giving structural support to the random-sequential scheme with ordered pathway being dominant.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: copper nitrite reductase, XFEL, atomic resolution, catalytic mechanism, redox enzyme, CuNiR, SHELXL refinement, type-2 copper

### 23. ❌ Dynamic bond-driven encapsulation of enzymes in metal–organic frameworks beyond pore size constraints

**作者**: Youcong Li, Meng Qiao, Lei Gao, Yuxiu Zhong, Y. X. Yang, Jie Zheng, Jing Lin Zuo, Xing Zhang, Shuai Yuan
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究解决了金属有机框架（MOF）因孔径限制无法封装大尺寸酶的问题，通过动态金属-吡啶键作为分子门控，实现了超越孔径限制的酶封装，提高了酶的稳定性和可重用性，并成功应用于多酶系统的共固定化。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 将酶固定于金属有机框架（MOF）中是提升其稳定性和可重复使用性的有效策略，但大多数MOF的孔径较小，限制了众多工业相关酶的包载。本文提出一种动态键介导的方法，能够突破孔径限制实现酶封装。我们通过将稳定的三价金属-羧酸盐簇与动态的二价金属-吡啶单元相结合，构建了一系列介孔MOF。通过系统改变金属组合与连接体长度，可精确调控框架稳定性与动态性，实现金属-吡啶键的可逆解离与重组。这些动态键充当分子门控，允许大于固有孔径的酶渗入框架，同时保持结构完整性。该策略成功应用于多种酶的封装，在维持高酶活性的同时显著提升了操作稳定性。此外，该方法支持多酶系统（如NahK与GlmU）的共固定化，可用于高效级联合成高价值糖基化供体。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Immobilizing enzymes in a metal-organic framework (MOF) is an effective approach to improve their stability and reusability, but the small pore sizes of most MOFs exclude many industrially relevant enzymes. Here, we present a dynamic bond-mediated approach that enables enzyme encapsulation beyond pore size constraints. We constructed a series of mesoporous MOFs by integrating robust trivalent metal-carboxylate clusters with dynamic divalent metal-pyridyl units. Systematic variation of metal combinations and linker lengths precisely tunes the framework stability and dynamics, enabling reversible dissociation and reformation of metal-pyridyl bonds. These dynamic bonds function as molecular gates, permitting enzymes larger than the intrinsic pores to infiltrate while preserving framework integrity. The strategy was applied to encapsulate diverse enzymes, preserving high enzymatic activity and enhancing operational stability. Furthermore, it supports the co-immobilization of multi-enzyme systems, such as NahK and GlmU, for efficient cascade synthesis of high-value glycosylated donors.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: enzyme encapsulation, metal-organic frameworks, dynamic bonds, pore size constraints, molecular gates, multi-enzyme systems, cascade synthesis

### 24. ❌ Conformal and adhesive gel for stable electrophysiology on hairy animals without shaving

**作者**: Leyi Yang, Miaoxi Chen, Jiongyang Qi, Wenya Hu, Shiyu Wang, Yujie Wu, Chen Hu, Dajun Xing, Nan Liu
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications

| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是用于有毛动物和人类头皮的非侵入性电神经信号采集的凝胶电极接口技术，属于生物医学工程、神经科学和材料科学领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像，没有使用任何图像数据、成像技术或图像分析方法。所有关键词与论文主题完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    A hair-adaptable and adhesion-tunable (HAAT) scalp-electrode interface that can accurately acquire electroneurographic signals from hairy skins of animal and human is reported and the accurate event-related potential monitored during monkey vision-attention tasks facilitates the study of monkey brain activity.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文开发了一种可穿透毛发、粘附可调的凝胶电极接口，实现了从有毛动物和人类头皮稳定、精确地采集电神经信号，为动物认知的非侵入性研究提供了新平台。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 非侵入式采集微弱神经电信号对认知神经科学至关重要。然而动物头皮常被浓密毛发覆盖，这对头皮-电极界面的精确电生理信号采集构成了显著障碍。尽管临床实践中常采用头皮脱毛方法，但这会对测试对象造成损害，且在众多非临床场景中难以实施。本文报道了一种可适应毛发且粘附力可调（HAAT）的头皮-电极界面，该界面能够从动物和人类的多毛皮肤准确采集神经电信号。通过在共聚物聚（硫辛酸钠-甲基丙烯酰氧乙基磺基甜菜碱）中协同整合动态共价键与离子传导通道，我们实现了HAAT界面的关键功能：穿透浓密毛发层、实现强保形皮肤-电极粘附、按需无痛分离以及灵敏的神经电耦合。我们成功从人类、猴子和小鼠等不同毛发密度的头皮上实现了稳定精确的神经电信号采集。在猴子视觉注意任务期间监测到的精确事件相关电位，为研究猴子大脑活动提供了便利。这些结果表明HAAT界面是开展动物认知非侵入式研究的卓越平台。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Non-invasive collection of weak electroneurographic signals is crucial for cognitive neuroscience. However, animal scalps are often covered by dense hair, which presents a substantial barrier in the scalp-electrode interface for accurate electrophysiological acquisition. Although scalp hair removal is common practice in clinical settings, it has detrimental effects on the test subjects and is infeasible in many non-clinical scenarios. Here we report a hair-adaptable and adhesion-tunable (HAAT) scalp-electrode interface that can accurately acquire electroneurographic signals from hairy skins of animal and human. By synthetically integrating dynamic covalent bonds and ionic conduction channels in the copolymer poly(sodium thioctate-co-sulfobetaine methacrylate), we implement the key functionalities of the HAAT interface including penetration of dense hair layers, strong conformal skin-electrode adhesion, on-demand painless detachment, and sensitive neuroelectric coupling. We achieve stable and precise electroneurographic signals acquisition from human, monkey and mouse's scalps with various hair densities. The accurate event-related potential monitored during monkey vision-attention tasks facilitates the study of monkey brain activity. These results demonstrate the HAAT interface as an outstanding platform for conducting non-invasive research on animal cognition.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: electroneurographic signals, hairy skin, scalp-electrode interface, non-invasive, conformal adhesion, dynamic covalent bonds, ionic conduction, animal cognition

### 25. ❌ A scalable and quantum-accurate foundation model for biomolecular force fields via linearly tensorized quadrangle attention

**作者**: Qi Su, Kai Zhu, Qiaolin Gou, Jintu Zhang, Renling Hu, Y Li, Yongze Wang, Haitao Zhang, Ziyi You, Linlong Jiang, Yu Kang, Jike Wang, Chang-Yu Hsieh, Tingjun Hou
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
