**评分理由**: 论文研究的是生物分子力场和分子模拟，使用深度学习模型（LiTEN）提高计算精度和效率，应用于药物发现和疾病机制研究。虽然涉及医学应用背景（药物发现），但核心内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或相关深度学习技术。所有关键词与论文主题无直接关联。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    LiTEN achieves state-of-the-art accuracy on standard benchmarks, consistently outperforming leading approaches in both precision and speed, and enables comprehensive modeling tasks, ranging from geometry optimization to free energy surface construction, with high computational efficiency for large biomolecules.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了生物分子模拟中量子精度与计算可扩展性的平衡问题，通过提出LiTEN神经网络模型实现了高精度、高效率的分子力场计算。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 精确的原子尺度生物分子模拟对于理解疾病机制和药物发现至关重要，然而现有方法难以在量子力学精度与计算可扩展性之间取得平衡。经典力场往往缺乏精确性，而量子方法对于复杂生物系统的计算成本则高不可攀。本文展示了一种可扩展的等变神经网络LiTEN，它通过线性张量化的四边形注意力机制，以线性复杂度高效建模复杂的三体与四体相互作用，从而解决了这一难题。我们推出了LiTEN-FF，这是一个基于大规模数据集预训练的基础模型，旨在确保跨多样分子空间的广泛化学泛化能力。我们证明，LiTEN在标准基准测试中达到了最先进的精度，在准确性和速度上均持续优于主流方法。此外，LiTEN-FF能够以高效的计算性能完成从几何结构优化到自由能面构建等一系列综合建模任务，适用于大型生物分子。该框架为先进的生物分子建模与药物设计应用提供了一个基于物理原理、多功能的坚实基础。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Accurate atomistic biomolecular simulations are vital for understanding disease mechanisms and drug discovery, yet existing methods struggle to balance quantum-mechanical accuracy with computational scalability. Classical force fields often lack precision, while quantum methods are computationally prohibitive for complex biological systems. Here we show that LiTEN, a scalable equivariant neural network, resolves this dilemma by efficiently modeling complex three- and four-body interactions with linear complexity via Linearly Tensorized Quadrangle Attention. We introduce LiTEN-FF, a foundation model pre-trained on extensive datasets to ensure broad chemical generalization across diverse molecular spaces. We demonstrate that LiTEN achieves state-of-the-art accuracy on standard benchmarks, consistently outperforming leading approaches in both precision and speed. Furthermore, LiTEN-FF enables comprehensive modeling tasks, ranging from geometry optimization to free energy surface construction, with high computational efficiency for large biomolecules. This framework provides a physically grounded, versatile foundation for advanced biomolecular modeling and drug design applications.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: biomolecular force fields, neural network, quantum-mechanical accuracy, computational scalability, drug discovery, molecular simulations, LiTEN, foundation model

### 26. ❌ Frequency-division routing via spin–refractive-index locking

**作者**: Yuan-Peng Peng, Shi-Yao Zhu, J. Q. You, Yi-Pu Wang
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70460-w](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70460-w)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是基于超材料的自旋-折射率锁定现象及其在微波频率选择性路由和非互易信号处理中的应用，属于物理学、电磁学和光子学领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像，没有提到任何医学图像、医学数据、诊断、治疗或相关应用。因此，所有关键词的相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种基于自旋-折射率锁定的超材料，实现了频率选择性手性光子-磁振子相互作用，并开发了一种可重构的片上路由器件，用于自旋选择性微波控制和非互易信号处理。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 本文展示了一种复合左右手传输线超材料中的自旋折射率锁定现象，其中表面模式的横向自旋被锁定在等效折射率的符号上。与传统自旋动量锁定不同，自旋折射率锁定在左右手频带中针对相同的能量传播方向反转自旋方向。利用这种依赖于折射率的自旋调控，我们通过将钇铁石榴石球置于超材料上方，实现了频率选择性的手性光子-磁子相互作用，并获得了强非互易性：磁子仅与自旋匹配的微波发生耦合，且所需方向由工作频带决定。通过在两频带间调谐频率，可动态切换耦合方向，从而构建出一种紧凑、可重构的片上路由器件，用于自旋选择性的微波调控与非互易信号处理。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Here we demonstrate spin-refractive-index locking (SRIL) in a composite right-left-handed transmission-line metamaterial, where the transverse spin of surface modes is locked to the sign of the effective refractive index. Unlike conventional spin-momentum locking (SML), the SRIL reverses the spin for the same energy propagation direction in right- and left-handed bands. Using this index-dependent spin control, we realize frequency-selective chiral photon-magnon interaction by placing a yttrium iron garnet (YIG) sphere above the metamaterial and achieving strong nonreciprocity, where magnons only couple to microwaves of matching spin and the required direction is determined by the operating band. Tuning the frequency across the two bands dynamically switches the coupling direction, enabling a compact, reconfigurable on-chip routing device for spin-selective microwave control and nonreciprocal signal processing.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: spin-refractive-index locking, metamaterial, frequency-selective routing, chiral photon-magnon interaction, nonreciprocal signal processing, microwave control, composite right-left-handed transmission-line, yttrium iron garnet

### 27. ❌ Discovery of van Hove singularities: electronic fingerprints of 3Q magnetic order in a van der Waals quantum magnet

**作者**: Hai-Lan Luo, Josue Rodriguez, Debasis Dutta, Maximilian Huber, Haoyue Jiang, Luca Moreschini, Caizhi Xu, Alexei Fedorov, Chris Jozwiak, Aaron Bostwick, Guoqing Chang, James G. Analytis, Dung-Hai Lee, Alessandra Lanzara
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**arXiv链接**: [https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.11796](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.11796)
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70063-5](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70063-5)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是量子磁体中的电子结构和磁性有序，属于凝聚态物理和材料科学领域，与医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像完全无关。论文使用角分辨光电子能谱研究磁性材料，不涉及任何医学图像处理或分析技术。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过角分辨光电子能谱揭示了CoₓTaS₂中3Q磁序的电子指纹，包括反墨西哥帽色散和范霍夫奇点，证实了范德华磁体中磁性与拓扑的相互作用。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 磁插层过渡金属二硫属化物正成为探索范德华磁体中奇异量子态的丰富平台。其中，Co<sub>x</sub>TaS<sub>2</sub>在近期被发现具有独特的3Q磁基态以及在临界掺杂浓度x ≈ 1/3以下存在显著的拓扑霍尔效应后，引起了广泛关注，这两种现象均与钴浓度密切相关。迄今为止，这种神秘的3Q磁序在电子结构中的直接证据仍然难以捉摸。本文报道了一项全面的掺杂依赖角分辨光电子能谱研究，揭示了这些长期寻求的特征指纹。我们的数据揭示出沿K-M-K′方向存在一个出乎意料的反墨西哥帽形色散，并伴随两个范霍夫奇点。这些特征与钴三角晶格上四分之三能带填充附近出现3Q磁序的理论预测相符。这些结果为电子结构中存在3Q磁序提供了证据，确立了TMD范德华磁体可作为可调谐材料，用以探索磁性与拓扑之间的相互作用。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Magnetically intercalated transition metal dichalcogenides are emerging as a rich platform for exploring exotic quantum states in van der Waals magnets. Among them, Co<sub>x</sub>TaS<sub>2</sub> has attracted intense interest following the recent discovery of a distinctive 3Q magnetic ground state and a pronounced topological Hall effect below a critical doping of x ≈ 1/3, both intimately tied to cobalt concentration. To date, direct signatures of this enigmatic 3Q magnetic order in the electronic structure remain elusive. Here we report a comprehensive doping dependent angle resolved photoemission spectroscopy study that unveils these long-sought fingerprints. Our data reveal an unexpected inverse-Mexican-hat dispersion along the K-M-<mml:math xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mml:msup><mml:mrow><mml:mi>K</mml:mi></mml:mrow><mml:mrow><mml:mo>'</mml:mo></mml:mrow></mml:msup></mml:math> direction, accompanied by two van Hove singularities. These features are consistent with theoretical predictions for a 3Q magnetic order near three-quarters band filling on a cobalt triangular lattice. These results provide evidence of 3Q magnetic order in the electronic structure, establishing TMD van der Waals magnets as tunable materials to explore the interplay between magnetism and topology.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: van der Waals magnet, 3Q magnetic order, angle resolved photoemission spectroscopy, van Hove singularities, topological Hall effect, transition metal dichalcogenide, electronic structure, quantum magnet

---

### 28. ❌ Evaluating LLMs' divergent thinking capabilities for scientific idea generation with minimal context

**作者**: Kai Ruan, Xuan Wang, Jixiang Hong, Peng Wang, Yang Liu, Hao Sun
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70245-1](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70245-1)

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是评估大型语言模型在科学创意生成中的发散思维能力，使用单关键词提示进行测试，涉及22个科学领域的关键词。虽然论文提到了科学领域，但具体内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像。论文的核心是LLM的创意评估基准，与医学图像处理无关。

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    LiveIdeaBench is introduced, a comprehensive benchmark evaluating LLMs' scientific idea generation by assessing divergent thinking capabilities using single-keyword prompts, and it is revealed that the scientific idea generation capabilities measured by this benchmark are poorly predicted by standard metrics of general intelligence scores.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了大型语言模型在科学创意生成中的发散思维能力，发现创意生成能力与通用智能评分相关性较弱，需要专门的评估基准和不同的训练策略。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 大型语言模型（LLM）在文献分析、实验设计等科学任务中展现出卓越能力。例如，这些模型能够精准地从论文中提取关键发现，或生成连贯的实验流程。然而，现有的评估基准主要依赖丰富的上下文输入来评测模型性能。本文提出LiveIdeaBench，这是一个通过单一关键词提示评估发散性思维能力的综合性基准，旨在系统评测LLM的科学创意生成能力。基于吉尔福德创造力理论，本基准采用动态的前沿LLM专家小组，从原创性、可行性、流畅性、灵活性及清晰度五个维度对生成的创意进行评估。通过对涵盖22个科学领域的1180个关键词进行实验，测试了超过40个领先模型，我们发现：本基准所衡量的科学创意生成能力，与通用智力评分的标准指标之间预测关联性较弱。实验结果表明，尽管在通用智力评分上存在显著差距，但如QwQ-32B-preview等模型在创意表现上可达到与claude-3.7-sonnet: thinking模型相当的水平。这些发现凸显了针对科学创意生成开发专门评估基准的必要性，并表明提升LLM的创意生成能力可能需要不同于改进通用问题解决能力的训练策略。此类策略有望推动开发更多样化的AI工具，以适应科学研究流程的不同阶段。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate remarkable capabilities in scientific tasks such as literature analysis and experimental design. For instance, these models excel at accurately extracting key findings from papers or generating coherent experimental procedures. However, existing evaluation benchmarks primarily assess performance using rich contextual inputs. We introduce LiveIdeaBench, a comprehensive benchmark evaluating LLMs' scientific idea generation by assessing divergent thinking capabilities using single-keyword prompts. Drawing from Guilford's creativity theory, our benchmark employs a dynamic panel of state-of-the-art LLMs to assess generated ideas across five dimensions: originality, feasibility, fluency, flexibility, and clarity. Through experimentation with over 40 leading models across 1180 keywords spanning 22 scientific domains, we reveal that the scientific idea generation capabilities measured by our benchmark are poorly predicted by standard metrics of general intelligence scores. Our results demonstrate that models like QwQ-32B-preview achieve creative performance comparable to models such as claude-3.7-sonnet: thinking, despite significant gaps in their general intelligence scores. These findings highlight the need for specialized evaluation benchmarks for scientific idea generation and suggest that enhancing these idea generation capabilities in LLMs may require different training strategies than those used for improving general problem-solving abilities. Such strategies could potentially enable a wider range of AI tools tailored for different stages of the scientific process.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Large Language Models, scientific idea generation, divergent thinking, evaluation benchmark, creativity assessment, single-keyword prompts, general intelligence scores, training strategies

### 29. ❌ Spatio-spectral light-by-light moulding in multimode fibre

**作者**: Yago Arosa, Tigran Mansuryan, A.C. Poisson, Wasyhun A. Gemechu, Katarzyna Krupa, Mario Ferraro, Fabio Mangini, B. Wetzel, Stefan Wabnitz, Alessandro Tonello, Laure Lavoute
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是非线性多模光纤中的光控光现象，具体涉及二次谐波信号的空间质量调控、模式转换和拉曼斯托克斯级联调控。所有关键词（medical image analysis, medical imaging, deep learning medical imaging）均与医学图像分析相关，而论文内容完全属于物理光学和光纤光子学领域，未涉及任何医学图像、医学成像或深度学习在医学成像中的应用，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了在非线性多模光纤中，通过泵浦光束调控二次谐波信号的空间质量，实现了光控光现象，并实验观察到了由二次谐波调控的拉曼斯托克斯级联增强或抑制。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 按需调控复杂光波以实现预期行为或特性是一项重大挑战。当操纵散斑光束时，由于它们固有的模糊强度与相位结构，这一任务变得尤为复杂。本文中，我们证明可通过弱散斑二次谐波信号与高功率同向传输基频泵浦波之间的保守相互作用，在多模渐变折射率光纤中对信号进行调控。具体而言，通过改变泵浦的功率或其模态分布，信号的空间质量既可被提升也可被劣化。其背后的物理机制是可由泵浦光束形状控制的光致模式转换。这一现象为在非线性多模波导中操控复杂光场开辟了新途径。这种新型光控光机制的一个突出例证是：实验中观察到可见光拉曼斯托克斯级联在二次谐波光束调控下，同时受基频光束模式功率分布调制，可实现增强或部分抑制。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Controlling complex light waves to achieve desired behaviours or characteristics on demand presents a significant challenge. This task becomes even more complicated when manipulating speckled light beams, owing to their inherently fuzzy intensity and phase structures. Here we demonstrate that a weak speckled second-harmonic signal in a multimode graded-index fibre can be manipulated via its conservative interaction with a high-power co-propagating fundamental pump wave. Specifically, the spatial quality of the signal can be either enhanced or degraded by varying the pump's power or its modal distribution. The underlying physical mechanism is the optically induced mode conversion that can be controlled by the pump beam shape. This phenomenon enables new possibilities to manipulate complex light in nonlinear multimode waveguides. A striking example of this novel light-by-light control is the experimentally observed enhancement or partial suppression of the visible Raman Stokes cascade regulated by the second harmonic beam, while modulated by the mode power distribution of the fundamental beam.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: multimode fibre, second-harmonic signal, spatial quality, mode conversion, light-by-light control, Raman Stokes cascade, nonlinear waveguides, speckled light beams

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过低聚物溶剂工程构建了具有分级氢键网络的多功能凝胶夹层，实现了透明、自修复、声学阻尼和热缓冲性能，并应用于节能安全建筑玻璃。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 聚合物凝胶的性质不仅受交联网络调控，更取决于溶剂体系。传统小分子溶剂在环境适应性、成本与生物相容性之间常需权衡取舍。本研究采用寡聚聚乙二醇作为聚甲基丙烯酸酸（PMAA）的多功能溶剂，将原本呈塑性特征的PMAA网络转化为透明、高耗散性凝胶。该寡聚溶剂通过构建具有宽强度分布的多级氢键结构，实现了弹性与黏性的耦合，在稳定网络的同时赋予体系高声阻尼与抗冲击的能量耗散能力。此外，热可逆氢键解离过程可产生宽温域吸热效应，从而提供热缓冲功能。该凝胶还表现出高透明度、强黏附性与自修复特性。基于此凝胶夹层设计，我们制备出集光透射、热调控、声衰减与机械防护于一体的复合层压玻璃。这种寡聚溶剂策略为实际建筑场景中开发多功能、高能效、高安全性的建筑玻璃应用提供了实用化路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The properties of polymer gels are governed not only by the crosslinked network but also by the solvent. Conventional small-molecule solvents impose trade-offs among environmental adaptability, cost, and biocompatibility. Here, we employ oligomeric polyethylene glycol as a multifunctional solvent for poly (methacrylic acid) (PMAA), converting the otherwise plastic PMAA network into a transparent, dissipative gel. The oligomeric solvent promotes a hierarchical hydrogen-bonding architecture with broadly distributed strengths, coupling elasticity and viscosity, stabilizing the network, and enabling high energy dissipation for acoustic damping and impact resistance. Meanwhile, thermally reversible hydrogen-bond dissociation provides broad endothermic heat absorption, affording thermal buffering. The gels further exhibit high transparency, robust adhesion, and self-healing. Harnessing the gel as an interlayer, we fabricate laminated glass that integrates light transmission, thermal regulation, sound attenuation, and mechanical protection. This oligomer-solvent strategy offers a practical route to multifunctional, energy-efficient, safer building glazing applications in real-world architecture settings.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: oligomeric solvent, hierarchical hydrogen-bonding networks, polymer gels, multifunctional glass interlayers, acoustic damping, thermal buffering, self-healing, laminated glass

### 31. ❌ Built-in tandem catalysis in hierarchical pores for efficient vinyl chloride production

**作者**: Bolin Wang, Xingyun Li, Yuxue Yue, Shuheng Tian, Ruoting Liu, Haifeng Zhang, Ding Ma
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07

|------|------|------|------|

| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是化学催化领域，具体涉及乙烯二氯和乙炔串联反应生产氯乙烯的催化剂设计，与医学图像分析、医学成像、深度学习医学成像等关键词完全无关。论文内容聚焦于多孔材料、串联催化、反应机理等化学工程主题，没有任何医学或图像处理相关内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过构建具有分级孔结构的单催化剂实现乙烯二氯和乙炔串联反应高效生产氯乙烯，并稳定运行1200小时。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 串联催化常通过设计异质活性位点以提升工业反应效率。本文针对二氯乙烷与乙炔级联生产氯乙烯的反应，在单一多级孔催化剂中构建了内置串联催化体系。采用孔道选择性填充策略，将Ru、CuRu和AuRu组分依次限域于碳材料的大孔、介孔及微孔中。机理研究表明，二氯乙烷脱氯化氢反应发生在大孔Ru位点上，生成氯乙烯；产生的H和Cl自由基在介孔CuRu位点与乙炔反应，残余乙炔则在微孔AuRu位点上发生氢氯化反应。在富氯乙烯气氛中，CuRu和AuRu对乙炔的强吸附能力使乙炔转化率接近热力学极限，并实现了1200小时连续稳定运行。这种多级孔道内的内置串联催化为单一多孔催化剂中的级联反应提供了普适性范式。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Tandem catalysis over disparate active sites is frequently designed to promote the catalytic efficiency for industrial reactions. Herein, a built-in tandem system in a single hierarchical porous catalyst is constructed for vinyl chloride production from ethylene dichloride and acetylene cascade. Using a pore-selective filling strategy, Ru, CuRu, and AuRu components are sequentially confined in the macro-, meso- and micropores of carbon material. Mechanism study shows that ethylene-dichloride dehydrochlorination occurs on macropore Ru sites, generating vinyl chloride. H and Cl radicals react with acetylene on mesopore CuRu sites, and the residual acetylene is hydrochlorinated over micropore AuRu sites. The stronger acetylene adsorption of CuRu and AuRu in a VCM-rich atmosphere enables acetylene conversion near the thermodynamic limit and stable operation for 1200 h on stream. This built-in tandem catalysis in hierarchical pores provides a general paradigm for cascade reactions in a single porous catalyst.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: tandem catalysis, hierarchical pores, vinyl chloride production, cascade reactions, porous catalyst, acetylene conversion, dehydrochlorination, thermodynamic limit

### 32. ❌ Coupling programmable shape morphing and solvent-fueled propulsion in a soft bicontinuous composite

**作者**: Pritam Giri, Angana Borbora, Debasmita Sarkar, Sourav Dutta, Alan H. Weible, Hrisikesh Sarma, Arijit Mohanta, Xiaoguang Wang, Uttam Manna
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-69432-x](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-69432-x)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|

| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是软材料、双连续复合材料、形状变形和溶剂驱动推进，属于软机器人、智能材料和材料科学领域。论文完全没有涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像的任何内容。标题、摘要和内容都与医学图像处理无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究开发了一种双连续液晶弹性体-水凝胶复合材料，实现了多刺激形状重构和溶剂驱动自推进，为无束缚软机器人和智能可重构材料提供了平台。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 自然生物常通过可逆形变重构与自主运动的耦合来适应动态环境。然而，由于结构各向异性、溶剂相容性和驱动可逆性之间存在固有矛盾，合成软材料很少能在单一平台上同时实现这两种行为。本文报道了一种双连续、单轴取向的液晶弹性体-水凝胶复合材料（BALCEH），它能够实现多刺激响应的形状重构与溶剂驱动的自主推进。该材料整合了亲水与疏水网络，从而在水性和非水性环境中均能产生不对称溶剂吸收与定向溶胀。这种结构在湿度、温度和有机溶剂作用下可实现可逆驱动，其机制由各向异性水凝胶膨胀与液晶弹性体弹性之间的相互作用所调控。BALCEH还能实现持续的Marangoni推进运动，其运动轨迹可通过燃料成分与几何结构进行编程。此外，双网络的空间重排赋予材料自适应润湿性，可在超疏油态与超疏水态之间切换。通过将形变与运动耦合于单一系统，BALCEH为无缆软体机器人与智能可重构材料提供了一个多功能平台。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Natural organisms often couple reversible shape reconfiguration and autonomous motion to adapt and respond to dynamic environments. However, synthetic soft materials rarely achieve both behaviors within a single platform due to fundamental trade-offs in structural anisotropy, solvent compatibility, and actuation reversibility. Here, we report a bicontinuous, uniaxially aligned liquid crystal elastomer-hydrogel composite (BALCEH) that allows both multi-stimuli shape reconfiguration and solvent-driven self-propulsion. The material integrates hydrophilic and hydrophobic networks, resulting in asymmetric solvent uptake and directional swelling across both aqueous and non-aqueous environments. This architecture supports reversible actuation under humidity, temperature, and organic solvents, governed by the interplay between anisotropic hydrogel expansion and LCE elasticity. BALCEH also achieves sustained Marangoni propulsion, with trajectory programmability through fuel composition and geometry. Additionally, spatial rearrangement of the dual networks imparts adaptive wettability, switching between superoleophobic and superhydrophobic states. By coupling deformation and motion in a single system, BALCEH offers a versatile platform for untethered soft robotics and intelligent, reconfigurable materials.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: soft materials, bicontinuous composite, shape morphing, self-propulsion, liquid crystal elastomer, hydrogel, soft robotics, reconfigurable materials

### 33. ❌ Electric double layer structure in concentrated aqueous solution

**作者**: Minho M. Kim, Dong Hyun Kim, Junsic Cho, Seung-Jae Shin, Chang Hyuck Choi, Hyungjun Kim
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70322-5](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70322-5)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是电化学界面中的电双层结构，使用全原子模拟和原位光谱学方法，主题为电化学、界面科学和计算化学，与医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文通过全原子模拟和实验验证，揭示了非稀释电解质浓度下电双层结构的原子尺度细节及其相变机制，并构建了电双层结构相图。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 为实现定制化电催化，电极-电解质界面受到了广泛关注。双电层为电化学反应提供了关键的微环境。然而，其原子尺度结构，尤其是与实际体系相关的非稀溶液浓度下的结构，仍未得到解析。一个显著的例子是电容曲线中从驼峰状到钟形的转变——随着浓度增加，两个峰合并，这一现象在分子层面仍知之甚少。本文通过全原子模拟，阐明了导致电容峰出现的双电层结构及其相变过程。预测的转变电位与实验峰位相符。我们观察到在阴极区域存在集体水分子重新取向，在阳极区域存在阴离子表面凝聚，这些现象通过原位光谱技术得到了进一步验证。最后，我们构建了双电层结构相图，以深入揭示双电层微环境。这项工作为设计改进的界面提供了一个有价值的框架。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Toward tailored electrocatalysis, significant attention has been directed to the electrode-electrolyte interface. The electric double layer provides a crucial microenvironment for electrochemical reactions. However, its atomic-scale structure remains unresolved, particularly for non-dilute electrolyte concentrations relevant to practical systems. A notable example is the camel-to-bell shape transition in the capacitance curve, where two peaks merge as the concentration increases, which is still poorly understood at the molecular level. Herein, using all-atom simulations, we elucidate the electric double layer structures and their phase transitions which give rise to capacitance peaks. The predicted transition potentials match the experimental peak positions. We observe collective water reorientation in the cathodic region and anion surface condensation in the anodic region, which are further validated by in situ spectroscopy. Finally, we construct an electric double layer structural phase diagram to provide detailed insight into the electric double layer microenvironment. This work presents a valuable framework for design of improved interfaces.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: electric double layer, electrocatalysis, electrode-electrolyte interface, all-atom simulations, capacitance curve, phase transitions, in situ spectroscopy, structural phase diagram

### 34. ❌ Ballistic transport in nanodevices based on single-crystalline Cu thin films

**作者**: Yongjin Cho, Su Jae Kim, Min-Hyoung Jung, Yousil Lee, Hu Young Jeong, Young-Min Kim, Hu-Jong Lee, Seong-Gon Kim, Se-Young Jeong, Gil-ho Lee
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications

**arXiv链接**: [https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.13624](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.13624)
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70252-2](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70252-2)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是纳米器件中铜薄膜的弹道输运特性，属于凝聚态物理、纳米电子学和量子输运领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像，所有关键词与论文主题完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了无晶界的90纳米厚铜薄膜纳米器件中的电子输运，通过在150纳米通道宽度器件中测量负弯曲电阻，在85K以下温度下实现了弹道输运，为探索铜的本征量子力学特性提供了可扩展平台。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 在弹道输运中，带电载流子的运动不受散射事件阻碍。在此极限下，晶体动量、自旋和量子相等微观参数得到良好保持，使得电子能在更长距离上维持量子相干性。碳纳米管、石墨烯和纳米线等纳米级材料可呈现弹道输运特性，但其在器件中的可扩展性受到显著限制。虽然沉积金属薄膜为纳米器件提供了可扩展性，但其较短的电子平均自由程阻碍了弹道输运的实现。本研究通过无晶界的90纳米厚铜薄膜制备交叉几何结构器件，探究其电子输运行为。借助负弯曲电阻测量，我们在低于85 K的温度下，于沟道宽度为150纳米的器件中实现了弹道输运。这些发现为探索铜的本征量子力学特性建立了可扩展平台，不仅深化了对金属量子输运的基础理解，也推动了其在下一代电子量子技术中的实际应用。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> In ballistic transport, the movement of charged carriers remains unimpeded by scattering events. In this limit, microscopic parameters such as crystal momentum, spin and quantum phase are well conserved, allowing electrons to maintain their quantum coherence over longer distances. Nanoscale materials, such as carbon nanotubes, graphene, and nanowires, can exhibit ballistic transport. However, their scalability in devices is significantly limited. While deposited metal films offer scalability for nanodevices, their short electronic mean free paths hinder ballistic transport. In this study, we investigated the electronic transport in cross-geometry devices fabricated with 90-nm-thick Cu films without grain boundaries. We demonstrated ballistic transport in devices with channel widths of 150 nm at temperatures below 85 K via negative bend resistance measurements. Our findings establish a scalable platform for exploring the intrinsic quantum mechanical properties of Cu, advancing both the fundamental understanding of quantum transport in metals and its practical applications in next-generation electronic quantum technologies.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: ballistic transport, nanodevices, Cu thin films, negative bend resistance, quantum transport, electronic transport, cross-geometry devices, quantum coherence

### 35. ❌ Recurrent and novel evolutionary pathways drive in vitro HIV-1 lenacapavir resistance with diverse phenotypic consequences

**作者**: Luke L. Orris, Siddiqui MA, Junyi Tang, Raajita Bose, Masahiro Yamashita
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07

| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究HIV-1对lenacapavir药物的耐药性进化机制，属于病毒学、药物开发和分子生物学领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学影像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像技术。所有关键词与论文主题无任何关联。

<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    This work supports surveillance and forecasting efforts while guiding further drug development to sustain the capsid as a viable antiviral target, as the novel pathways observed here may represent natural extensions of recurrent ones.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过加速进化方法揭示了HIV-1对lenacapavir产生耐药性的多种进化途径，包括结合口袋突变和远端电荷反转突变，其中E213K突变导致病毒产生药物依赖性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 小分子抑制剂来那卡帕韦（LEN）已明确将HIV-1衣壳确立为一个前景广阔的临床靶点。然而，早期研究表明，HIV-1可通过获得衣壳突变对LEN产生耐药性。这些突变局限于药物结合口袋，但病毒在LEN选择压力下进化潜力的广度仍未完全阐明。本研究采用加速进化方法探究HIV-1对LEN的耐药能力。尽管数千种临床毒株的序列高度保守，但结合口袋内两个位点仍表现出较高的突变耐受性和多样化的耐药特征。这些低水平耐药突变会反复选择高水平耐药突变M66I，并与其他突变协同作用，通过恢复病毒核进入能力而增强病毒适应性。随后，在结合口袋远端出现多个电荷反转替换。这些位于六聚体界面的替换可调节衣壳稳定性，并减轻LEN对衣壳的破坏作用。携带E213K替换的高度耐药变异体甚至产生药物依赖性——需要LEN才能产生具有感染性的病毒颗粒。由于本研究观察到的新耐药途径可能代表常见途径的自然延伸，这项工作不仅为监测与预测工作提供支持，同时能指导进一步的药物开发，以维持衣壳作为可行抗病毒靶点的有效性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The small-molecule inhibitor lenacapavir (LEN) has firmly established the HIV-1 capsid as a promising clinical target. However, early studies have shown that HIV-1 can develop resistance to LEN by acquiring capsid mutations. These mutations are restricted to the drug-binding pocket, but the breadth of the virus's capacity to evolve under LEN-directed pressure remains incompletely understood. Here, we employ an accelerated evolution approach to probe HIV-1's capacity for LEN resistance. Despite strong sequence conservation across thousands of clinical strains, two positions within the binding pocket exhibit high mutational tolerance and diverse resistance profiles. These low-level resistance mutations recurrently select the high-level resistance mutation M66I and together with further mutations, synergistically enhance viral fitness by restoring nuclear entry. Subsequently, multiple charge-reversing substitutions distal to the binding pocket emerge. Located at inter-hexamer interfaces, these substitutions modulate capsid stability and mitigate LEN's capsid-disrupting effects. A highly resistant variant carrying the E213K substitution becomes drug dependent; it requires LEN to generate infectious particles. As the novel pathways observed here may represent natural extensions of recurrent ones, this work supports surveillance and forecasting efforts while guiding further drug development to sustain the capsid as a viable antiviral target.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: HIV-1, lenacapavir resistance, capsid mutations, accelerated evolution, drug-binding pocket, E213K substitution, nuclear entry, antiviral target

### 36. ❌ In-situ recomposition of polyethyleneimine additive enables a multiprocess long-lifetime thermocell

**作者**: Xinya Wu, Chunlin Pang, Qikai Li, Yu-Ting Huang, Sijia Wang, Chun Cheng, Wei Li, Chuan He, Qiyu Deng, Hengjia Zhu, Meng Ni, Yun Chi, Liqiu Wang, Shien-Ping Feng
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70392-5](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70392-5)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是热电池（thermocell）技术，具体涉及聚乙烯亚胺添加剂在K3Fe(CN)6/K4Fe(CN)6热电池中的原位重组，以提高热电转换性能和长期稳定性。全文内容完全围绕热电材料、电化学、能量转换等主题，未涉及任何医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习在医学成像中的应用。因此，所有关键词的相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文通过引入聚乙烯亚胺作为自限性牺牲添加剂，显著提升了K3Fe(CN)6/K4Fe(CN)6热电池的热电性能（热电功率从1.4 mV K⁻¹提高到7.76 mV K⁻¹）和长期稳定性（>1000小时），并展示了其在温差发电系统中的可扩展性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 离子热电池为将低品位热能转化为电能提供了一条极具前景的路径，但其实际应用受到性能在波动条件下衰减以及协同作用路径有限的阻碍。本文中，我们在K<sub>3</sub>Fe(CN)<sub>6</sub>/K<sub>4</sub>Fe(CN)<sub>6</sub>热电池中引入聚乙烯亚胺作为一种自限性牺牲添加剂。在初始运行期间，聚乙烯亚胺中仅有一部分胺基与Fe(CN)<sub>6</sub><sup>3-</sup>/Fe(CN)<sub>6</sub><sup>4-</sup>发生氧化还原反应，而剩余的胺基则介导了热诱导的吸附-脱附、选择性缩合以及均相催化。这些级联效应将热电势从1.4 mV K<sup>-1</sup>提升至7.76 mV K<sup>-1</sup>。至关重要的是，聚乙烯亚胺-Fe(CN)<sub>6</sub><sup>3-</sup>反应的自限性及温度依赖性反应活性，不仅生成了扰动溶剂化的物种，而且确保了长期的功能稳定性（>1000小时）。一个概念验证面板在50 K温差下可输出超过5 V电压和7.5 mW功率，证明了系统的可扩展性。这项工作凸显了牺牲添加剂工程在实现耐用、高性能热电池以用于可持续热电转换方面的潜力。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Ionic thermocells offer a compelling route for converting low-grade heat into electricity, yet their real-world deployment is hindered by performance decay under fluctuating conditions and limited synergistic pathways. Herein, we introduce polyethyleneimine as a self-limiting sacrificial additive in a K<sub>3</sub>Fe(CN)<sub>6</sub>/K<sub>4</sub>Fe(CN)<sub>6</sub> thermocell. During initial operation, only a fraction of amine groups in polyethyleneimine engages in redox with Fe(CN)<sub>6</sub><sup>3-</sup>/Fe(CN)<sub>6</sub><sup>4-</sup>, while the remaining amine groups mediate thermally induced adsorption-desorption, selective condensation, and homogeneous catalysis. These cascaded effects boost the thermopower from 1.4 mV K<sup>-1</sup> to 7.76 mV K<sup>-1</sup>. Crucially, the self-limiting nature and temperature-dependent reactivity of polyethyleneimine-Fe(CN)<sub>6</sub><sup>3-</sup> reaction not only generates solvation-perturbing species but also ensures long-term functional stability (>1000 hours). A proof-of-concept panel delivers over 5 V and 7.5 mW under a 50 K temperature difference, demonstrating system scalability. This work highlights the potential of sacrificial additive engineering to enable durable and high-performance thermocells for sustainable heat-to-electricity conversion.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: thermocell, polyethyleneimine additive, thermopower enhancement, long-term stability, heat-to-electricity conversion, K3Fe(CN)6/K4Fe(CN)6, sacrificial additive engineering, temperature difference

### 37. ❌ High-resolution, high-throughput detection of hidden antibiotic resistance with the dilution-and-delay (DnD) susceptibility assay

**作者**: Muqing Ma, Minsu Kim
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70174-z](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70174-z)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是细菌抗生素耐药性检测的新方法（Dilution-and-Delay assay），属于微生物学、传染病学和临床诊断领域，与医学影像分析（medical image analysis/imaging）或深度学习医学影像完全无关。论文中未涉及任何图像处理、影像数据或相关技术。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    High-resolution assay-Dilution-and-Delay (DnD) provides an advanced platform for antibiotic susceptibility testing with broad impact on basic research, clinical practice, and epidemiological surveillance and supports a new framework for measuring, defining, and understanding antibiotic resistance.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文开发了一种高分辨率、高通量的Dilution-and-Delay（DnD）检测方法，用于发现传统方法难以检测的抗生素耐药性表型机制，并在临床分离株中揭示了普遍存在的隐性多药耐药性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 抗生素治疗失败率的上升凸显了耐药机制的复杂性。尽管基因编码的耐药性已得到充分研究，但近期临床研究揭示了由表型异质性驱动的非经典机制，例如异质性耐药（heteroresistance）、持留菌（persistence）或适应性耐药。然而，标准药敏试验缺乏检测这些多样化表型机制的分辨率或通量。为应对这些局限，我们基于细菌生长的两个基本原理，开发了一种可扩展的高分辨率检测方法——稀释延迟法（Dilution-and-Delay, DnD）。DnD能够检测频率低至亿分之一的罕见药物不敏感细胞，同时也能像传统最低抑菌浓度（MIC）一样反映群体抑制水平。我们在合成群落、异质性耐药、持留菌及进化进程中验证了该方法的检测能力。这些高分辨率数据揭示了传统药敏试验如何受统计检测限的制约。将DnD扩展应用于约120株临床分离株的高通量分析表明，隐蔽的多重耐药或耐受现象普遍存在。通过将高分辨率与可扩展性相结合，DnD为抗生素药敏测试提供了一个先进平台，对基础研究、临床实践和流行病学监测具有广泛影响。它支持建立一个用于测量、定义和理解抗生素耐药性的新框架。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Rising rates of antibiotic treatment failure highlight the complexity of resistance mechanisms. While genetically encoded resistance is well established, recent clinical studies have uncovered noncanonical mechanisms driven by phenotypic heterogeneity, such as heteroresistance, persistence, or adaptive resistance. Yet, standard susceptibility tests lack the resolution or throughput to detect these diverse phenotypic mechanisms. To address these limitations, we develop a scalable, high-resolution assay-Dilution-and-Delay (DnD)-by implementing two basic principles of bacterial growth. DnD detects rare drug-insensitive cells at frequencies as low as 1 in 100 million, while also reporting bulk population inhibition as the conventional MIC. We demonstrate this capability across synthetic communities, heteroresistance, persistence, and evolutionary progression. These high-resolution data expose how traditional susceptibility assays are constrained by statistical detection limits. Scaling up DnD for high-throughput application to ~120 clinical isolates reveals that under-the-radar multidrug resistance or tolerance is common. By combining resolution with scalability, DnD provides an advanced platform for antibiotic susceptibility testing with broad impact on basic research, clinical practice, and epidemiological surveillance. It supports a new framework for measuring, defining, and understanding antibiotic resistance.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: antibiotic resistance, susceptibility assay, phenotypic heterogeneity, high-throughput detection, clinical isolates, Dilution-and-Delay (DnD), heteroresistance, persistence

### 38. ❌ Reaction-induced modification of Co nanoclusters driven by Co-Mn interfacial sites to control selectivity in CO2 hydrogenation

**作者**: Hui Kang, Rong Cao, Yanlin Zhang, Xu Wang, Luming Li, Wei Chu, Riguang Zhang, Siglinda Perathoner, Gabriele Centi, Yuefeng Liu
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70328-z](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70328-z)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是催化化学领域，具体涉及钴纳米团簇在二氧化碳加氢反应中的选择性调控，通过反应诱导的结构修饰和界面位点工程来实现产物从甲烷到一氧化碳的转变。全文内容完全围绕催化剂设计、表面结构演化、反应机理等化学催化主题展开，未涉及任何医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习在医学成像中的应用。因此，所有关键词与论文内容完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究揭示了在二氧化碳加氢反应中，钴/锰氧化物界面位点驱动的碳诱导表面重构能够调控钴纳米团簇的选择性，将产物从甲烷转向一氧化碳，CO/CH4比例从0.89显著提升至13.4。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 在众多催化应用中，控制小尺寸钴纳米颗粒上化学产物的选择性至关重要。反应驱动的结构变化为调控其性能提供了另一种方法。本文发现，在热催化CO₂加氢过程中，2Co/MnOₓ催化剂（氧化锰上负载质量分数为2%的钴纳米团簇）因桥式Co-C-O-Mn界面位点的形成，发生了碳诱导的表面重构。这导致产物选择性从甲烷转向一氧化碳，CO/CH₄产物比从0.89显著提升至13.4。该Co/MnOₓ体系具有独特的界面性质，包括强亲碳性和亲氧性。它能化学吸附反应衍生的CO，促进C-O键断裂，从而加速CO解离及后续碳物种在钴纳米团簇表面的覆盖。钴纳米团簇的这种重构抑制了CO中间体加氢生成甲烷的过程。此效应为2Co/MnOₓ所特有，在更高或更低钴负载量或其他氧化物载体上均未出现。这一认识揭示了催化过程中的结构演变如何实现精确的表面工程，从而克服钴纳米团簇的结构敏感性限制。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Controlling the selectivity of chemical products on small Co nanoparticles is crucial in many catalytic applications. Reaction-driven structural changes offer an alternative methodology to regulate their properties. Herein, carbon-induced surface restructuring occurs on a 2Co/MnOₓ catalyst (cobalt nanoclusters with 2% mass loading on manganese oxide) during thermal CO<sub>2</sub> hydrogenation, driven by the formation of bridging Co-C-O-Mn interfacial sites. This leads to a shift in selectivity from methane to CO, with a remarkable enhancement of the CO/CH<sub>4</sub> product ratio from 0.89 to 13.4. Such a Co/MnO<sub>x</sub> system has unique interfacial properties, including strong carbonophilic and oxophilic characteristics. It chemisorbs reaction-derived CO and facilitates C-O bond breaking, promoting rapid CO dissociation and subsequent carbon coverage on Co nanoclusters. This restructuring of Co nanoclusters suppresses the hydrogenation of CO intermediates to methane. This effect is unique to 2Co/MnOₓ and absent at higher/lower Co loadings or other oxide supports. This insight shows how structural evolution during catalysis enables precise surface engineering, overcoming the structure-sensitivity limits of Co nanoclusters.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: CO2 hydrogenation, cobalt nanoclusters, selectivity control, interfacial sites, surface restructuring, catalyst design, reaction-driven modification, Co-Mn interface

### 39. ❌ Radiolabeling of oligopeptides by selective hydrogen isotope exchange with deuterium and tritium in aqueous buffers

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    The development of an in situ prepared catalyst for Hydrogen Isotope Exchange reactions with deuterium or tritium gas as the isotope source to selectively label peptides in aqueous solutions is reported, leading to the high selectivity in this late-stage functionalization approach of complex peptide compounds.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文开发了一种在水溶液中用氘或氚气选择性标记肽类化合物的氢同位素交换方法，通过原位制备的催化剂实现了高选择性标记，为生物药物研究提供了放射性标记示踪剂。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 有机化合物的同位素标记对生命科学的发展至关重要，并广泛应用于药物研发领域。尽管同位素标记在小分子中的应用已十分广泛，但对于肽类、抗体或酶等生物大分子的同位素标记研究仍相对不足，尽管这些大分子生物制剂在制药行业中作为变革性疗法正日益普及。本研究报道了一种原位制备的催化剂，该催化剂可利用氘气或氚气作为同位素源，在水溶液中选择性标记肽类化合物。该方法仅需少量催化剂，通过单一反应步骤即可获得放射性标记肽，其比活度足以满足生物体外实验需求，为基于生物药物的研究提供了未来发展与应用的新途径。此外，我们发现该过程中存在底物介导的活性催化物种形成机制，从而实现了对复杂肽类化合物进行后期官能团化的高选择性。通过密度泛函理论计算与核磁共振研究，我们鉴定了反应中涉及的中间体物种。这些发现加速了放射性标记示踪剂的获取，以促进对生物过程的理解，同时为高选择性碳氢键活化及碳碳键或碳杂原子键的形成提供了新机遇，有望实现高选择性的后期官能团化产物合成。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Isotopic labeling of organic compounds is crucial for advancements in life sciences and is extensively utilized in drug discovery. While isotopic labeling is widely applied to small molecules, research on isotopically labeled biologics such as peptides, antibodies, or enzymes remains less developed, despite the increasing prevalence of these larger biologics in the pharmaceutical industry as transformative treatments for patients. We report the development of an in situ prepared catalyst for Hydrogen Isotope Exchange reactions with deuterium or tritium gas as the isotope source to selectively label peptides in aqueous solutions. The method requires only low amounts of catalyst and provides the radiolabeled peptide in a single reaction step with sufficient specific activity for biological in-vitro experiments, paving the way for future developments and applications in biological based drugs studies. Furthermore, we have identified a substrate-mediated formation of the active catalytic species, leading to the high selectivity in this late-stage functionalization approach of complex peptide compounds. DFT calculations and NMR studies have identified the intermediate species involved. The reported insights accelerate the access to radiolabeled tracers to understand biological processes, as well as offer future opportunities for highly selective C-H activation and C-C or C-X bond formation to achieve highly selective late-stage functionalization products.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: isotopic labeling, hydrogen isotope exchange, peptides, radiolabeled tracers, aqueous solutions, catalyst, late-stage functionalization, biological drugs

### 40. ❌ Preventing subsoil enhanced nitrification to safeguard agroecosystem sustainability

**作者**: Yao Wang, Xin Luo, Estéban G. Jobbágy, Nandita B. Basu, Ganlin ZHANG, Yupeng Zheng, Baojing Gu, Shaoliang Zhang, Yiqi Yu, Fenfang Wang, Zeyang Lu, Ruifeng Yan, Scott X. Chang, Yonglong Lu, Qing Tian

**评分理由**: 论文研究农业生态系统中的氮循环过程，特别是亚表层增强硝化层（ENL）的形成机制及其对土壤退化和地下水硝酸盐污染的影响。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析领域，与论文的农业、环境科学主题完全无关。

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过全球氮剖面和田间实验，在约0.6米深度发现了一个以前被忽视的增强硝化层（ENL），它作为生物地球化学热点，驱动亚表层pH下降和硝酸盐淋溶到地下水，从而为农业生态系统可持续性管理提供了精确的地下目标。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 农田中氮肥的过量施用导致硝化作用驱动的氮素损失，加剧了土壤退化与地下水硝酸盐污染。通过整合全球氮素剖面数据与实地研究，我们在全球农田约0.6米深度（范围0.3至0.9米）识别出一个先前被忽视的“强化硝化层（enhanced nitrification layer, ENL）”。该层的形成依赖于四个关键过程的相互作用：根系介导的氮素输送（传送带）、土壤质地维持的富氧微环境（反应室）、硝化微生物群落（硝化引擎）以及适宜的水文条件（激活开关）。这一强化硝化层作为生物地球化学热点，驱动着深层土壤pH值下降及硝酸盐向地下水的淋溶。其发现确立了一个精确的地下作用靶区，将氮素管理从地表措施延伸至应对峰值转化的关键深度，从而推动农业生态系统的可持续发展。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The excessive application of nitrogen fertilizers in croplands drives nitrification-induced nitrogen losses, accelerating soil degradation and groundwater nitrate pollution. By synthesizing global nitrogen profiles and field studies, we identify a previously overlooked "enhanced nitrification layer (ENL)" at approximately 0.6 m depth (ranging from 0.3 to 0.9 m) across global croplands. The formation of the ENL relies on the interplay of four key processes: root-mediated nitrogen transport (the conveyor belt), an oxygenated microenvironment sustained by soil texture (the reaction chamber), nitrifier communities (the nitrification engine), and favorable hydrological conditions (the activating switch). This ENL acts as a biogeochemical hotspot, driving subsoil pH declines and nitrate leaching to groundwater. Its identification establishes a precise subsurface target, expanding nitrogen management to address the critical depth of peak transformation alongside surface measures, thereby advancing agroecosystem sustainability.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: enhanced nitrification layer, nitrogen fertilizers, soil degradation, groundwater nitrate pollution, agroecosystem sustainability, subsoil pH decline, nitrate leaching, biogeochemical hotspot

### 41. ❌ Ligand engineering tailors hydrophobic microenvironments for efficient electrocatalytic oxidation of fatty alcohol

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是电催化氧化脂肪醇的配体工程策略，属于电化学、催化、材料科学领域，与医学图像分析、医学成像、深度学习医学成像等关键词完全无关。论文内容涉及金属有机框架、疏水微环境、电催化、有机合成等，没有任何医学图像或医学成像相关内容。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文通过配体工程策略构建疏水微环境，解决了脂肪醇在水性电解质中溶解度低导致的传质限制问题，使优化的镍基金属有机框架在辛醇氧化中表现出比氢氧化镍高三倍的产率和显著提高的法拉第效率。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 脂肪醇在水系电解质中固有的低溶解度对其电催化氧化过程造成了严重的传质限制。传统阳极电催化剂因其亲水性通常活性较低，且伴随严重的析氧副反应。本研究提出了一种配体工程策略，利用镍基金属有机框架（Ni-MOFs）构建疏水微环境。通过精确调控有机配体的芳香结构，促进了脂肪醇的局部富集，并借助π-π堆积相互作用增强了结构稳定性。因此，优化后的Ni-MOF在辛醇氧化反应中表现出优于Ni(OH)<sub>2</sub>的活性，其产物生成速率提升了三倍，法拉第效率显著提高（84.7% 对比 30.8%）。所得辛酸的生产速率与先进的热催化氧化法相当。本工作阐明了一种构建疏水微环境以克服有机电催化中传质障碍的通用设计原则，展示了其实际应用潜力。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The intrinsically low solubility of fatty alcohols in aqueous electrolytes imposes critical mass transport limitations for electrocatalytic oxidation. Conventional anodic electrocatalysts typically suffer from poor activity along with severe oxygen evolution reaction due to their hydrophilicity. Here, we present a ligand engineering strategy utilizing nickel-based metal-organic frameworks (Ni-MOFs) to construct hydrophobic microenvironments. Precise modulation of the aromatic structures of organic ligands promotes local enrichment of fatty alcohols and enhances structural robustness through π-π stacking interactions. Consequently, the optimized Ni-MOF exhibits enhanced activity for octanol oxidation compared to Ni(OH)<sub>2</sub>, achieving a threefold higher production rate and significantly improved Faradaic efficiency (84.7% versus 30.8%). The octanoic acid production rate is competitive with that of state-of-the-art thermocatalytic aerobic oxidation. This work highlights a general design principle for hydrophobic microenvironment to overcome mass transport barriers in organic electrocatalysis, demonstrating its potential for practical applications.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: ligand engineering, hydrophobic microenvironment, electrocatalytic oxidation, fatty alcohol, nickel-based metal-organic frameworks, mass transport, Faradaic efficiency, octanoic acid production

### 42. ❌ Multi-electron nitrobenzothiadiazole sp-conjugated-alkynyl covalent organic frameworks for ammonium-ion batteries

**作者**: Yumin Chen, Da Zhang, Yang Qin, Chengmin Hu, Ling Miao, Yaokang Lv, Ziyang Song, LiHua GAN, Mingxian Liu
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70370-x](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70370-x)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

|------|------|------|------|

| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是用于铵离子电池的共价有机框架材料，属于材料科学和电化学领域，与医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像完全无关。论文内容涉及电池电极材料设计、电化学性能测试等，没有任何医学图像相关的内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文通过设计多电子硝基苯并噻二唑共价有机框架材料，解决了铵离子电池负极材料容量低和循环稳定性差的问题，实现了317 mAh g⁻¹的高比容量和70,000次循环的优异耐久性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 含有周期性氧化还原活性基元和共轭结构的共价有机框架正作为铵离子电池极具竞争力的负极材料而迅速发展。通过引入由动态亚胺键连接的大量单电子活性基元可提升其容量，但该设计受限于单电子氧化还原效率欠佳及连接键稳定性不足。本研究通过整合炔基苯与硝基功能化的四电子苯并噻二唑，开发出一种多双电子转移硝基苯并噻二唑共价有机框架。硝基苯并噻二唑共价有机框架中沿炔基连接的高程度π电子sp-共轭效应，以及硝基苯并噻二唑基元强大的吸电子效应，确保了多双电子硝基/噻唑位点对NH<sub>4</sub><sup>+</sup>的高可达性（利用率为95.2%），并具有更低的活化能（25.99 kJ mol<sup>-1</sup>，而苯并噻二唑共价有机框架为35.99 kJ mol<sup>-1</sup>）。硝基苯并噻二唑单元中快速的十八氢键NH<sub>4</sub><sup>+</sup>配位作用，使硝基苯并噻二唑共价有机框架负极释放出317 mAh g<sup>-1</sup>的高比容量。炔基桥联的π-共轭网络形成了抗溶解结构，实现了70,000次循环的耐久性。与高压普鲁士蓝类似物正极配对后，铵离子全电池可提供86.1 Wh kg<sup>-1</sup>的比能量（基于活性材料总质量）及25,000次循环寿命。本研究拓展了面向先进铵离子电池的高性能共价有机框架的设计视野。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Covalent organic frameworks containing periodic redox-active motifs and conjugation structures are booming as competitive negative electrodes for ammonium-ion batteries. Introducing substantial single-electron active motifs linked by dynamic imine bonds can increase their capacity; however, this design is constrained by suboptimal single-electron redox efficiency and insufficient linkage stability. Here we unlock a multiple two-electron-transfer nitrobenzothiadiazole covalent organic framework via integrating alkynyl benzenes and nitro-functionalized four-electron benzothiadiazoles. The high degree of π-electron sp-conjugation along alkynyl linkages and strong electron-drawing effect of nitrobenzothiadiazole motifs in nitrobenzothiadiazole covalent organic framework promise high NH<sub>4</sub><sup>+</sup> accessibility of multi-two-electron nitro/thiazole sites (95.2% utilization) with a lower activation energy (25.93 vs. 35.99 kJ mol<sup>-1</sup> of benzothiadiazole covalent organic framework).The fast octadeca-H-bonded NH<sub>4</sub><sup>+</sup> coordination in nitrobenzothiadiazole units liberates a high specific capacity of 317 mAh g<sup>-1</sup> for nitrobenzothiadiazole covalent organic framework negative electrode. The alkynyl-bridged π-conjugation network establishes structural anti-dissolution to enable a cycling durability of 70,000 cycles. Paired with high-voltage Prussian blue analogue positive electrode, the ammonium-ion full battery delivers a specific energy of 86.1 Wh kg<sup>-1</sup> (based on total active material mass) and a lifespan of 25,000 cycles. This work extends the design landscape of high-performance covalent organic frameworks for advanced ammonium-ion batteries.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: covalent organic frameworks, ammonium-ion batteries, nitrobenzothiadiazole, multi-electron transfer, alkynyl conjugation, high specific capacity, cycling durability, Prussian blue analogue

### 43. ❌ Lorentz skew scattering and giant nonreciprocal magneto-transport

**作者**: Cong Xiao, Yue-Xin Huang, Shengyuan A. Yang
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**arXiv链接**: [https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.07746](https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.07746)
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70269-7](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70269-7)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|

| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是凝聚态物理中的非线性磁输运理论，具体涉及洛伦兹偏散射机制、拓扑晶体绝缘体和外尔半金属的输运特性。所有评分关键词（medical image analysis, medical imaging, deep learning medical imaging）均与医学图像分析相关，而论文内容完全不涉及医学、图像处理或深度学习，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该理论研究揭示了洛伦兹偏散射作为清洁样品中非线性磁输运的主导机制，并应用于拓扑材料中实现了巨大的输运非互易性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 尽管已有大量研究，洁净样品中非线性（非互易）磁输运的主导机制仍不明确。这一理论空白阻碍了高效非互易器件设计原则的发展。本文揭示了一种由洛伦兹力与斜散射协同作用产生的、迄今尚未被探索的非互易磁输运效应。该洛伦兹斜散射机制的重要性在于，它在高电导率体系中同时主导纵向与横向响应，并展现出区别于所有已知机制的标度行为。在低温下，其线性电导率呈现三次方标度关系；而当温度升高、声子散射开始作用时，标度行为则转变为四次方。将我们发展的微观理论应用于拓扑晶体绝缘体SnTe的表面输运以及外尔半金属的体输运，均得到了重要结果，这为在具有拓扑能带特征的高迁移率材料中实现巨大的输运非互易性指明了一条新路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Despite extensive research, the primary mechanism governing nonlinear (nonreciprocal) magneto-transport in clean samples remains unknown. This theoretical gap has impeded the development of design principles for efficient nonreciprocal devices. Here, we unveil a hitherto unexplored effect in nonreciprocal magneto-transport from cooperative action of Lorentz force and skew scattering. The significance of this Lorentz skew scattering mechanism lies in that it dominates both longitudinal and transverse responses in highly conductive systems, and it exhibits a scaling behavior distinct from all known mechanisms. At low temperature, it shows a cubic scaling in linear conductivity, whereas the scaling becomes quartic at elevated temperature when phonon scattering kicks in. Applying our developed microscopic theory to surface transport in topological crystalline insulator SnTe and bulk transport in Weyl semimetals leads to significant results, suggesting a new route to achieve giant transport nonreciprocity in high-mobility materials with topological band features.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: nonreciprocal magneto-transport, Lorentz skew scattering, topological crystalline insulator, Weyl semimetals, nonlinear transport, scaling behavior, high-mobility materials, theoretical mechanism

### 44. ❌ Cyclophilin A stabilizes the capsid protein p72 to facilitate African swine fever virus replication

**作者**: Hui Kong, Liqin Yang, Zhenjiang Zhang, Ying Zhang, Linlin Liu, Wan Wang, Linfei Song, Yuanmao Zhu, Encheng Sun, Fang Li, Zhigao Bu, Xiangpeng Sheng, Dongming Zhao
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70430-2](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70430-2)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究非洲猪瘟病毒（ASFV）的复制机制，聚焦于宿主蛋白CypA如何稳定病毒衣壳蛋白p72以促进病毒复制。研究内容属于病毒学、分子生物学和传染病学领域，涉及蛋白质相互作用、稳定性和抗病毒策略。论文未涉及医学影像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像的任何方面，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    It is demonstrated that host-mediated stabilization of p72 is essential for efficient ASFV replication and host CypA is highlighted as a promising target for antiviral strategies against ASFV.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究发现宿主蛋白CypA通过稳定非洲猪瘟病毒的衣壳蛋白p72来促进病毒复制，抑制CypA可破坏病毒工厂形成和病毒组装，为抗病毒策略提供了新靶点。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 非洲猪瘟病毒（ASFV）是一种大型DNA病毒，对全球养猪业构成重大威胁。其病毒粒子由主要结构蛋白p72构成的二十面体衣壳包裹，p72约占病毒粒子总质量的三分之一。尽管p72含量丰富，但调控其稳定性的机制尚不清楚。本研究证明，宿主介导的p72稳定化对于ASFV的有效复制至关重要。通过p72共沉淀物的质谱分析，我们鉴定出宿主亲环蛋白A（Cyclophilin A, CypA，亦称PPIA）是p72的关键结合伴侣。CypA在体外和体内均与p72相互作用，并通过其疏水腔特异性结合p72的暴露区域。CypA的相互作用通过减少p72的泛素化和阻止蛋白酶体降解来稳定p72，而环状CypA抑制剂则通过破坏这种相互作用并促进其泛素化来使p72失稳。重要的是，对CypA进行遗传或药理学抑制会显著损害ASFV的复制。从机制上讲，抑制CypA会通过降低p72蛋白积累（而不影响其转录）来破坏病毒工厂的形成和病毒粒子的组装。综上所述，我们的研究揭示了一种依赖宿主的衣壳蛋白稳定性调控机制，并强调宿主CypA是抗ASFV病毒策略的一个有前景的靶点。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> African swine fever virus (ASFV) is a large DNA virus that poses a major threat to the global swine industry. Its virion is encapsulated by an icosahedral capsid predominantly composed of the structural protein p72, which constitutes approximately one-third of the total virion mass. Despite its abundance, the mechanisms regulating p72 stability remain poorly understood. Here, we demonstrate that host-mediated stabilization of p72 is essential for efficient ASFV replication. Mass spectrometry of p72 co-precipitates identified host cyclophilin A (CypA, also known as PPIA) as a key binding partner of p72. CypA interacts with p72 both in vitro and in vivo, specifically engaging exposed regions of p72 via its hydrophobic cavity. CypA interaction stabilizes p72 by reducing its ubiquitination and preventing proteasomal degradation, whereas cyclic CypA inhibitors destabilize p72 by disrupting this interaction and promoting its ubiquitination. Importantly, genetic or pharmacological inhibition of CypA markedly impairs ASFV replication. Mechanistically, CypA inhibition disrupts viral factory formation and virion assembly by decreasing p72 protein accumulation without affecting its transcription. Together, our findings uncover a host-dependent mechanism regulating capsid protein stability and highlight host CypA as a promising target for antiviral strategies against ASFV.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: African swine fever virus, ASFV, cyclophilin A, CypA, capsid protein p72, viral replication, protein stability, antiviral target

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 禽流感病毒（AIV）构成重大的人畜共患威胁，并具有引发大流行的潜力。水鸟通过接触和病毒重配，促进了禽流感病毒向家畜和人类的溢出。本文提出水鸟活动熵（Waterbird Activity Entropy, WAE），这是一个基于全球779个物种月度分布的水鸟活动强度指标。WAE对全球禽流感病例（尤其是H5N1亚型）展现出强大的解释力（AUC = 0.87 ± 0.001），揭示了其识别禽流感病毒暴露热点的潜力，这些热点覆盖了全球14%的陆地面积。值得注意的是，美国、欧盟、中国和印度境内的禽流感暴露热点，包含了全球52%的暴露人口、41%的牛以及51%的家禽。尽管报告病例数不足全球的1%，但撒哈拉以南非洲地区拥有超过3亿公顷的热点区域（占全球15%），凸显了巨大的监测缺口。这一基于WAE的框架通过纳入水鸟居留时间，增强了禽流感风险评估能力，为预测禽流感病毒的出现和改进监测工作提供了关键见解。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Avian influenza viruses (AIV) pose a major zoonotic threat with pandemic potential. Waterbirds facilitate AIV spillovers into farm animals and humans through exposure and virus reassortment. Here, we propose waterbird activity entropy (WAE), an indicator of waterbird activity intensity based on monthly distributions of 779 species worldwide. WAE demonstrated high explanative power (AUC = 0.87 ± 0.001) for global avian influenza cases, particularly for H5N1, revealing the potential of WAE for identifying AIV exposure hotspots which cover 14% of global land area. Notably, the AIV exposure hotspots in the USA, EU, China, and India contain 52% of the globally exposed human population, 41% cattle, and 51% poultry. Despite reporting <1% of global cases, sub-Saharan Africa contains >300 Mha of hotspots area (15% globally), highlighting considerable surveillance gaps. This WAE-based framework enhances AIV risk assessment by incorporating waterbird residency time, offering critical insights for anticipating AIV emergence and improving surveillance.

</details>
<br>

**作者**: Zhe Lu, Wei Liu, Zeshu Zhang, Zhongyi Chen, Jian Sun, Wanguo Gao, Yao Liu, Wa Gao, Guoping Hu, Yingfang Yao, Dongxu Ji, Junhua Zhao, Zhigang Zou, Linlin Wang

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了通过烷基硅烷修饰Ni/CeO2催化剂来增强氢迁移，从而显著提升光热Sabatier反应性能，实现了99.9%的CO2单程转化率、接近100%的CH4选择性和约25.0%的户外能量转换效率。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 氢迁移是加氢反应中至关重要的过程。在过去的数十年中，表面氧一直被认为是氢迁移的主要路径，而还原反应的发生可能生成水并抑制迁移过程。因此，通过精确的表面修饰来扩展氢迁移路径，可能对提升加氢反应活性具有潜在益处，但这仍具挑战性。本文选择萨巴蒂尔（Sabatier）反应作为原型反应，其催化性能高度依赖于氢迁移的活性。通过在基准Ni/CeO<sub>2</sub>催化剂上修饰少量不可还原的烷基硅烷，氢的活化、迁移及整体加氢反应均得到显著增强。得益于此，结合萨巴蒂尔反应本身的放热特性，仅依靠太阳能驱动的反应即可实现99.9%的CO<sub>2</sub>单程转化率、接近100%的CH<sub>4</sub>选择性，并在户外实践中达到约25.0%的能量转换效率。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Hydrogen migration is a process of key importance in hydrogenation reactions. In past decades, surface oxygen has been considered the major pathway for hydrogen migration, whereas the reduction reaction may occur to yield water and inhibit the migration. Thus, extending hydrogen migration via precise surface decoration could potentially be beneficial to the activity of hydrogenation reactions, yet it remains challenging. Herein, the Sabatier reaction is chosen as the archetype reaction, in which the catalytic performance is highly dependent on the activity of hydrogen migration. By decorating a minor amount of non-reducible alkylsilane over the benchmark Ni/CeO<sub>2</sub> catalyst, the hydrogen activation, migration, and overall hydrogenation reaction have been enhanced significantly. As a result, with the help of the exothermic nature of the Sabatier reaction, the solely solar-driven reaction can be conducted with a CO<sub>2</sub> single pass conversion of 99.9%, a near-unity CH<sub>4</sub> selectivity, and an energy conversion efficiency of ~25.0% for outdoor practice.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Sabatier reaction, hydrogen migration, alkylsilane decoration, Ni/CeO2 catalyst, photothermal catalysis, CO2 conversion, CH4 selectivity, solar-driven reaction

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究发现常见的财富分布呈现方式会导致人们低估经济不平等，并提出了两种认知偏差（分区依赖和中层忽视）以及缓解这些偏差的呈现指南。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 经济不平等是选举与立法中的关键议题，因此拥有具备认知能力的选民对明智的政策制定至关重要。然而，公众对不平等真实程度的误解普遍存在。本文证明，当前呈现经济分布最常用的形式往往会弱化观看者对不平等的感知。我们首先指出，主流媒体对不平等的描绘包含可能引发偏差的特征。随后，通过九项实验（样本量 N = 3599 名美国成年人），我们探究了这些常见的不平等表征如何引发认知偏差，并测试了缓解这些偏差的方法。具体而言，我们记录了人们在评估经济分布时的两种偏差：第一，人们对已识别群体规模差异（例如前1%与前10%）的敏感度不足，导致其判断受到人口划分方式的任意性影响（分割依赖，partition dependence）；第二，相对于最富裕与最贫困群体，人们的判断会低估中间群体信息的重要性（中间忽视，middle neglect）。我们测试了缓解这些偏差的方法，并最终提出能够促进形成更准确认知的呈现准则。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Economic inequality is a critical issue in elections and legislating, so having an informed electorate is vital to sensible policymaking. Unfortunately, misperceptions about the true extent of inequality abound. Here, we demonstrate that the most prevalent formats for representing economic distributions tend to dampen viewer impressions of inequality. We begin by showing that the most popular newspaper portrayals of inequality contain potentially biasing features. Next, in nine experiments (N = 3599 U.S. adults), we explore how these common representations of inequality evoke biased impressions and we test methods to mitigate these biases. Specifically, we document two biases in how people evaluate economic distributions. First, people are under-sensitive to differences in the size of identified population groups (e.g., top 1% vs. top 10%) such that their judgments become distorted by arbitrary ways in which a population is divided (partition dependence). Second, people's judgments under-weight information about intermediate groups relative to the most- and least-wealthy groups (middle neglect). We test ways to mitigate these biases and conclude by proposing presentation guidelines that promote more accurate impressions.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: economic inequality, wealth distributions, cognitive biases, partition dependence, middle neglect, visual representations, experimental studies, presentation guidelines

### 48. ❌ Molecular fence Cu-based catalyst for CO2 hydrogenation to CO with high activity and durability

**作者**: Weige Su, Xuehui Jia, Xintan Deng, Xu Fan, Syed Jalil Shah, Changhao Li, Jiajun Zeng, Yilin Lou, Jianhua Chen, Zhongxing Zhao, Yujiao Wang
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70333-2](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70333-2)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|

| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是CO2氢化制CO的Cu基催化剂（Cu@mMOR），涉及催化化学、材料科学和化学工程领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像。标题、摘要和内容均未提及任何医学图像相关概念，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了通过将Cu簇封装到mMOR沸石中制备Cu@mMOR催化剂，用于CO2氢化制CO反应，解决了传统Cu基催化剂因Ostwald-ripening和热聚集而快速失活的问题，实现了高达3290 mmol gcat-1 h-1的CO产率和788小时的催化稳定性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 利用铜基催化剂将CO<sub>2</sub>转化为高附加值合成气（CO与H<sub>2</sub>）的研究备受关注。然而，这类催化剂因奥斯特瓦尔德熟化和热聚集作用而快速失活。本研究提出将铜簇封装于mMOR沸石中，构建分离位点催化剂Cu@mMOR。在逆水煤气变换反应（RWGS）中，Cu@mMOR中的mMOR沸石直接捕获并活化CO<sub>2</sub>，同时凭借其小于3.0 Å的孔道作为分子栅栏，阻止CO<sub>2</sub>接触铜簇。封装于mMOR中的铜簇具有丰富的铜空位，可显著促进H<sub>2</sub>的异裂解离，将H<sup>*</sup>物种传递至mMOR上活化的CO<sub>2</sub>并转化为CO。这种分离位点策略在提升催化活性的同时，巧妙改变了CO<sub>2</sub>反应路径，有效抑制了铜组分的烧结聚集与奥斯特瓦尔德熟化。最终，Cu@mMOR实现了高达3290 mmol g<sub>cat</sub><sup>-1</sup> h<sup>-1</sup>的CO时空产率，且催化稳定性长达788小时。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The conversion of CO<sub>2</sub> into high-value syngas (CO and H<sub>2</sub>) using Cu-based catalysts has garnered considerable interest. However, these catalysts deactivate rapidly due to Ostwald-ripening and thermal aggregation. Herein, we propose to encapsulate Cu-cluster into mMOR zeolite for engineering a separation-site catalyst Cu@mMOR. In the reverse water-gas shift reaction (RWGS), mMOR zeolite of Cu@mMOR directly captures and then activates CO<sub>2</sub>, and simultaneously serves as a molecular fence to prevent CO<sub>2</sub> contact with Cu-clusters surrounding with small pore of mMOR (<3.0 Å) channels. These encapsulated Cu-clusters in mMOR possess considerable Cu vacancies, which significantly facilitate H<sub>2</sub> heterolytic dissociation, transferring H<sup>*</sup> species towards activated CO<sub>2</sub> on mMOR and converting them into CO. This separation-site strategy efficiently increases catalytic activation while intelligently altering the CO<sub>2</sub> reaction pathway, preventing Cu from thermal agglomeration and Oswald ripening in the catalyst. Consequently, Cu@mMOR attains a space-time yield of CO as high as 3290 mmol g<sub>cat</sub><sup>-1</sup> h<sup>-1</sup>, with catalytic stability extending up to 788 hours.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: CO2 hydrogenation, Cu-based catalyst, mMOR zeolite, reverse water-gas shift reaction, catalytic stability, separation-site strategy, Cu@mMOR, CO production

### 50. ❌ Updating an allocentric goal from lateralised egocentric visual memories

**作者**: Antoine Wystrach, Florent Le Moël, Léo Clément, Sebastian Schwarz
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-025-67545-3](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-025-67545-3)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究昆虫（蚂蚁）的视觉导航神经机制，涉及大脑半球处理、空间记忆整合和计算建模，完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像。所有关键词与论文内容无任何关联。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    How compact brains leverage bilateral processing to combine spatial representations for visual navigation is revealed, demonstrating how noisy, viewpoint-dependent lateralized inputs are transformed into stable allocentric directional control.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究揭示了蚂蚁如何通过大脑半球处理将自我中心的视觉记忆整合为世界参照的目标方向，用于视觉导航。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 动物通过整合自我中心（视角依赖）与异我中心（世界参照）的空间表征进行导航，但其大脑如何实现这种整合尚不明确。本研究揭示了蚂蚁等昆虫导航专家的脑部如何完成这一任务。野外实验表明，蚂蚁通过一种偏侧化机制识别长期自我中心视觉记忆——这些记忆被认为编码于蘑菇体中：蚂蚁并非在朝向目标时记忆视图，而是通过侧视存储这些记忆。识别信号传递左转或右转的信息，但并不直接驱动运动反应。相反，这些信号被分别处理——可能是在两个大脑半球中——并在一个古老的中枢脑区（中央复合体）中整合，以更新目标朝向。这一目标朝向——此时已锚定于异我中心参照系中——随后与天体罗盘线索共同用于稳健的转向控制。基于昆虫神经回路构建的计算模型验证了这一两阶段过程，阐明了嘈杂的、视角依赖的偏侧化输入如何转化为稳定的异我中心方向控制。这些发现揭示了紧凑的大脑如何利用双侧处理机制，将不同空间表征整合用于视觉导航。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Animals navigate by combining egocentric (viewpoint-dependent) and allocentric (world-referenced) spatial representations, yet how their brains achieve this integration remains unclear. Here we show how the brains of insect expert navigators, such as ants, accomplish this task. Field experiments reveal that ants recognise long-term egocentric visual memories - assumed to be encoded in the Mushroom Bodies - via a lateralized mechanism: instead of memorising views while facing their goal, ants store these memories by looking to the sides. Recognition signals inform whether to turn left or right, but do not directly drive motor responses. Instead, they are processed separately - presumably in the two brain hemispheres - and integrated to update a goal heading in an ancestral, central brain region -the central complex. This goal heading -now anchored in an allocentric frame-is then used with celestial compass cues for robust steering. Computational models based on insect neural circuits validate this two-stage process, demonstrating how noisy, viewpoint-dependent lateralized inputs are transformed into stable allocentric directional control. These findings reveal how compact brains leverage bilateral processing to combine spatial representations for visual navigation.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: visual navigation, egocentric memory, allocentric representation, lateralized processing, insect brain, central complex, computational modeling, spatial integration

### 51. ❌ African inland wetland area on the rise during the 21st century

**作者**: Anzhen Li, Shengbo Chen, Kaishan Song, Yuanzhi Zhang, Zongming Wang, Dehua Mao
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06

**评分理由**: 论文研究非洲湿地（包括沿海和内陆湿地）的面积变化、驱动因素及未来趋势，使用遥感影像（Landsat）、土壤湿度数据和气候模型进行分析。研究主题属于环境科学、遥感、生态学和气候变化领域，与医学影像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学影像完全无关。

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究利用遥感数据和气候模型分析非洲湿地变化，发现1984-2021年间非洲湿地总体损失轻微（0.51%），内陆湿地面积略有增加（0.50%），而沿海湿地损失显著（9.64%），且未来内陆湿地面积可能呈上升趋势但仍有不确定性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 全球湿地正面临气候变化与人类活动的威胁，然而非洲湿地的现状尚不明确。本研究利用27万个采样点、81万幅Landsat影像及14个CMIP6模型的土壤湿度数据，绘制了非洲湿地分布图，评估了其面积损失、驱动因素及气候变化下的未来趋势。结果显示，1984年至2021年间非洲未出现大规模湿地丧失（净损失0.51%），损失集中于沿海区域（净损失9.64%），而内陆湿地面积略有增加（净增长0.50%）。通过对比湿地面积时间序列与相关驱动因子发现，内陆湿地面积变化与气候变化密切相关，人类活动则加剧了沿海湿地的丧失。TOPMODEL模型预测表明，至2100年内陆湿地面积将呈上升趋势，但仍存在不确定性，未来内陆湿地仍面临丧失风险。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Wetlands face threats from climate change and human activities worldwide, yet the status of African wetlands remains unknown. This study mapped African wetlands and assessed area loss, drivers, and future trends under climate change using 270,000 sampling points, 810,000 Landsat images, and soil moisture data from 14 CMIP6 models. The results reveal no large-scale loss of wetlands in Africa from 1984 to 2021 (0.51% net loss), with the loss concentrated in coastal areas (9.64% net loss), while inland wetlands show a slight increase in area (0.50% net increase). A comparison of the time series of wetland area and related drivers showed that the change of inland wetland area is closely related to climate change, and human activities have exacerbated the loss of coastal wetlands. TOPMODEL projections suggest an upward trend in inland wetland area by 2100, but uncertainty persists and inland wetlands remain at risk of loss in the future.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: African wetlands, wetland area change, Landsat images, climate change, coastal wetland loss, inland wetland increase, CMIP6 models, TOPMODEL projections

### 52. ❌ AMR-GNN: a multi-representation graph neural network framework to enable genomic antimicrobial resistance prediction

**作者**: Hoai-An Nguyen, Anton Y. Peleg, Jessica A. Wisniewski, Xiaoyu Wang, Zhikang Wang, Luke V. Blakeway, Gnei Z. Badoordeen, Ravali Theegala, Nhu Quynh Doan, Matthew H. Parker, Anna G. Green, Jiangning Song, Dowe Dl, Nenad Maćešić
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-69934-8](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-69934-8)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文《AMR-GNN: a multi-representation graph neural network framework to enable genomic antimicrobial resistance prediction》的研究主题是基因组学、抗菌素耐药性（AMR）预测和深度学习，具体涉及全基因组测序（WGS）数据、图神经网络（GNN）和机器学习方法。论文内容完全聚焦于基因组序列分析和AMR表型预测，未涉及任何医学影像分析（如X光、CT、MRI等）或医学成像技术。因此，所有评分关键词（medical image analysis, medical imaging, deep learning medical imaging）与论文主题完全无关，相关度均为0分。加权总分为0.0分（0×1.0 + 0×1.0 + 0×1.0），低于动态及格分14.0分。作者列表中未包含指定专家。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种基于多表示图神经网络（AMR-GNN）的框架，用于从基因组序列数据预测抗菌素耐药性（AMR）表型，并在铜绿假单胞菌和公开数据集上验证了其有效性和广泛适用性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 全基因组测序数据是理解抗菌素耐药性机制的重要资源。然而，全基因组测序数据具有高维度特性，且缺乏标准化的基因组表征方法，这是预测抗菌素耐药性表型的主要障碍。为充分挖掘这些高分辨率数据，我们提出了AMR-GNN——一个基于图深度学习的框架，该框架通过图神经网络整合多种基因组表征，以实现从基因组序列数据中预测抗菌素耐药性表型。我们以铜绿假单胞菌（一种因其复杂抗菌素耐药性机制而闻名的临床相关革兰氏阴性细菌病原体）对AMR-GNN进行了测试。我们将AMR-GNN作为一个概念验证框架提出，旨在通过数据驱动的机器学习方法解决抗菌素耐药性表型预测中的若干关键问题，包括利用多种基因组表征以提升性能、减轻克隆关系的影响，以及识别有信息量的生物标志物以提供可解释性。在涵盖革兰氏阴性和革兰氏阳性病原体的最大公开数据集上进行的后续验证表明，AMR-GNN在检测多样化的、临床相关的病原体-药物组合中的抗菌素耐药性方面具有广泛的适用性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Whole-genome sequencing (WGS) data are an invaluable resource for understanding antimicrobial resistance (AMR) mechanisms. However, WGS data are high-dimensional and the lack of standardized genomic representations is a key barrier to AMR phenotype prediction. To fully explore these high-resolution data, we propose AMR-GNN, a graph deep learning-based framework that integrates multiple genomic representations with graph neural networks (GNN) to enable AMR phenotype prediction from genomic sequence data. We test AMR-GNN with Pseudomonas aeruginosa, a clinically relevant Gram-negative bacterial pathogen known for its complex AMR mechanisms. We present AMR-GNN as a proof-of-concept framework designed to address several key problems in AMR phenotype prediction with data-driven machine learning (ML) approaches, including using multiple genomic representations to enhance performance, to mitigate the influence of clonal relationships and to identify informative biomarkers to provide explainability. Follow-up validation on the largest publicly available dataset spanning both Gram-negative and Gram-positive pathogens highlights AMR-GNN's broad applicability in detecting AMR in diverse and clinically relevant pathogen-drug combinations.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: antimicrobial resistance prediction, graph neural network, whole-genome sequencing, genomic representations, machine learning, AMR phenotype, Pseudomonas aeruginosa, biomarkers

### 53. ❌ Phosphorylation of WDR48 by phototropins drives starch degradation to promote stomatal opening

**作者**: Shota Yamauchi, Saashia Fuji, Hiroki Ikuta, Naoyuki Sugiyama, Yutaka Kodama, Luca Distefano, Haruki Fujii, Kota Yamashita, Hinano Takase, Mika Nomoto, Y. Tada, Taishi Umezawa, Kazuhiro Hotta, Diana Santelia, Ken-ichiro Shimazaki, Atsushi Takemiya
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70314-5](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70314-5)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 该论文研究植物气孔开闭的分子机制，具体涉及光受体phototropins、WD-repeat蛋白48（WDR48）的磷酸化以及淀粉降解过程。所有评分关键词均与医学影像分析相关，而论文内容完全属于植物生物学领域，未涉及任何医学、影像或深度学习内容，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    It is proposed that the coordinated control of starch synthesis by red light and its degradation by blue light signalling through WDR48 and BLUS1 is a key mechanism for stomatal opening by red and blue light.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究发现光受体phototropins通过磷酸化WDR48驱动淀粉降解，从而促进植物气孔在蓝光下开放，揭示了红光和蓝光协同调控气孔开闭的关键机制。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 植物气孔在红光背景照射下响应蓝光开放。红光通过保卫细胞光合作用诱导淀粉积累，而蓝光则通过向光色素磷酸化BLUS1激活质膜H<sup>+</sup>-ATP酶，导致淀粉快速降解，从而促进气孔开放。然而，向光色素介导淀粉降解的具体机制尚不明确。本研究鉴定出WD重复蛋白48（WDR48）为淀粉降解的关键因子。磷酸化蛋白质组学分析显示，WDR48响应蓝光发生磷酸化。WDR48突变会损害蓝光诱导的淀粉降解与气孔开放。向光色素可与WDR48互作并使其磷酸化。WDR48与BLUS1构成了淀粉降解所需的两条独立信号通路。我们认为，红光通过促进淀粉合成与蓝光信号通过WDR48和BLUS1介导的淀粉降解协同调控，是红光与蓝光共同驱动气孔开放的关键机制。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Plant stomata open in response to blue light under a background of red light. Red light induces starch accumulation through guard cell photosynthesis, whereas blue light causes rapid starch degradation via the activation of plasma membrane H<sup>+</sup>-ATPase through phosphorylation of BLUS1 by phototropins, thus promoting stomatal opening. However, how phototropins mediate starch degradation remains unclear. In this study, we identified WD-repeat protein 48 (WDR48), which is essential for starch degradation. Phosphoproteomic analysis revealed that WDR48 was phosphorylated in response to blue light. Mutation of WDR48 impaired starch degradation and stomatal opening by blue light. Phototropins interacted with and phosphorylated WDR48. WDR48 and BLUS1 constituted separate signalling pathways required for starch degradation. We propose that the coordinated control of starch synthesis by red light and its degradation by blue light signalling through WDR48 and BLUS1 is a key mechanism for stomatal opening by red and blue light.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: stomatal opening, starch degradation, phototropins, WDR48 phosphorylation, blue light signaling, plant biology, guard cells, red and blue light coordination

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文通过综合古海洋学证据，提出北美冰盖在过去的温暖间冰期持续存在，这一发现挑战了现有假设，并表明忽视这一持续性可能导致低估南极冰盖对变暖的敏感性，从而影响未来气候和海平面预测的准确性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 未来海平面上升的速度将取决于南极冰盖对气候变暖的响应。当前对南极冰盖的预测基于一个假设：过去间冰期的海平面峰值出现在北美冰盖复合体消失之后。我们综合古海洋学及相关学科的证据，提出北美冰盖复合体在最近百万年间部分最温暖的间冰期依然持续存在。研究表明，忽视北美冰盖的持续性可能导致低估南极冰盖对变暖的敏感性；这一范式转变开辟了新的研究路径，有望提升气候与海平面预测准确性的可信度。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> How fast future sea level rises will depend on the Antarctic Ice Sheet (AIS) response to warming. AIS projections are shaped by the assumption that sea-level peaks during past interglacials occurred after the North American ice sheet complex (NAIS) disappeared. We synthesize evidence from paleoceanography and allied disciplines to argue that NAIS persisted into some of the warmest interglacials of the last million years. We show that overlooking NAIS persistence may lead to underestimation of AIS sensitivity to warming, and propose that this paradigm shift opens research avenues that can increase confidence in the accuracy of climate and sea-level projections.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: North American ice sheet, interglacials, sea-level projections, Antarctic Ice Sheet sensitivity, paleoceanography, climate projections, ice sheet persistence, warming response

### 55. ❌ STIM1-Mitofusin2 interactions tether mitochondria and melanosome contacts that promote melanosome maturation

**作者**: Isshin Shiiba, Yuto Ishikawa, Hijiri Oshio, Naoki Ito, Fuya Yamaguchi, Hiroaki Sato, H. Ando, Keitaro Umezawa, Yuri Miura, Yuhei Araiso, Koki Nakamura, Yusuke Hirabayashi, Ryoko Inatome, Shigeru Yanagi
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70282-w](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70282-w)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是细胞生物学中STIM1-MFN2介导的线粒体-黑素体接触调控黑素体成熟的分子机制，属于基础细胞生物学研究。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像技术，这些关键词与论文主题无任何关联。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    This work shows that mitochondria-melanosome contacts dynamically increase during melanosome maturation and are mediated by STIM1-MFN2 interactions, and reveals a mechanism by which mitochondria-melanosome contacts regulate melanosome maturation.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究发现STIM1-MFN2相互作用介导线粒体与黑素体接触，通过增加局部ATP供应促进黑素体酸化，从而调控黑素体成熟。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 线粒体与多种细胞器形成接触位点以协调多样化的细胞过程。黑素体作为溶酶体相关细胞器，通过逐步成熟来合成并储存黑色素，但其与线粒体的相互作用机制尚不明确。本研究揭示线粒体-黑素体接触在黑素体成熟过程中动态增加，并由STIM1-MFN2相互作用介导。利用基于NanoBiT的活细胞可逆接触监测系统MiMSBiT（应用NanoBiT技术的线粒体-黑素体接触报告系统），我们发现STIM1定位于黑素体并促进其与线粒体MFN2的接触。黑素体腔内钙离子的瞬时下降可诱导STIM1聚集并增强其与MFN2的结合。这些接触能局部提升线粒体ATP供应，通过质子通道激活导致黑素体腔酸化。该酸化过程促进PMEL原纤维形成——这是黑素体成熟的关键步骤。综上，我们的研究揭示了线粒体-黑素体接触调控黑素体成熟的新机制。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Mitochondria form contact sites with multiple organelles to coordinate diverse cellular processes. Melanosomes, lysosome-related organelles, undergo stepwise maturation to synthesize and store melanin, but how they interact with mitochondria remains unclear. Here we show that mitochondria-melanosome contacts dynamically increase during melanosome maturation and are mediated by STIM1-MFN2 interactions. Using a NanoBiT-based reporter system, MiMSBiT (Mitochondria-Melanosome contact reporter applying NanoBiT), to monitor reversible mitochondria-melanosome contacts in living cells, we demonstrate that STIM1 localizes to melanosomes and promotes their contact with mitochondrial MFN2. A transient decrease in melanosomal lumen calcium induces STIM1 clustering and enhances its association with MFN2. These contacts locally increase mitochondrial ATP availability, leading to melanosome lumen acidification via proton channel activation. This acidification facilitates PMEL fibrillation, a key step in melanosome maturation. Together, our findings reveal a mechanism by which mitochondria-melanosome contacts regulate melanosome maturation.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: mitochondria-melanosome contacts, STIM1-MFN2 interactions, melanosome maturation, calcium signaling, ATP availability, lumen acidification, PMEL fibrillation, cellular organelle contacts

**作者**: Feng Li, Qikang Wu, Yan Zhou, Shanshan Lv, Jing Meng, Yongning Zhang, Sixin Dou, Yanyang Cheng, C. L. Philip Chen, Wenming Sun, Zheng Chen
