    该研究解决了电催化中单原子与团簇空间解耦阻碍协同作用的问题，通过设计纳米指纹碳锚定的Zn₁Fe₁ₓ/f-NC复合电催化剂，实现了优异的氧还原反应性能和锌空气电池的长期稳定性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 由单原子位点（M₁）与团簇（Mₓ）共同构成的杂化位点（M₁₊ₓ）在克服电催化中的线性标度关系方面具有巨大潜力，但M₁与Mₓ在空间上的分离从根本上阻碍了组分间的协同作用。本文报道了一种复合电催化剂（Zn₁Fe₁₊ₓ/f-NC），其特点是将Feₓ团簇封装在纳米指纹状碳层内，并被密集分散的Fe/Zn-N₄原子位点所环绕。解耦实验表明，Fe₁/Zn₁原子位点主要引发催化活性，而Feₓ团簇则进一步提升本征活性，同时纳米指纹碳层促进了M₁₊ₓ的限域与稳定。该Zn₁Fe₁₊ₓ/f-NC催化剂展现出优异的氧还原反应性能，其半波电位达到0.93 V，并保持超过50小时的稳定性。以Zn₁Fe₁₊ₓ/f-NC为空气阴极的锌-空气电池实现了263.82 mW·cm⁻²的峰值功率密度，并在10 mA cm⁻²电流密度下表现出超过2200小时的强健稳定性。密度泛函理论计算表明，原子级Zn位点、Feₓ团簇和纳米指纹碳层通过调控Fe-N₄位点的电子结构并优化关键中间体（尤其是OH*）的吸附能，共同提升了催化活性和稳定性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Hybrid sites (M<sub>1+x</sub>) that incorporate single atoms (M<sub>1</sub>) with clusters (M<sub>x</sub>) hold great potential for overcoming linear scaling relations in electrocatalysis, but spatial decoupling of M<sub>1</sub> from M<sub>x</sub> fundamentally hampers intercomponent synergy. Here, we report a composite electrocatalyst (Zn<sub>1</sub>Fe<sub>1+x</sub>/f-NC) featuring Fe<sub>x</sub> clusters encapsulated within nano-fingerprint carbon layers and surrounded by densely dispersed Fe/Zn-N<sub>4</sub> atomic sites. Decoupling experiments revealed that Fe<sub>1</sub>/Zn<sub>1</sub> atomic sites mainly initiate catalytic activity, while Fe<sub>x</sub> clusters further boost intrinsic activity, whereas nano-fingerprint carbon facilitates the confinement and stabilization of M<sub>1+x</sub>. The Zn<sub>1</sub>Fe<sub>1+x</sub>/f-NC demonstrates competitive oxygen reduction reaction performance, achieving a half-wave potential of 0.93 V and stability over 50 h. Zinc-air batteries with Zn<sub>1</sub>Fe<sub>1+x</sub>/f-NC air cathode exhibit a peak power density of 263.82 mW·cm<sup>-2</sup> and robust stability exceeding 2200 h at 10 mA cm<sup>-2</sup>. Density functional theory calculations reveal that the atomic Zn sites, Fe<sub>x</sub> clusters and nano-fingerprint carbon layers jointly enhance the catalytic activity and stability by modulating the electronic structure of Fe-N<sub>4</sub> sites and optimizing the adsorption energy of the key intermediate, especially OH*.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: electrocatalyst, oxygen reduction reaction, single-atom catalyst, metal clusters, nano-fingerprint carbon, zinc-air battery, density functional theory, activity-stability trade-off

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了复杂网络中社区结构如何影响节点对之间最短路径的多样性，发现社区结构是塑造路径多样性的关键因素，并提出了一个基于部落结构的网络模型来重现真实网络中的现象。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 具有复杂拓扑结构的网络描述了众多自然与社会系统。近期关于路径多重性的研究表明，现实网络节点对间最短路径存在显著异质性，但这一现象的内在机制尚未得到阐明。本文揭示出社区结构是塑造路径多重性的关键因素。为探究影响路径多重性的内在要素，我们首先引入相对路径多重性概念，发现社区结构与路径多重性的关联性强于其他网络度量指标。通过定向边重连实验，我们验证了路径多重性与社区结构之间的关联。其内在机制可解释为一种界面驱动效应，该效应会急剧增加最短路径的数量。受这些发现启发，我们提出一种基于部落结构的网络模型，该模型重现了现实网络中观察到的现象。本研究深化了对网络组织机制的理解，在网络设计与优化领域具有潜在应用价值。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Networks with complex topologies describe numerous natural and social systems. Recent studies on path multiplicity have shown strong heterogeneity in shortest paths between node pairs in real-world networks. However, the mechanism underlying this phenomenon remains unexplored. Here, we reveal that community structure is a key factor shaping path multiplicity. To explore the intrinsic factors that influence path multiplicity, we first introduce the concept of relative path multiplicity and find that community structure is more strongly correlated with path multiplicity than other network metrics. Through targeted edge-rewiring experiments, we verify the link between path multiplicity and community structure. The underlying mechanism can be interpreted as an interface-driven effect that sharply increases the number of shortest paths. Inspired by these findings, we propose a tribal-structure-based network model that reproduces phenomena observed in real-world networks. Our work enhances the understanding of network organization, with potential applications in network design and optimization.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: complex networks, community structure, path multiplicity, shortest paths, network topology, network model, edge-rewiring, tribal-structure

### 58. ❌ Magnon damping as a probe of Kondo coupling in magnetically ordered systems

**作者**: Song Bao, Yipeng Gao, Junsen Wang, Shin-ichiro Yano, Yanyan Shangguan, Zhentao Huang, Junbo Liao, Wei Wang, Bo Zhang, ShuFan Cheng, X. Q. Hao, Zhao-Yang Dong, Shunli Yu, Wei Li, Jian-Xin Li, Jun Li
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70241-5](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70241-5)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是凝聚态物理中的磁性系统，具体探讨Kondo耦合与磁有序的相互作用，使用中子散射研究自旋波（磁振子）阻尼。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析，而论文完全不涉及医学、生物医学或临床相关内容，属于完全不同的研究领域。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过中子散射测量金属范德华铁磁体Fe3-xGeTe2中磁振子的阻尼行为，发现其可作为探测Kondo耦合的有效探针，揭示了巡游电子与自旋波在磁性有序系统中的相互作用机制。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 在d电子体系中，近藤耦合与磁相互作用之间同样可能存在如f电子体系中那般复杂的相互影响，但其内在机制尚不明确。本文通过非弹性中子散射技术，研究了金属性范德华铁磁体Fe<sub>3-x</sub>GeTe<sub>2</sub>中低能自旋波（磁振子）的温度演化行为，观测到磁振子阻尼在低温和高温区均呈现发散趋势，并在中间温度出现极小值。这些行为可通过一个结合对数项与幂律项的公式进行描述，分别代表了近藤耦合（Kondo coupling）与热涨落的主导贡献。这些现象可以在铁磁近藤-海森堡晶格模型中，通过考虑自旋翻转型的电子-磁振子散射来得到解释，这与仅考虑巡游电子与局域杂质自旋间耦合的原始近藤效应有所不同。本研究揭示了具有磁有序的金属性3d电子体系中巡游电子与自旋波之间有趣的相互作用，并将磁振子阻尼发展为金属性量子磁体中近藤耦合的一种新型有效探针，从而为从磁振子视角探索近藤物理开辟了新途径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> In d-electron systems, there can also be intricate interplay between Kondo coupling and magnetic interactions as that in f-electron systems, but the underlying mechanism remains elusive. Here, using inelastic neutron scattering, we investigate the temperature evolution of the low-energy spin waves (magnons) in a metallic van der Waals ferromagnet Fe<sub>3-x</sub>GeTe<sub>2</sub>, and observe that the magnon damping diverges at both low and high temperatures and exhibits a minimum at an intermediate temperature. These behaviors are described by a formula that combines logarithmic and power-law terms, representing the dominant contributions from Kondo coupling and thermal fluctuations, respectively. These findings can be explained by considering electron-magnon scattering of spin-flip type within the ferromagnetic Kondo-Heisenberg lattice model, distinct from the original Kondo effect which only considers the coupling between itinerant electrons and isolated impurity spins. These results unveil the intriguing interplay between itinerant electrons and spin waves in metallic 3d-electron systems with magnetic order, and provide magnon damping as a new effective probe of Kondo coupling in metallic quantum magnets, thereby opening new avenues for exploring Kondo physics from the magnon perspective.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: magnon damping, Kondo coupling, ferromagnetic, inelastic neutron scattering, spin waves, itinerant electrons, van der Waals magnet, quantum magnets

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究评估了中国气候政策实施的不确定性对全球碳排放和气候变暖的影响，发现政策实施差异可能导致到2100年累计排放量相差约500 GtCO₂（约0.17°C变暖）。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 中国气候政策的实施具有重大的全球影响，然而政策目标与执行之间持续存在的差距引发了对其政策可信度的担忧。本研究对58项国家气候与能源政策（包括中国更新的2035年国家自主贡献）中的292个目标进行了结构化可信度评估。我们运用形态学情景框架，分析了政策不确定性与社会经济及技术驱动因素之间的相互作用，并将这些情景嵌入综合评估模型中，置于两种全球背景下：一种与当前国家自主贡献目标一致，另一种与全球净零排放雄心相符。研究发现，中国若能及时或加速实现其净零目标，可在本世纪中叶部分抵消其他地区减排雄心的不足。若到2050年全面实现政策目标，全球二氧化碳排放量将降至130亿吨，而无此类政策的情况下则为230亿吨。仅政策实施的不确定性就可能导致到2100年累计排放量相差约5000亿吨二氧化碳（约相当于0.17°C的全球变暖效应）。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The delivery of China's climate policy has substantial global implications, yet persistent gaps between policy targets and implementation raise concerns about policy credibility. This study presents a structured credibility assessment of 292 targets across 58 national climate and energy policies, including China's updated 2035 NDC. We apply a morphological scenario framework to examine interactions between policy uncertainty and socio-economic and technological drivers, embedding these scenarios in an integrated assessment model under two global contexts: one aligned with current NDCs and one consistent with global net-zero ambition. We find that timely or accelerated delivery of China's net-zero target could partially offset insufficient ambition elsewhere by mid-century. Full delivery by 2050 reduces global CO₂ emissions to 13 Gt, compared with 23 Gt without such policies. Policy delivery uncertainty alone could imply up to ~500 GtCO₂ difference in cumulative emissions by 2100 (~0.17 °C warming).

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: China's climate policy, policy credibility, uncertainty, global CO₂ emissions, integrated assessment model, net-zero target, morphological scenario framework, NDC

### 60. ❌ Upwind electromigration of sub-10-nm metallic nano-interconnects

**作者**: Youran Hong, Tianqi Deng, Xinwei Li, Zhongkang Han, Yì Wáng, Kexing Song, Ze Zhang, Yì Wáng
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70283-9](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70283-9)

| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究纳米级金属互连中的电迁移现象，属于纳米电子器件、材料科学和凝聚态物理领域。标题、摘要和内容均未涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像。论文关注的是电子器件可靠性、原子迁移机制和材料特性，与医学图像处理完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文揭示了在下一代过渡金属纳米互连中，表面原子逆电子流方向迁移的反常电迁移现象，挑战了传统电迁移理论，对优化极端工艺下电子互连的可靠性具有重要意义。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 纳米尺度电子器件在极端工作条件下面临关键可靠性挑战，其中由高密度电流驱动的电迁移——原子定向运动——会逐步导致金属组件性能退化。传统观点认为，在金属互连线中，电子风力驱动原子沿电子流动方向迁移。然而，通过采用集成的原位纳米加工-电脉冲技术，我们在原子尺度上揭示了下一代过渡金属纳米互连线中的反常电迁移现象：表面原子逆着电子流动方向迁移。这种“逆流迁移”在不同难熔金属纳米互连线（包括钨和钼）中表现出普适性。第一性原理计算表明，这种迁移方向的逆转源于具有复杂电子结构的材料中直接力对电子风力的主导作用。我们的发现挑战了现有电迁移理论范式，并对面向极端工艺的下一代电子互连可靠性优化具有重要启示。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Nanoscale electronic devices face critical reliability challenges under extreme operating conditions, where electromigration-atomic motion driven by high density current-progressively degrades metallic components. Conventional wisdom maintains that electron wind force drives atomic migration along electron flow direction in metallic interconnects. However, using an integrated in situ nanofabrication-electropulsing approach, we reveal an anomalous electromigration phenomenon in next-generation transition metal nano-interconnects at atomic scale, where surface atoms migrate against the direction of electron flow. This upwind migration demonstrates universality across different refractory nano-interconnects including tungsten and molybdenum. First-principles calculations attribute this reversal to the predominance of direct forces over electron wind forces in materials with complex electronic structures. Our findings challenge the existing paradigm of electromigration and hold great implications for optimizing the reliability of next-generation electronic interconnections toward extreme process.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: electromigration, nano-interconnects, atomic migration, transition metals, electron wind force, reliability, in situ nanofabrication, first-principles calculations

### 61. ❌ Bipartite entanglement in a nuclear spin register mediated by a quasi-free electron spin

**作者**: Marco Klotz, Andreas Tangemann, David Opferkuch, Alexander Kubanek
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**arXiv链接**: [https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.05255](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.05255)
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70154-3](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70154-3)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是量子网络、核自旋寄存器、硅空位中心和量子纠缠，属于量子物理和量子计算领域。所有评分关键词（medical image analysis, medical imaging, deep learning medical imaging）均与医学图像分析相关，而论文内容完全不涉及医学图像、医学成像或深度学习在医学成像中的应用，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了在金刚石中利用硅空位中心的准自由电子自旋介导三量子比特核自旋寄存器的控制和纠缠，实现了核自旋条件相位门以产生二分纠缠，为光学可访问的固态量子寄存器提供了新途径。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子网络将依赖于与稳健的局部量子寄存器纠缠的光子，以实现计算和纠错。我们在金刚石中一个全连接的三量子比特<sup>13</sup>C核自旋寄存器中实现了控制和纠缠。该寄存器与硅空位中心（SiV）的一个准自由电子自旋-1/2耦合。高应变使SiV的电子自旋与自旋-轨道相互作用解耦，从而降低了其在液氦温度下对声子的敏感性。因此，长达数百毫秒的电子自旋寿命使得对低至几赫兹的核间耦合进行探测成为可能。为了探测和控制该寄存器，我们利用整形低功率微波和直接射频驱动进行连续解耦。此外，我们在电子自旋上实现了一个核自旋条件相位门，以介导双体纠缠。这种方法为动态解耦核自旋纠缠提供了一种替代方案，不受电子自旋-1/2性质的限制，为构建光学可访问的固态量子寄存器开辟了新途径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum networks will rely on photons entangled to robust, local quantum registers for computation and error correction. We demonstrate control of and entanglement in a fully connected three-qubit <sup>13</sup>C nuclear spin register in diamond. The register is coupled to a quasi-free electron spin-1/2 of a silicon-vacancy center (SiV). High strain decouples the SiVs electron spin from spin-orbit interaction reducing the susceptibility to phonons at liquid helium temperature. As a result, the electron spin lifetime of hundreds of milli seconds enables sensing of nuclear-nuclear couplings down to few hertz. To detect and control the register we leverage continuous decoupling using shaped, low-power microwave and direct radio frequency driving. Furthermore, we implement a nuclear spin conditional phase-gate on the electron spin to mediate bipartite entanglement. This approach presents an alternative to dynamically decoupled nuclear spin entanglement, not limited by the electron spin-1/2's nature, opening up new avenues to an optically-accessible, solid-state quantum register.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum networks, nuclear spin register, silicon-vacancy center, quantum entanglement, solid-state quantum register, electron spin, conditional phase-gate, diamond

### 62. ❌ USP7 deubiquitinase stabilizes FAN1 to support DNA crosslink repair and suppress CAG repeat expansion

**作者**: Giulio Collotta, Marco Gatti, Irina-Maria Ungureanu, Vanessa van Ackeren, Emilie Rannou, Francesca Vivalda, Diego Gomez Vieito, Keri M. Fishwick, Christine von Aesch, Antônio Porro, Kyra Ungerleider, Ailin Heidari, Raphaël Guérois, Rachel J. Harding, Sylvain Bischof, Gabriel Balmus, Alessandro A. Sartori
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70051-9](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70051-9)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是DNA修复、泛素化调控和亨廷顿病相关的CAG重复序列扩展的分子机制，涉及USP7去泛素化酶稳定FAN1蛋白、DNA交联修复和基因组稳定性。所有评分关键词（medical image analysis, medical imaging, deep learning medical imaging）均与医学影像分析直接相关，而论文内容完全属于分子生物学、细胞生物学和遗传学领域，未涉及任何医学影像技术、分析或应用，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究发现USP7去泛素化酶通过稳定FAN1蛋白来促进DNA交联修复并抑制亨廷顿病相关的CAG重复序列扩展。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 人类FAN1是一种结构特异性核酸内切酶，参与DNA链间交联（ICLs）的修复以及螺旋外CAG重复序列的切除——该序列的病理性扩增是亨廷顿病（HD）的分子基础，HD是一种进行性且目前无法治愈的神经退行性疾病。然而，FAN1的翻译后调控机制在很大程度上仍属未知。本研究鉴定出泛素特异性蛋白酶7（USP7）是FAN1的相互作用蛋白。USP7以去泛素化依赖的方式稳定FAN1蛋白水平，防止其发生蛋白酶体降解。由此，我们证明USP7的缺失会导致FAN1在染色质上的结合减少，并在ICL损伤后加剧细胞的超敏反应。此外，在稳定表达含有129个CAG重复序列的突变亨廷顿蛋白（mHTT）外显子1的RPE-1细胞模型（RPE-1<sup>HTT-CAG129</sup>）中，USP7的缺失会加速CAG重复序列的扩增。总之，我们的研究结果揭示了USP7与FAN1在维持基因组稳定性和影响重复序列不稳定性机制中的关联。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Human FAN1 is a structure-specific endonuclease implicated in the repair of DNA interstrand crosslinks (ICLs) and the excision of extrahelical CAG repeats-whose pathological expansion underlies Huntington's disease (HD), a progressive and currently incurable neurodegenerative disorder. However, mechanisms of post-translational regulation of FAN1 are still largely unknown. Here, we identify the ubiquitin-specific protease 7 (USP7) as an interactor of FAN1. USP7 stabilizes FAN1 protein levels in a deubiquitination-dependent manner, preventing FAN1 from proteasomal degradation. Consequently, we demonstrate that USP7 depletion leads to reduced chromatin association of FAN1 and increased cellular hypersensitivity following ICL damage. Moreover, loss of USP7 accelerates CAG repeat expansion in an RPE-1 cell model stably expressing mutant huntingtin (mHTT) exon 1 containing 129 CAG repeats (RPE-1<sup>HTT-CAG129</sup>). Collectively, our findings uncover a link between USP7 and FAN1 in mechanisms that preserve genome stability and influence repeat instability.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: USP7, FAN1, DNA interstrand crosslink repair, deubiquitination, CAG repeat expansion, Huntington's disease, genome stability, proteasomal degradation

### 63. ❌ The natural flavonoid dihydromyricetin targets senescent cells via PRDX2 and alleviates age-related diseases

**作者**: Qixia Xu, Gaoxiang Li, Heng Zhang, Zhirui Jiang, Xiuxia Gao, Zi Li, Larissa Langhi Prata, James L. Kirkland, Guilong Zhang, Yu Sun
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70302-9](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70302-9)

| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是天然黄酮类化合物二氢杨梅素通过靶向衰老细胞来缓解年龄相关疾病（如癌症和阿尔茨海默病）的机制，属于细胞生物学、衰老研究和药物发现领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像技术，没有使用任何图像数据或成像方法，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    In mice developing Alzheimer's disease, dihydromyricetin eliminates senescent microglial cells from amyloid β-protein plaques and alleviates neurodegenerative symptoms, and dihydromyricetin is proposed as a natural senotherapeutic agent for mitigating age-related morbidities.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究发现天然黄酮类化合物二氢杨梅素通过靶向PRDX2蛋白清除衰老细胞，能够缓解组织衰老、改善化疗效果并减轻阿尔茨海默病症状。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 衰老是慢性疾病的主要风险因素，细胞衰老是延缓、预防或减轻年龄相关疾病的有效干预靶点。本研究报道了天然药物库的体外筛选结果，其中天然黄酮类化合物二氢杨梅素展现出衰老治疗潜力。二氢杨梅素能保护衰老成纤维细胞免受进一步DNA损伤，并减弱衰老相关分泌表型，发挥衰老形态调节剂作用。蛋白质组学分析表明，二氢杨梅素通过促进过氧化物还原酶2（peroxiredoxin 2, PRDX2）的核转位来增强衰老细胞的DNA修复能力。在早衰小鼠模型中，二氢杨梅素给药能缓解组织衰老和年龄相关的生理功能衰退。在抗癌治疗方案中，二氢杨梅素可改善化疗效果。值得注意的是，该化合物对基础PRDX2表达水平持续低下的衰老小胶质细胞表现出衰老清除活性，通过破坏线粒体功能促进细胞凋亡。在阿尔茨海默病模型小鼠中，二氢杨梅素能清除β淀粉样蛋白斑块中的衰老小胶质细胞，并减轻神经退行性症状。综上，本研究提出二氢杨梅素作为一种天然衰老治疗剂，可用于缓解包括癌症和阿尔茨海默病在内的年龄相关疾病。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Aging is a primary risk factor for chronic diseases, with cellular senescence as an effective target to delay, prevent or alleviate age-related disorders. Here we report in vitro screening outputs from a natural medicinal agent library, wherein dihydromyricetin, a natural flavonoid, showed senotherapeutic potential. Dihydromyricetin protects senescent fibroblasts against further DNA damage and attenuates the senescence-associated secretory phenotype, acting as a senomorphic agent. Proteomics suggests that dihydromyricetin promotes nuclear translocation of peroxiredoxin 2 (PRDX2) to facilitate DNA repair in senescent cells. In prematurely aged mice, dihydromyricetin administration mitigates tissue aging and age-related physiological decline. In anticancer regimens, dihydromyricetin improves outcomes of chemotherapy. However, dihydromyricetin demonstrates senolytic activity against senescent microglial cells, whose basal PRDX2 expression remains low, by impairing mitochondrial function to promote apoptosis. In mice developing Alzheimer's disease, dihydromyricetin eliminates senescent microglial cells from amyloid β-protein plaques and alleviates neurodegenerative symptoms. Together, our study proposes dihydromyricetin as a natural senotherapeutic agent for mitigating age-related morbidities, including but not limited to cancers and Alzheimer's disease.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: dihydromyricetin, senescent cells, PRDX2, age-related diseases, Alzheimer's disease, senotherapeutic agent, cellular senescence, DNA repair

### 64. ❌ Native chromatome profiling reveals hundreds of metabolic enzymes in the nucleus across tissues

**作者**: S. Kourtis, A. Gañez Zapater, CR Elbæk, Alisa Schmidt, R. Ghose, A. Coll Manzano, L. Espinar Calvo, María Guirola, N. Pardo-Lorente, M. Garcia-Cao, Matilda Pfeiffer, S. Haynes, F. Fontaine, André C. Müller, Sara Sdelci
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-69217-2](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-69217-2)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是代谢酶在细胞核中的定位及其在染色质调控和癌症中的作用，通过色谱组蛋白质组学分析揭示代谢酶在染色质上的广泛存在。研究内容完全聚焦于分子生物学、代谢组学和癌症生物学领域，未涉及任何医学影像分析、医学成像或深度学习在医学影像中的应用。所有关键词与论文主题无直接关联。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    The hypothesis that the nucleus is populated by metabolic enzymes is underscores, offering new avenues for understanding how nuclear metabolism impacts chromatin function and cancer progression, and proposes and validate novel non-canonical nuclear roles for several metabolic enzymes.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过色谱组蛋白质组学分析揭示了代谢酶在细胞核染色质上的广泛存在及其组织特异性，验证了代谢酶在DNA损伤修复和转录调控中的非经典核功能，为理解核代谢如何影响染色质功能和癌症进展提供了新见解。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 代谢重编程与表观遗传重塑是癌症的典型特征，越来越多的证据表明这两个过程之间存在交互作用。尽管先前研究已暗示代谢酶在细胞核内的作用，但其核定位的程度及功能相关性仍不明确。本研究通过跨癌谱系与健康样本的全面染色质组蛋白质组学分析，揭示代谢酶在染色质上的兼职现象广泛存在于多种组织及代谢通路中。我们发现染色质上代谢酶的丰度具有组织特异性，其中氧化磷酸化蛋白在肺癌中显著缺失，这提示核内代谢与细胞身份之间存在关联。进一步，我们探究了一碳叶酸代谢酶的动态染色质结合行为，证明其参与DNA损伤与修复过程。最后，我们通过限制代谢酶于特定亚细胞区室，探究其是否重构转录组，从而将观察到的转录变化与单纯的代谢物扩散效应解耦。我们的研究提出并验证了多种代谢酶的非经典核功能，为理解代谢与染色质调控之间的功能关系提供了新视角。此项工作进一步佐证了“细胞核内存在代谢酶群”的假说，为探索核内代谢如何影响染色质功能及癌症进展开辟了新途径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Metabolic and epigenetic rewiring are hallmarks of cancer, with increasing evidence suggesting crosstalk between these processes. While previous studies have hinted at the role of metabolic enzymes in the nucleus, the extent and functional relevance of their nuclear localization remain unclear. In this study, we present a comprehensive chromatome proteomic analysis across cancer lineages and healthy samples, revealing that metabolic enzyme moonlighting on chromatin is widespread across various tissues and metabolic pathways. We show that the abundance of metabolic enzymes on chromatin is tissue-specific, with oxidative phosphorylation proteins notably depleted in lung cancer, suggesting a link between nuclear metabolism and cell identity. Further, we explore the dynamic chromatin association of one-carbon folate enzymes, demonstrating their involvement in DNA damage and repair processes. Finally, we asked whether restricting metabolic enzymes to specific subcellular compartments rewires the transcriptome, thereby decoupling the observed transcriptional changes from mere metabolite diffusion. Our findings propose and validate novel non-canonical nuclear roles for several metabolic enzymes, providing new insights into the functional relationship between metabolism and chromatin regulation. This study underscores the hypothesis that the nucleus is populated by metabolic enzymes, offering new avenues for understanding how nuclear metabolism impacts chromatin function and cancer progression.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: chromatome proteomic analysis, metabolic enzymes, nuclear localization, chromatin regulation, cancer progression, DNA damage repair, tissue-specific, metabolic rewiring

### 65. ❌ CPF-CF-terminated snoRNAs shuttle through the cytoplasm via an mRNA guard protein-mediated surveillance mechanism

**作者**: Fei Yu, Gianluca Zaccagnini, Yawen Duan, Jan-Phillip Lamping, Sophie Tagnères, Katherine E. Bohnsack, Heike Krebber
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70373-8](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70373-8)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是酵母中snoRNA的转录终止模式如何通过保护蛋白机制决定其核质穿梭，属于分子生物学和细胞生物学领域，与医学影像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学影像完全无关。论文内容涉及RNA转录、核质运输、蛋白质复合物等，没有任何医学影像相关的内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    This work identified Mex67 and Xpo1 as snoRNP export receptors, and Mtr10 and Cse1 as their re-import factors, and identified that transcription termination mode determines snoRNA export through a guard protein-controlled mechanism.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究发现酵母中snoRNA的转录终止模式（CPF-CF终止而非NNS终止）通过保护蛋白Hrp1和Nab2介导Mex67-Mtr2依赖的核输出，决定了snoRNA能否穿梭到细胞质并形成功能性snoRNP。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 虽然指导核糖体RNA修饰的小核仁RNA主要在细胞核内合成并发挥功能，但部分小核仁RNA可在细胞质中被检测到。本研究鉴定出Mex67与Xpo1作为小核仁核糖核蛋白复合体的输出受体，Mtr10和Cse1则作为其再输入因子。值得注意的是，仅部分小核仁RNA存在穿梭现象，我们揭示其转录终止方式决定了小核仁RNA是否被输出。在酿酒酵母中，RNA聚合酶II转录的RNA可通过Nrd1-Nab3-Sen1复合体或剪切与多聚腺苷酸化因子复合体两种途径终止。主要作用于小核仁RNA的NNS终止方式会导致核内滞留；反之，作为保险机制的CPF-CF终止方式会引起转录本多聚腺苷酸化，随后结合监护蛋白Hrp1与Nab2，进而介导Mex67-Mtr2依赖的输出途径。重要的是，经再输入的CPF-CF终止型小核仁RNA能形成具有功能的小核仁核糖核蛋白复合体。本研究共同揭示了转录终止模式通过监护蛋白调控机制决定小核仁RNA输出的分子路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Although small nucleolar (sno)RNAs, which guide ribosomal (r)RNA modification, are synthesized and function in the nucleus, some of them can be detected in the cytoplasm. Here, we identify Mex67 and Xpo1 as snoRNP export receptors, and Mtr10 and Cse1 as their re-import factors. Interestingly, only a fraction of snoRNAs shuttle, and we reveal that the mode of transcription determines whether or not the snoRNA is exported. In Saccharomyces cerevisiae, RNA polymerase II-transcribed RNAs are terminated either via the Nrd1-Nab3-Sen1 (NNS) complex or the cleavage and polyadenylation factor (CPF-CF) complex. NNS termination, which mostly occurs for snoRNAs, leads to nuclear retention. Conversely, fail-safe CPF-CF termination results in transcript polyadenylation and subsequent association of the guard proteins Hrp1 and Nab2, which in turn mediate Mex67-Mtr2 dependent export. Importantly, re-imported CPF-CF-terminated snoRNAs form functional snoRNPs. Together, we identified that transcription termination mode determines snoRNA export through a guard protein-controlled mechanism.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: snoRNA, transcription termination, nuclear export, Mex67, guard proteins, CPF-CF, NNS, snoRNP

### 66. ❌ Tudor domain-containing protein 9-targeting siRNA nanoparticles alleviate Pseudomonas aeruginosa lung injury in preclinical models by promoting neutrophil cuproptosis

**作者**: Wen Zhang, Hui Li, Huayun Jia, Weixia Xuan, Lisha Ding, Xi Zeng, Qian Wu, Meiyun Zhao, Xu Wu
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06

|------|------|------|------|

| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是使用siRNA纳米颗粒靶向TDRD9蛋白来治疗铜绿假单胞菌引起的肺损伤，通过促进中性粒细胞铜死亡机制。全文聚焦于分子生物学、纳米药物递送、免疫治疗和肺部疾病模型，未涉及任何医学影像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像技术。论文中未使用或提及影像数据采集、处理、分析或相关算法。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    This work demonstrates that targeting TDRD9 with siRNA nanoparticle platform presents a promising therapeutic strategy for treating bacterial lung injury.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究开发了一种靶向TDRD9的siRNA纳米颗粒，通过促进中性粒细胞铜死亡来减轻铜绿假单胞菌引起的肺损伤，并在临床前模型中验证了其治疗效果。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 铜绿假单胞菌肺炎构成显著的治疗挑战。纳米颗粒作为核酸递送的有效工具，能够高效缓解肺炎。本研究开发了一种透明质酸（HA）包被的肽纳米颗粒系统，用于靶向递送针对含Tudor结构域蛋白9（TDRD9）的小干扰RNA（siRNA）；该靶点是通过对21例招募患者（11名男性/10名女性）的支气管肺泡灌洗液来源中性粒细胞进行RNA测序所鉴定。将TDRD9沉默的多形核中性粒细胞过继转移至中性粒细胞耗竭的雄性小鼠体内，可减轻肺部炎症和水肿。机制上，TDRD9通过与CD80相互作用激活p38丝裂原活化蛋白激酶（MAPK）信号通路，上调程序性死亡配体1（PD-L1），从而抑制中性粒细胞的铜死亡。HA-si-TDRD9纳米颗粒通过PD-L1/CD80/MAPK轴增强中性粒细胞铜死亡，减少肺中性粒细胞积聚，并改善肺损伤。重要的是，HA-si-TDRD9纳米颗粒能减少人肺类器官中的细菌生长、细胞凋亡和炎症反应。本研究表明，利用siRNA纳米颗粒平台靶向TDRD9为治疗细菌性肺损伤提供了一种前景广阔的治疗策略。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Pseudomonas aeruginosa pneumonia poses a significant therapeutic challenge. Nanoparticles serve as an effective tool for nucleic acid delivery to efficiently alleviate pneumonia. This study develops a hyaluronic acid (HA)-coated peptide nanoparticle system for targeted delivery of small interfering RNA (siRNA) against Tudor domain-containing protein 9 (TDRD9), identified via RNA sequencing of bronchoalveolar lavage fluid-derived neutrophils from 21 recruited patients (11 males/10 females). Adoptive transfer of TDRD9-silenced polymorphonuclear neutrophils into neutrophil-depleted male mice attenuates lung inflammation and edema. Mechanistically, TDRD9 suppresses neutrophil cuproptosis by upregulating programmed death ligand 1 (PD-L1) through interaction with CD80 to activate p38 mitogen-activated protein kinase (MAPK) signaling. HA-si-TDRD9 nanoparticles enhance neutrophil cuproptosis, reduce pulmonary neutrophil accumulation, and ameliorate lung injury via PD-L1/CD80/MAPK. Importantly, HA-si-TDRD9 nanoparticles reduce bacterial growth, apoptosis, and inflammation in human lung organoids. This work demonstrates that targeting TDRD9 with siRNA nanoparticle platform presents a promising therapeutic strategy for treating bacterial lung injury.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: siRNA nanoparticles, TDRD9, neutrophil cuproptosis, Pseudomonas aeruginosa pneumonia, lung injury, PD-L1/CD80/MAPK pathway, hyaluronic acid coating, human lung organoids

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是基因调控、染色质重塑、组蛋白变体H2A.Z和SRCAP蛋白在干细胞中的功能，属于分子生物学和表观遗传学领域。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析，而论文完全不涉及任何医学影像、图像处理或深度学习在医学影像中的应用，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    This study establishes the catalytic-independent role of a chromatin remodeler in broadly regulating transcription factor binding, and demonstrates how a chromatin remodeler-histone variant pair orchestrates transcription to maintain self-renewal and plasticity of pluripotent stem cells.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    本研究通过急性降解SRCAP和构建突变体，揭示了染色质重塑复合物SRCAP及其沉积的组蛋白变体H2A.Z在干细胞基因调控中的独立功能：SRCAP通过空间位阻抑制转录因子结合，而H2A.Z主要作为谱系特异性基因的转录抑制因子。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 区分染色质组成的调控功能与染色质修饰复合物的功能是基因调控领域的核心问题。这一问题在组蛋白变体及其专用染色质重塑因子的背景下尚未得到探索。本研究解析了多能干细胞基因调控中Snf2相关CREBBP激活蛋白（SRCAP）与H2A.Z所具有的独特且依赖细胞周期的功能。通过对内源性SRCAP进行快速降解，我们揭示了H2A.Z占据的动态变化以及SRCAP在整个细胞周期中的持续需求。我们还构建了一种H2A.Z沉积功能缺陷的SRCAP突变体，从而得以区分SRCAP依赖H2A.Z与不依赖H2A.Z的功能。研究发现，SRCAP通过空间位阻作用，在抑制数十种先锋转录因子与增强子的DNA结合方面表现出不依赖H2A.Z的关键功能。相比之下，H2A.Z主要作为转录抑制因子，调控谱系特异性基因的表达。本研究确立了一种染色质重塑因子以非催化方式广泛调控转录因子结合的机制，并阐明了染色质重塑因子-组蛋白变体配对如何协同调控转录，以维持多能干细胞的自我更新与可塑性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Discriminating regulatory functions of chromatin composition from those of chromatin-modifying complexes is a central problem in gene regulation. This question remains unexplored in the context of histone variants and their dedicated chromatin remodelers. Here we dissect the distinct and cell cycle-dependent functions of Snf2 Related CREBBP Activator Protein (SRCAP) and H2A.Z in gene regulation of pluripotent stem cells. Using acute degradation of endogenous SRCAP, we uncover dynamic changes of H2A.Z occupancy and continuous requirement of SRCAP over the cell cycle. We also engineered an SRCAP mutant, defective for H2A.Z deposition, allowing us to distinguish H2A.Z-dependent and independent functions of SRCAP. We discover that SRCAP exhibits essential H2A.Z-independent functions in inhibiting DNA binding of dozens of pioneer transcription factors at enhancers by steric hindrance. In contrast, H2A.Z acts mainly as a transcriptional repressor gatekeeping the expression of lineage-specific genes. Our study establishes the catalytic-independent role of a chromatin remodeler in broadly regulating transcription factor binding, and demonstrates how a chromatin remodeler-histone variant pair orchestrates transcription to maintain self-renewal and plasticity of pluripotent stem cells.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: SRCAP, H2A.Z, chromatin remodeling, gene regulation, pluripotent stem cells, transcription factor binding, histone variant, epigenetics

### 69. ❌ The oncogenic CCDC6-RET fusion protein is a dual ATP- and ADP-dependent kinase

**作者**: Ana Martín-Hurtado, Julia Contreras, Jana Sánchez-Wandelmer, Eduardo Zarzuela, Hiroyuki Fukuda, Johanne Le Coq, Jasminka Boskovic, Inés G. Muñoz, Federico Gago, Javier Muñoz, Marta Isasa, Iván Plaza-Menacho
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-69833-y](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-69833-y)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是CCDC6-RET融合蛋白的结构、功能和分子机制，属于癌症生物学、结构生物学和分子生物学领域。论文使用质谱、生物化学、生物物理、电子显微镜、X射线散射和分子动力学模拟等方法，但完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像。论文内容与所有评分关键词完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    It is shown that a CCDC6-RET fusion protein, a driver and therapeutic target in lung and thyroid cancers, is a highly active dimeric kinase able to bind both nucleotides and to use them as phosphoryl donors.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究揭示了驱动肺癌和甲状腺癌的CCDC6-RET融合蛋白是一种双ATP-和ADP依赖性激酶，通过结构模型阐明了其自激活的分子机制。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 涉及蛋白激酶的基因融合产物是已知的人类癌症驱动因子及个体化治疗的作用靶点，然而控制其功能的结构与分子决定因素在很大程度上尚未被探索。本文研究表明，CCDC6-RET融合蛋白（作为肺癌和甲状腺癌的驱动因子及治疗靶点）是一种高活性的二聚体激酶。通过时间分辨质谱结合稳健的生物化学与生物物理学表征，我们发现CCDC6-RET能够作为同时依赖ATP和ADP的双功能激酶，可结合这两种核苷酸并将其用作磷酸基团供体。我们还发现其C末端与激活段之间存在交互作用，共同调控融合蛋白的加工过程与催化活性。此外，我们结合单颗粒电子显微镜、小角X射线散射及计算机分子动力学模拟，构建了CCDC6-RET同源二聚体的三维结构组装模型。我们的结构模型与交联质谱数据共同表明，处于非活性状态的CCDC6-RET会形成一种面对面二聚体，其特征是激活段之间存在分子间交联。当核苷酸结合后，催化结构域会发生摆动分离，其激活环的快速磷酸化可能由顺式机制驱动。本研究揭示了控制CCDC6-RET自激活机制的分子与结构决定因素。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Gene fusion products involving protein kinases are known drivers in human cancers and actionable targets for personalized therapy, yet the structural and molecular determinants that control their function are largely unexplored. Here we show that a CCDC6-RET fusion protein, a driver and therapeutic target in lung and thyroid cancers, is a highly active dimeric kinase. Time-resolved mass spectrometry together with a robust biochemical and biophysical characterization reveal that CCDC6-RET functions as a dual ATP- and ADP-dependent kinase able to bind both nucleotides and to use them as phosphoryl donors. We also identify a crosstalk between the C-terminal and the activation segments controlling both the processing and the catalytic activity of the fusion protein. Furthermore, a 3D-structural assembly of a CCDC6-RET homodimer was generated combining single particle electron microscopy, small-angle X-ray scattering and in silico molecular dynamics simulations. Our structural model together with cross-linking mass spectrometry data demonstrated that CCDC6-RET in the inactive state forms a face-to-face dimer characterized by intermolecular-crosslinked activation segments. Upon nucleotide binding the catalytic domains swing apart and fast activation loop phosphorylation could be driven by a mechanism in cis. Our work uncovers the molecular and structural determinants that control the mechanism of CCDC6-RET autoactivation.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: CCDC6-RET fusion protein, dual ATP- and ADP-dependent kinase, cancer driver, structural biology, molecular mechanism, autoactivation, dimeric kinase, therapeutic target

### 70. ❌ Tumor-induced orexigenic imbalance lowers protein appetite and drives early organ wasting symptoms

**作者**: Afroditi Petsakou, Elizabeth Filine, Matthew Li, Yuchen Chen, Alice Zheng, Norbert Perrimon
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70074-2](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70074-2)

<details>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |

| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究癌症恶病质的早期机制，使用果蝇肠道肿瘤模型，通过分子生物学方法（如炎症因子、胰岛素信号通路、神经肽分析）研究肿瘤如何导致食欲减退和器官消耗。全文未涉及医学影像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像的任何内容，完全属于基础生物学和癌症机制研究领域。

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究使用果蝇模型发现，肿瘤通过炎症因子和胰岛素信号通路降低大脑神经肽NPF水平，导致早期蛋白质食欲减退，从而驱动器官消耗和体重下降的起始。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 癌症恶病质（CC）的特征是器官消耗及随之发生的非自主性体重下降。尽管研究有所进展，但引发CC的潜在机制仍不明确，包括厌食等早期症状。本研究利用果蝇肠道肿瘤模型，在器官消耗开始前设定精确的时间窗口。我们发现，在器官消耗发生前，肿瘤诱导的炎症相关因子（unpaired 3/类白细胞介素-6）及胰岛素信号减弱因子（ImpL2/胰岛素样生长因子结合蛋白）会降低大脑中的NPF（神经肽F/神经肽Y）。这种早期的NPF下降会引发低蛋白质特异性食欲和厌食。我们发现ImpL2会减弱NPF信号，而upd3则通过同时影响血脑屏障发挥作用。肿瘤诱导的NPF下降及早期蛋白质食欲降低，共同驱动体重下降的发生，并加剧器官消耗期间的死亡风险。总之，我们证明了早期促食欲大脑失衡导致低蛋白质食欲，从而调控器官消耗的发生与结局。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Cancer cachexia (CC) is characterized by organ wasting and ensuing involuntary weight loss. Despite advances, underlying mechanisms initiating CC remain unclear, including early symptoms like anorexia. Here, we use a fly gut-tumor model with a precise time-window before organ wasting starts. We show that tumor-induced factors involved in inflammation (unpaired 3/ Interleukin-6-like) and reduced insulin signaling (ImpL2/ Insulin Growth Factor Binding Protein) decrease NPF (Neuropeptide F/ Neuropeptide Y) in the brain prior to organ wasting. This early NPF decrease triggers low protein-specific food appetite and anorexia. We find that ImpL2 reduces NPF signaling while upd3 helps by concurrently affecting the blood brain barrier. Tumor-induced NPF decrease, and early reduction of protein appetite drive the onset of weight loss and exacerbate the risk of death during organ wasting. Altogether, we provide evidence for an early orexigenic brain imbalance causing low protein appetite that regulates the onset and outcome of organ wasting.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: cancer cachexia, organ wasting, tumor-induced anorexia, NPF/Neuropeptide F, insulin signaling, inflammation, protein appetite, Drosophila model

### 71. ❌ Mechanisms of PfDNMT2 inhibition and PfATP6-mediated resistance to the antimalarial candidate SC83288 in Plasmodium falciparum

**作者**: Cecília P. Sanchez, Maëlle Duffey, Romina V. Celada, Michal Kucharski, Marie Hoarau, Thanaya Saeyang, Sumalee Kamchonwongpaisan, Farzin Sohraby, Svenja de Buhr, Ariane Nunes Alves, Amuza Byaruhanga Lucky, Jun Miao, Clément Regnault, Jerzy M. Dziekan, Zbynek Bozdech, Michael P. Barrett, Michael Lanzer
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70280-y](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70280-y)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是疟疾寄生虫（Plasmodium falciparum）的抗疟药物SC83288的作用机制和耐药性，涉及分子生物学、遗传学和药理学领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像，这些关键词与论文主题无任何关联。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    It is shown that SC83288 disrupts blood-stage development by blocking DNA replication and arresting karyokinesis, and target validation, a unique resistance profile, and high fitness cost strengthen SC83288's potential as a promising clinical development candidate for malaria treatment.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了抗疟候选药物SC83288通过抑制PfDNMT2阻断疟原虫DNA复制的作用机制，并发现PfATP6突变导致药物耐药性但伴随适应性代价，验证了SC83288作为疟疾治疗候选药物的潜力。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 多重耐药恶性疟原虫的出现凸显了对新型抗疟疗法的迫切需求。SC83288是一种化学结构独特的抗疟化合物，在体内和体外均对恶性疟原虫表现出高效活性，包括对青蒿素及其联合用药耐药的虫株。本研究表明，SC83288通过阻断DNA复制和抑制核分裂，破坏疟原虫血液期的发育。我们鉴定出寄生虫的DNA和tRNA<sup>Asp</sup>甲基转移酶PfDNMT2为其主要分子靶点，将药物作用与受损的表观遗传调控、改变的S-腺苷甲硫氨酸通量以及代偿性转录反应联系起来。对SC83288的耐药性源于寄生虫SERCA型Ca²⁺ ATP酶PfATP6的突变，该突变使得化合物能被转运至内质网，从而远离其细胞核内的靶点。这种耐药机制伴随着显著的适应性代价，限制了其传播潜力。综上所述，明确的靶点验证、独特的耐药特性以及高昂的适应性代价，共同增强了SC83288作为疟疾治疗临床开发候选药物的潜力。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The emergence of multi-drug resistant Plasmodium falciparum underscores the urgent need for new antimalarial therapies. SC83288, a chemically distinct antimalarial compound, is highly effective against P. falciparum both in vivo and in vitro, including strains resistant to artemisinin and partner drugs. Here, we show that SC83288 disrupts blood-stage development by blocking DNA replication and arresting karyokinesis. We identify the parasite's DNA and tRNA<sup>Asp</sup> methyltransferase PfDNMT2 as a primary molecular target, linking drug action to impaired epigenetic regulation, altered S-adenosylmethionine fluxes, and compensatory transcriptional responses. Resistance to SC83288 arises through mutations in the parasite's SERCA-type Ca²⁺ ATPase PfATP6, which enable transport of the compound into the endoplasmic reticulum, away from its nuclear targets. This resistance mechanism carries a substantial fitness cost, limiting its potential for spread. Together, target validation, a unique resistance profile, and high fitness cost strengthen SC83288's potential as a promising clinical development candidate for malaria treatment.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Plasmodium falciparum, antimalarial drug, SC83288, PfDNMT2, PfATP6, drug resistance, DNA replication, malaria treatment

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    The role of disrupted keratin biology, skin barrier defects, immune dysfunction, immune dysfunction, and obesity in dermatophytosis risk is highlighted, and genetic overlap with other skin conditions and obesity-related traits is observed, providing insights into disease mechanisms and potential targets for prevention and treatment.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过大规模全基因组关联分析揭示了皮肤真菌感染（dermatophytosis）的遗传基础，识别了30个全基因组显著位点，并发现疾病风险与角质生物学、皮肤屏障缺陷、免疫功能障碍和肥胖相关。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 皮肤癣菌病是一种影响皮肤、指甲和毛发等角质化组织的真菌感染，临床表现为红色瘙痒斑块、指甲增厚或脱发。该病影响全球约20%的人口，但其遗传结构仍不甚明晰。我们对来自FinnGen、爱沙尼亚生物样本库、英国生物样本库及百万退伍军人计划的超过25万病例和137万对照进行了全基因组关联荟萃分析，鉴定出30个全基因组显著位点，其中包括7个错义变异位点及2个与错义变异存在高连锁不平衡的位点。主要关联位点位于ZNF646、HLA-DQB1、FLG、FTO、SLURP2和KRT77基因附近。此外，针对皮肤癣菌病亚型的分析揭示了44个相关信号。我们的研究结果凸显了角质形成生物学紊乱、皮肤屏障缺陷、免疫功能障碍及肥胖在皮肤癣菌病发病风险中的作用。同时，我们观察到该病与其他皮肤疾病及肥胖相关性状存在遗传重叠，这为阐明疾病机制及开发预防与治疗靶点提供了新见解。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Dermatophytosis is a fungal infection affecting keratinized tissues such as skin, nails, and hair, presenting as red and itchy patches, nail thickening, or hair loss. It affects around 20% of the global population but the genetic architecture remains poorly understood. We performed a genome-wide association meta-analysis of over 250,000 cases and 1.37 million controls from FinnGen, Estonian Biobank, UK Biobank, and the Million Veteran Program and identified 30 genome-wide significant loci, including seven missense variants and two loci in high linkage disequilibrium with missense variants. Top associations were near ZNF646, HLA-DQB1, FLG, FTO, SLURP2, and KRT77. Additionally, dermatophytosis subtype analyses revealed 44 signals. Our results highlight the role of disrupted keratin biology, skin barrier defects, immune dysfunction, and obesity in dermatophytosis risk. We also observed genetic overlap with other skin conditions and obesity-related traits, providing insights into disease mechanisms and potential targets for prevention and treatment.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: dermatophytosis, genome-wide association study, genetic susceptibility, skin infection, keratin biology, immune dysfunction, obesity, FinnGen

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 竹简是记录东亚古代文明的重要载体。然而，许多出土竹简已碎裂为成千上万的不规则残片，其缀合工作成为解读内容的关键且极具挑战性的环节。本文提出WisePanda——一种物理驱动的深度学习框架，旨在实现碎裂竹简的自动缀合。基于断裂与材料劣化的物理原理，WisePanda能够自动生成成对的合成训练数据，这些数据捕捉了竹简碎片的物理特性。该方法使得匹配网络的训练无需依赖人工配对的样本，并能提供排序建议以辅助缀合流程。相较于主流的曲线匹配方法与现代生成式方法，WisePanda在匹配准确率上实现了显著且具有统计学意义的提升，从而提高了考古学家缀合竹简残片的工作效率。WisePanda通过物理驱动的机器学习，为应对古代文物修复中的数据稀缺问题提供了新范式。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Bamboo slips are a crucial medium for recording ancient civilizations in East Asia. However, many excavated bamboo slips have been fragmented into thousands of irregular pieces, making their rejoining a vital yet challenging step for understanding their content. Here we introduce WisePanda, a physics-driven deep learning framework designed to rejoin fragmented bamboo slips. Based on the physics of fracture and material deterioration, WisePanda automatically generates paired synthetic training data that captures the physical properties of bamboo fragmentations. This approach enables the training of a matching network without requiring manually paired samples, providing ranked suggestions to facilitate the rejoining process. Compared to the leading curve matching and modern generative methods, WisePanda yields a substantial and statistically significant increase in matching accuracy, accelerating archeologists' efficiency in rejoining fragmented bamboo slips. WisePanda provides a new paradigm for addressing data scarcity in ancient artifact restoration through physics-driven machine learning.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: bamboo slips, fragmented artifacts, physics-driven deep learning, ancient artifact restoration, matching network, synthetic training data, data scarcity, archaeology

### 74. ❌ A rubber-based sensor with over 100 million-level ultra-sensitivity (0–10% strain range) via 3D super-interface

**作者**: Xinghuo Wang, Yaru Huang, Hui Wang (30400), Shiheng Yin, Chuanhui Xu, Zuankai Wang, Yukun Chen
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70434-y](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70434-y)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

|------|------|------|------|

| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文标题为'A rubber-based sensor with over 100 million-level ultra-sensitivity (0–10% strain range) via 3D super-interface'，摘要描述了基于橡胶基底的3D超界面策略开发微裂纹超界面柔性传感器（MSFS），具有超高灵敏度（0-10%应变范围）和线性度，并应用于监测硅阳极电池的膨胀。论文的核心内容是柔性传感器材料、结构和性能，涉及橡胶基材、导电裂纹层、3D超界面、应变传感等。所有评分关键词（medical image analysis, medical imaging, deep learning medical imaging）均与医学图像分析或医学影像相关，而论文未提及任何医学图像、影像数据、诊断、分割、分类或深度学习在医学影像中的应用。论文的应用场景是电池膨胀监测，属于材料科学和传感器领域，与医学无关。因此，所有关键词的相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究解决了柔性传感器在同时实现高灵敏度、宽应变范围和线性度方面的难题，通过3D超界面策略开发了一种微裂纹超界面柔性传感器，在0-10%应变范围内具有超高灵敏度（GF 1.1 × 10⁸）和线性度（0.98），并成功应用于监测硅阳极电池的膨胀。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 受限于材料、结构和界面，同时实现高灵敏度、宽应变范围与线性度仍是柔性传感器领域的“不可能三角”。本研究提出基于图案化橡胶基底-导电裂纹层的三维超界面策略，成功开发出具有超高灵敏度（0-10%应变范围内，灵敏因子达1.1×10⁸，线性度0.98）的微裂纹超界面柔性传感器（MSFS）。该三维超界面依托橡胶基体与导电裂纹层之间微纳尺度物理锚定与氢键界面相互作用的协同效应，实现了强层间结合。在传感过程中，裂纹结构赋予传感器在0-10%应变范围内的超高灵敏度；而三维超界面则确保其在>50%应变条件下仍保持导电连续性。MSFS在硅负极电池膨胀监测中展现出潜在应用价值：当电池膨胀率达2%时，其电阻变化可高达22倍。该方法为超灵敏度应用的柔性传感器定制化设计提供了可行路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Constrained by materials, structures, and interface, achieving high sensitivity, wide strain range, and linearity simultaneously remains an impossible triangle for flexible sensors. Herein, we propose 3D super-interface strategy based on patterned rubber substrate-conductive crack layer, successfully developing a microcrack super-interface flexible sensor (MSFS) with ultra-sensitivity (0-10% strain, GF 1.1 × 10⁸ and linearity 0.98). The 3D super-interface relies on the synergistic micro/nano level physical anchoring, and hydrogen bonding interfacial interactions between the rubber matrix and conductive crack layer, achieving strong interlayer bonding. During the sensing process, the crack structure endows the sensor ultra-sensitivity within 0-10% strain range; while the 3D super-interface ensures continuous electrical conductivity under >50% strain conditions. MSFS holds potential application value in monitoring expansion in silicon anode batteries. When the battery expansion reaches 2%, its resistance change can be as high as 22-fold. This approach enables the customized design of flexible sensors for ultra-sensitivity applications.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: flexible sensor, 3D super-interface, ultra-sensitivity, rubber-based sensor, microcrack structure, strain sensing, silicon anode battery, battery expansion monitoring

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    It is suggested that enhancing trophic factor support, particularly MANF, and improving the host retinal environment are critical for sustaining long-term vision preservation.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过单细胞转录组学分析移植的人类神经祖细胞在视网膜色素变性大鼠模型中的动态基因表达变化，发现这些细胞主要通过分泌神经营养因子、调节代谢和抑制炎症等机制保护光感受器细胞，从而维持视力。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 人类神经祖细胞（hNPCs）在延缓视网膜变性方面展现出潜力，目前正针对视网膜色素变性（RP）进行临床试验评估。然而，移植后的hNPCs长期命运及其与宿主视网膜细胞的相互作用尚不明确。本研究利用单细胞转录组学技术，探究了在RP啮齿动物模型中经视网膜下注射后，移植的hNPCs及宿主视网膜细胞随时间推移的基因表达变化，揭示了退行性视网膜环境中的动态转录组改变。移植的hNPCs主要分化为星形胶质细胞表型并随时间逐渐成熟，通过神经营养因子分泌、代谢调节、抑制细胞凋亡、氧化应激及炎症反应，并协同细胞外基质重塑，从而发挥光感受器保护作用。CellChat分析显示，细胞间信号传递与通讯强度随时间推移而减弱，这与hNPCs-宿主相互作用的弱化相关。这些发现表明，增强神经营养因子支持（特别是MANF）并改善宿主视网膜微环境，对于维持长期视力保护至关重要。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Human neural progenitor cells (hNPCs) show promise in slowing retinal degeneration and are currently being tested in clinical trials for retinitis pigmentosa (RP). However, the long-term fate of grafted hNPCs and their interaction with host retinal cells remain unclear. Here, we used single-cell transcriptomics to investigate temporal gene expression changes in grafted hNPCs and host retinal cells following subretinal injection into a rodent model of RP, revealing dynamic transcriptomic changes in the degenerative retinal environment. Grafted hNPCs primarily differentiate into an astroglial phenotype and mature over time, contributing to photoreceptor protection through trophic factor secretion, metabolic modulation, suppression of apoptosis, oxidative stress, and inflammation, alongside extracellular matrix remodeling. CellChat analysis revealed a decline in intercellular signaling and communication strength over time, correlating with weakened hNPC-host interactions. These findings suggest that enhancing trophic factor support, particularly MANF, and improving the host retinal environment are critical for sustaining long-term vision preservation.

</details>

### 76. ❌ Optimizing spatial organization of FtsZ rings for large-scale constriction in synthetic cells

**作者**: Anastasija Panevska, Aleksandra Šakanović, Gianfranco Paccione, Germán Rivas, Petra Schwille
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70091-1](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70091-1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究合成细胞中FtsZ环的空间组织优化以实现膜收缩，属于合成生物学和细胞重建领域。虽然使用了荧光成像技术，但这是作为实验工具观察生物结构，而非用于医学诊断或临床分析。论文完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习在医学成像中的应用，与所有评分关键词完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    It is shown that cytoFtsN regulates the spatial organization of the FtsZ network primarily by aligning FtsZ filaments while reducing filament depolymerization, which helps to define key requirements in a minimal filament-based system for progressive membrane constriction.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究探索了cytoFtsN如何通过调节FtsZ丝的空间组织来促进大型闭合FtsZ环的形成，从而实现合成细胞中膜的有效收缩，推进了合成细胞自分裂能力的发展。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 空间调控的膜收缩是重构最小化细胞分裂的重要里程碑。在巨型脂质体中，自下而上的方法已成功再现了基于FtsZ的最小化分裂体（divisome）的组装、细胞中部定位及初始收缩过程。然而，迄今为止，从未能观察到由近赤道Z环（FtsZ ring）驱动、最终导致巨型囊泡分裂的渐进式变形。一个明显的主要限制是尺度不匹配，因为纯重构的FtsZ环通常呈现细菌尺度的直径，过小而无法有效收缩典型细胞尺寸的囊泡。因此，我们探索了其他关键分裂体因子在体外提升FtsZ环功能尺度、以匹配合成细胞分裂所需尺寸的潜力。本文重点关注FtsN的胞质结构域（cytoFtsN）及其对FtsZ自组织的影响。值得注意的是，摩尔过量的cytoFtsN能促进巨型囊泡膜上形成大型、闭合的赤道FtsZ环，这些环能够收缩至近乎完全闭合。通过荧光成像和生化分析，我们证明cytoFtsN主要通过对齐FtsZ丝状结构并减少其解聚，来调控FtsZ网络的空间组织。我们的研究结果有助于界定基于丝状结构的最小化系统中实现渐进式膜收缩的关键条件，从而代表了朝着构建能够自我分裂的合成细胞迈出的重要一步。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Spatially regulated membrane constriction is an important milestone in reconstituting minimal cell division. In giant lipid vesicles, bottom-up approaches have reproduced the assembly, mid-cell positioning, and the initial constriction of an FtsZ-based minimal divisome. However, progressive deformation towards giant vesicle scission by near-equatorial Z rings could so far never be observed. One obvious major limitation has been the scale mismatch, as pure reconstituted FtsZ rings typically exhibit bacterial diameters, too small to constrict typical cell-sized vesicles. Therefore, we explore the potential of other key divisome factors to scale up FtsZ-ring functionality in vitro to match the dimensions required for synthetic cell division. We here focus on cytoFtsN, the cytosolic domain of FtsN, and its effect on FtsZ self-organization. Remarkably, a molar excess of cytoFtsN promotes the formation of large, closed equatorial FtsZ rings on giant vesicle membranes, which are able to constrict to almost full closure. By fluorescence imaging and biochemical analysis, we show that cytoFtsN regulates the spatial organization of the FtsZ network primarily by aligning FtsZ filaments while reducing filament depolymerization. Our findings help to define key requirements in a minimal filament-based system for progressive membrane constriction and thus represent a major step forward towards constructing synthetic cells capable of self-division.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: synthetic cells, FtsZ rings, membrane constriction, cytoFtsN, spatial organization, giant vesicles, cell division, minimal divisome

### 77. ❌ MXene-driven nanoscale field-effect junction for advanced 4-terminal perovskite/silicon tandem solar panels

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文通过MXene基掺杂和表面梯度钝化，在钙钛矿活性层中诱导形成场效应结，开发了高效半透明钙钛矿模块，并集成到四端钙钛矿/硅串联太阳能面板中，实现了19.45%的功率转换效率和超过三个月的实际稳定性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 钙钛矿/硅叠层太阳能电池的商业化关键在于实现高效率与高稳定性，并保持可扩展性。本研究提出了一种创新方法，通过在钙钛矿活性层内诱导形成场效应结，以制备可用于四端钙钛矿/硅叠层组件的高效半透明顶板子模块。基于MXene的掺杂与表面梯度钝化的协同作用，使半透明钙钛矿模块在60 cm²有效面积上实现了超过16%的转换效率。这些模块被集成至一个四端叠层组件（0.2 m²）中，其功率转换效率达到19.45%，并借助双面硅异质结电池的增益，在30%地面反照率条件下发电密度提升至超过23 mWcm⁻²。该叠层组件在克里特岛实地安装运行三个月后，仍保持初始输出功率的95%以上，展现出优异的实际环境稳定性。此项研究为产业化应用迈出了重要一步，提出了一种可扩展的高效解决方案，用于下一代光伏技术，且对现有硅产线仅需极少的改造。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The commercialization of perovskite/silicon tandem solar cells hinges on achieving high efficiency and stability while maintaining scalability. This study demonstrates an original approach for inducing the formation of a field effect junction within the perovskite active layer for efficient semi-transparent top modules to be integrated in four-terminal perovskite/silicon tandem panels. A synergy of MXene-based doping and surface gradient passivation enabled semi-transparent perovskite modules with efficiencies surpassing 16% on 60 cm² active area. These were integrated into a four terminal tandem panel (0.2 m<sup>2</sup>) with a power conversion efficiency of 19.45%, further enhanced by bifacial silicon heterojunction cells to reach a power generation density exceeding 23 mWcm<sup>-</sup>² under 30% ground albedo conditions. The tandem panel, installed in Crete, retained over 95% of its initial delivered power after three months, showcasing robust real-world stability. This work provides a significant step toward industrial adoption, presenting a scalable, high-efficiency solution for next-generation photovoltaics with minimal modifications to silicon production lines.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: perovskite/silicon tandem solar cells, MXene, field effect junction, semi-transparent perovskite modules, four-terminal tandem panel, power conversion efficiency, scalability, real-world stability

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 土壤是影响全球粮食生产和生态系统生产力的植物病原体的主要环境储存库。然而，某些土壤也能通过环境和微生物调控来抑制病原体。本研究整合了来自59个国家的1602份土壤宏基因组数据，并结合温室实验，鉴定出32种优势病原体，包括青枯菌（Ralstonia solanacearum）、密歇根棒形杆菌（Clavibacter michiganensis）和欧洲疮痂链霉菌（Streptomyces europaeiscabiei）。病原体热点主要出现在温暖的生态系统和农业土壤中，而较高的土壤微生物多样性、增加的土壤有机碳以及较冷的气候条件则与较低的病原体流行率相关。非致病性链霉菌属物种（Streptomyces spp.）、丛枝菌根真菌（arbuscular mycorrhizal fungi）以及编码萜烯和聚酮化合物的生物合成基因簇与病原体流行率的降低相关。预测模型表明，在未来气候情景下，几种优势细菌病原体的流行率可能会增加，特别是在热带和亚热带地区。通过识别优势病原体的全球驱动因素及其抑制机制，本研究为改进气候变化下植物病害风险的监测与管理奠定了基础。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Soils are the primary environmental reservoir of plant pathogens impacting food production and ecosystem productivity worldwide. Yet, some soils can also suppress pathogens through environmental and microbial regulation. Here we integrate 1602 soil metagenomes from 59 countries with a greenhouse experiment to identify 32 dominant pathogens, including Ralstonia solanacearum, Clavibacter michiganensis, and Streptomyces europaeiscabiei. Pathogen hotspots occur primarily in warm ecosystems and agricultural soils, whereas higher soil microbial diversity, increased soil organic carbon and colder climatic conditions are associated with lower pathogen prevalence. Non-pathogenic Streptomyces spp., arbuscular mycorrhizal fungi, and biosynthetic gene clusters encoding terpenes and polyketides are associated with reduced pathogen prevalence. Predictive modelling suggests that several dominant bacterial pathogens are likely to increase in prevalence under future climate scenarios, particularly in tropical and subtropical regions. By identifying global drivers of dominant pathogens and their suppression, this study provides a foundation for improved surveillance and management of plant disease risks under climate change.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: soil pathogens, metagenomics, plant disease suppression, microbial diversity, climate change, Ralstonia solanacearum, Streptomyces, biosynthetic gene clusters

### 80. ❌ Long-range magnetic order with disordered spin orientations in a high-entropy antiferromagnet

**作者**: Y. R. Shen, Gang Zhang, Qinghua Zhang, Xuejuan Gui, Yu Zhang, Heemin Lee, Cheng‐Tai Kuo, Jun-Sik Lee, Ronny Sutarto, Feng Ye, Z. W. Pan, Xiaomei Qin, Jinchen Wang, Tianping Ying, Youwen Long
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70184-x](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70184-x)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究高熵反铁磁体中的长程磁序与无序自旋取向，属于凝聚态物理和材料科学领域，涉及中子衍射、共振软X射线散射等实验技术。所有评分关键词均与医学图像分析相关，而论文完全不涉及医学、生物医学成像、医学诊断或深度学习在医学图像中的应用，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过元素特异性探测揭示了高熵范德华材料(MnFeCoNi)PS3中，尽管存在显著原子无序，但仍能在72K以下形成长程之字形反铁磁序，且四种过渡金属元素的自旋取向因各向异性与交换相互作用竞争而不同，展示了一种由不同磁性元素协同稳定的新型长程磁序。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 磁性系统中的无序性通常会抑制长程有序，促进如自旋玻璃和磁团簇等短程态的形成。这一现象在高熵材料中尤为显著，其特点是局域磁实体与交换相互作用呈随机分布。然而，在少数特例中，长程磁有序可以在高熵系统中持续存在，但其微观特征与内在机制仍不明确，尤其是各组成元素的磁行为。本研究结合中子衍射与共振软X射线散射技术，对一种高熵蜂窝状晶格范德华材料 (Mn<sub>1/4</sub>Fe<sub>1/4</sub>Co<sub>1/4</sub>Ni<sub>1/4</sub>)PS<sub>3</sub> 的磁有序进行了元素分辨的探测。尽管存在显著的原子无序，材料在72 K以下仍观测到长程之字形反铁磁有序，且所有四种过渡金属元素均参与了一个统一的相变。然而，不同元素的自旋取向存在差异，这归因于单离子各向异性与交换相互作用之间的竞争。我们的研究结果展示了一种具有无序自旋取向的新型长程磁有序态，它由高熵磁体中不同的磁性元素协同稳定，为理解复杂磁性系统提供了新的范式。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Disorder in magnetic systems typically suppresses long-range order, promoting short-range states such as spin glasses and magnetic clusters. This is particularly prominent in high-entropy materials, characterized by the random distributions of local magnetic entities and exchange interactions. However, in rare exceptions, long-range magnetic order can persist in high-entropy systems, while the microscopic characters and underlying mechanisms remain elusive, especially the magnetic behaviors of individual elements. Here, combining neutron diffraction and resonant soft x-ray scattering, we have conducted an element-specific investigation into the magnetic order of a high-entropy honeycomb-lattice van der Waals material (Mn<sub>1/4</sub>Fe<sub>1/4</sub>Co<sub>1/4</sub>Ni<sub>1/4</sub>)PS<sub>3</sub>. Despite significant atomic disorder, long-range zigzag antiferromagnetic order is observed below 72 K, with all four transition-metal elements participating in a unified phase transition. However, the spin orientations of various elements are distinct, attributed to the competition between single-ion anisotropies and exchange interactions. Our findings showcase a novel form of long-range magnetic order with disordered spin orientations, which is synergically stabilized by distinct magnetic elements in a high entropy magnet, offering a new paradigm for understanding complex magnetic systems.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: high-entropy antiferromagnet, long-range magnetic order, disordered spin orientations, element-specific investigation, zigzag antiferromagnetic order, honeycomb-lattice van der Waals material, single-ion anisotropies, exchange interactions

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文受变形虫启发开发了一种液态金属通用夹持器，能够以极低接触压力抓取和释放多种形状、尺寸和硬度的物体，实现了从微克到百克级的多尺度操作。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 变形虫能够像液体般流动以改变自身形态，从而有效捕获并排出各类猎物。受此启发，我们提出一种液态金属通用夹持器，能够在液体和空气中有效抓取并主动释放不同形状、尺寸及硬度的目标物。我们揭示了一种表面张力诱导的主动释放机制，实现了对微尺度物体的可调控主动释放。该夹持器的工作重量范围跨越14个数量级（从10<sup>-12</sup>克至200克），并实现了约10帕的低接触抓取压力，适用于操作精密物品。它能在毫秒级时间内捕获并释放运动物体，且无需精确对位。一种环境自适应的表面活性设计将其功能拓展至非电解质环境。该夹持器在多尺度操作、低接触压力和可调释放速度方面展现出优于现有机器人夹持器的性能指标，为生物体与微尺度物体的操作提供了重要解决方案。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The amoeba can flow like liquid to change its morphology to effectively capture and excrete various prey. Inspired by the amoeba, we present a liquid metal universal gripper capable of effective grasping and active releasing of targets with various shapes, sizes, and stiffnesses in liquid and air. We unveil a surface tension induced active release mechanism enabling tunable active release of micro-objects. The gripper operates across 14 orders of magnitude in weight (from 10<sup>-12 </sup>g to 200 g) and achieves a low gripping contact pressure of ~10 Pa for handling delicate items. It can capture and release moving objects within milliseconds without precise alignment. An environment-agnostic surface activity design extends its functionality to a non-electrolyte environment. The gripper offers notable performance metrics over existing robotic grippers in multiscale operation, low contact pressure, and tunable releasing speed, representing a notable solution for living organisms and microscale objects.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: liquid metal gripper, universal gripper, multiscale manipulation, low contact pressure, active release mechanism, surface tension, micro-object handling, robotic gripper

### 82. ❌ High-quality metagenome assembly from nanopore reads with nanoMDBG

**作者**: Gaëtan Benoit, Robert James, Sébastien Raguideau, Georgina Alabone, Tim Goodall, Rayan Chikhi, Christopher Quince
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    论文解决了纳米孔测序数据在宏基因组组装中效率低下的问题，开发了nanoMDBG方法，相比现有工具能重建更多高质量宏基因组组装基因组，同时减少计算资源消耗。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 第三代长读长测序技术显著提升了宏基因组组装质量。高准确度的PacBio HiFi测序读长能够从单个样本中产出数百个近乎完整的宏基因组组装基因组。近期，更具成本效益的牛津纳米孔测序技术的单碱基错误率已提升至1-2%。然而，当前主流的宏基因组组装工具主要针对HiFi数据优化，难以适配牛津纳米孔技术所产生的大规模数据集。我们推出了nanoMDBG——作为metaMDBG的演进版本，该工具通过在最小化空间进行纠错预处理，实现了对最新牛津纳米孔读长的支持。在一系列包括大型400 Gbp土壤样本在内的牛津纳米孔数据集中，nanoMDBG重建的高质量宏基因组组装基因组数量可达次优牛津纳米孔组装工具metaFlye的两倍，同时仅需其三分之一的CPU时间和内存。关键的是，最新牛津纳米孔技术如今能够在相同测序深度下，产出与PacBio HiFi技术相媲美的宏基因组组装结果。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Third-generation long-read sequencing technologies, significantly improve metagenome assemblies. Highly accurate PacBio HiFi reads can yield hundreds of near-complete metagenome-assembled genomes (MAGs) from a single sample. Recently, the accuracy of the more cost-effective Oxford Nanopore Technologies (ONT) platform has increased to a per-base error rate of 1-2%. However, current metagenome assemblers are optimized for HiFi and do not scale to the large data sets that ONT enables. We present nanoMDBG, an evolution of metaMDBG, which supports the latest ONT reads through an error correction pre-processing step in minimizer-space. Across a range of ONT datasets, including a large 400 Gbp soil sample, nanoMDBG reconstructs up to twice as many high-quality MAGs as the next best ONT assembler, metaFlye, while requiring a third of the CPU time and memory. Critically, the latest ONT technology can now produce comparable MAG construction results as those obtained using PacBio HiFi at the same sequencing depth.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: nanopore sequencing, metagenome assembly, nanoMDBG, metagenome-assembled genomes, ONT, PacBio HiFi, computational efficiency, error correction

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 水系锌金属电池为电网级储能提供了一条安全、低成本的路径，但存在枝晶生长与腐蚀问题。传统的电解质设计大多忽视了电场驱动的界面动力学过程，例如运行过程中溶剂化结构的演变与组分再分布。本文提出了一种具有高供体数与高偶极矩特性的亲和性添加剂策略，以N,N-二甲基脲（DMU）为例，在运行电场下动态调控Zn<sup>2+</sup>的溶剂化结构及双电层结构。基于物理基础的分子描述符指导，我们筛选出能够在电场诱导下实现界面富集的添加剂，在此过程中，强偶极-场耦合促进其进入Zn<sup>2+</sup>溶剂化壳层，从而促使锌沉积更均匀。结果表明，优化后的电解质仅需添加2 wt%的添加剂，即可实现锌沉积/剥离约99.9%的库仑效率。该体系在60%放电深度下稳定运行700小时，性能优于基准电解质。描述符指导的筛选进一步表明其他候选添加剂遵循相同规律，证明了该策略具有更广泛的适用性。采用高面容量（约3 mAh cm<sup>-2</sup>）和低N/P比（约1.8）的实用化Zn | |ZnI<sub>2</sub>全电池在0.15 A g<sup>-1</sup>电流密度下实现了750次稳定循环，容量保持率达84.5%。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Aqueous Zn metal batteries offer a safe, low-cost route to grid-scale energy storage yet suffer from dendrite growth and corrosion issues. Conventional electrolyte designs largely overlook electric-field-driven interfacial dynamics such as solvation structure evolution and component redistribution during operation. Here, we propose an affinitive additive strategy featuring high donor number and dipole moment, exemplified by N,N-dimethylurea (DMU), to dynamically modulate Zn<sup>2+</sup> solvation and the structure of the electric double layer under operational electric fields. Guided by physically grounded molecular descriptors, we identify additives capable of electric-field-induced interfacial enrichment, during which strong dipole-field coupling promotes their incorporation into the Zn<sup>2+</sup> solvation shell and promotes more uniform Zn deposition. As a result, the optimized electrolyte achieves a coulombic efficiency of ~99.9% for Zn plating/stripping with only 2 wt% additive. It also sustains stable operation for 700 h at 60% depth of discharge, outperforming the baseline electrolyte. Descriptor-guided screening further reveals that other candidates follow the same pattern, suggesting broader applicability of this approach. Practical Zn | |ZnI<sub>2</sub> full cells with high areal capacity (~3 mAh cm<sup>-2</sup>) and low N/P ratio (~1.8) achieve 750 stable cycles at 0.15 A g<sup>-1</sup> with 84.5% capacity retention.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: aqueous zinc metal batteries, electrolyte design, solvation structure, electric double layer, dendrite growth, coulombic efficiency, Zn plating/stripping, affinitive additives

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究解决了β-支链芳香族D-氨基酸高效合成不足的问题，通过转氨酶催化的动态动力学拆分方法成功合成了多种高收率、高对映选择性的β-支链芳香族D-氨基酸，并将其应用于抗癌药物兰瑞肽的修饰。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 近年来，非天然氨基酸（ncAAs）的生物催化合成领域取得了巨大进展，其中转氨酶、脱氢酶和氨裂解酶等酶的应用尤为突出。β-支链芳香族D-氨基酸的结构框架对药物效能至关重要，它影响着空间构象、与受体的结合模式以及药代动力学性质。然而，针对β-支链D-氨基酸高效合成的研究尚显匮乏，这严重阻碍了构效关系（SAR）研究的进展。本文报道了一种依赖于PLP的转氨酶BsDAAT（来源于Bacillus sp. strain YM-1）催化的β-支链芳香族D-氨基酸类似物的不对称合成方法。该高效的转氨化系统基于动态动力学拆分（DKR）过程。通过对接分析和简洁的酶工程改造，我们成功以高产率（最高达99%）、高非对映异构体比例（>20:1）和高对映体过量值（最高达99%）获得了多种β-取代的芳香族D-氨基酸。这些β-支链芳香族D-氨基酸随后被成功引入抗肿瘤药物兰瑞肽的修饰中。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The synthesis of non-canonical amino acids (ncAAs) has recently made tremendous progress in the field of biocatalysis, with enzymes such as transaminases, dehydrogenases, and ammonia lyases being used. Frameworks of β-branched aromatic D-amino acids are crucial for the efficacy of pharmaceuticals, influencing spatial conformation, binding modes with receptors and pharmacokinetic properties. However, there is a scarcity of studies on the efficient synthesis of β-branched D-amino acids, which has significantly hindered the advancement of structure-activity relationship (SAR) studies. Here, we present the asymmetric synthesis of β-branched aromatic D-amino acid analogues catalyzed by PLP-dependent transaminase BsDAAT (from Bacillus sp. strain YM-1), an efficient transamination system that relies on the dynamic kinetic resolution (DKR) process. Through docking analysis and concise enzyme engineering, we successfully obtain various aromatic D-amino acids with β-substitution in high yields (up to 99%), dr ratios (>20:1) and ee values (up to 99%). These β-branched aromatic D-amino acids are then successfully introduced into the modifications of the antineoplastic reagent Lanreotide.

</details>

**关键词**: β-branched aromatic D-amino acids, transaminase, dynamic kinetic resolution, enzyme engineering, asymmetric synthesis, biocatalysis, Lanreotide modification, PLP-dependent transaminase

Goode, Crescens Tiu, Scott Layzell, Joshua Konecnik, Rebecca Wilson, Sidonie Wicky John, Samuel Jouny, Naomi Guppy, Victoire Boulat, Jonathan Mannion, Maria Goicoechea, Shaun Tan, Sam Lawson, Chris Starling, Gabrielle Elshtein, Nivedita Ravindran

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究发现肿瘤和基质细胞中的坏死性凋亡协同作用是免疫原性细胞死亡疗法联合检查点阻断治疗三阴性乳腺癌的关键机制，并证明STING激动剂可使免疫“冷”肿瘤对该疗法产生反应。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 免疫疗法已改变了包括早期三阴性乳腺癌（TNBC）在内的癌症治疗格局，但大多数晚期TNBC患者对免疫检查点阻断（ICB）联合化疗方案仍无应答。要实现持久控制，不仅需要杀伤肿瘤细胞，还需依赖激活抗肿瘤免疫的免疫原性细胞死亡（ICD）。本研究采用能重现基底样肿瘤免疫特征的Brca1<sup>⁻/⁻</sup>p53<sup>⁻/⁻</sup>类器官来源TNBC模型，发现RIPK1驱动的ICD与抗PD-1疗法在免疫浸润型肿瘤中产生协同作用，可诱导持久的肿瘤控制并形成免疫记忆。机制研究表明，该过程同时需要肿瘤细胞内在性及基质细胞程序性坏死。敲除肿瘤细胞中的Ripk1或Mlkl基因，或敲除基质区室中的Mlkl基因，均会显著削弱治疗效果。此外，通过STING激动剂干预，可使免疫学意义上的"冷肿瘤"对基于ICD的疗法产生应答。这些发现证明，IAP拮抗剂与检查点阻断联合治疗的获益，关键取决于肿瘤细胞与基质细胞程序性坏死的协同作用，强调了在设计靶向ICD的免疫疗法时，必须综合考虑肿瘤微环境背景。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Immunotherapy has transformed cancer treatment, including early triple-negative breast cancer (TNBC), yet most patients with advanced TNBC fail to respond to immune checkpoint blockade (ICB) plus chemotherapy. Durable control likely requires not only tumour cell killing but also immunogenic cell death (ICD) that activates antitumour immunity. Using a Brca1<sup>⁻/⁻</sup>p53<sup>⁻/⁻</sup> organoid-derived TNBC model that recapitulates the immune landscapes of basal-like tumours, we show that RIPK1-driven ICD synergises with anti-PD-1 therapy to induce durable tumour control and immune memory in immune-infiltrated tumours. Mechanistically, both tumour-intrinsic and stromal necroptosis are required. Deletion of Ripk1 or Mlkl in tumour cells, or Mlkl in the stromal compartment, markedly impairs therapeutic efficacy. Moreover, immunologically "cold" tumours can be rendered responsive to ICD-based therapy by STING agonists. These findings demonstrate that the benefit of IAP antagonism with checkpoint blockade critically depends on coordinated necroptosis in both tumour and stromal cells, underscoring the need to integrate tumour microenvironmental context when designing ICD-targeted immunotherapies.

</details>
<br>

### 86. ❌ Synergistic aluminum dual-atom sites and nickel nanoclusters for acetylene selective hydrogenation

**作者**: Yanan Liu, He Yu, Mengjiao Li, Li Yan, Ruihu Lu, Xiuting Fu, Zhenfei Zhang, Youqi Zhu, Ziyun Wang, Shubo Tian
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-05
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70323-4](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70323-4)

| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文标题和摘要明确表明该研究属于化学催化领域，具体涉及铝双原子位点和镍纳米团簇协同催化乙炔选择性加氢。全文未提及任何医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像相关内容，与给定的三个关键词完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过设计铝双原子位点与镍纳米团簇的协同催化剂，解决了乙炔选择性加氢中活性与选择性的权衡问题，在温和条件下实现了近乎完全的乙炔转化和约90%的乙烯选择性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 协同催化通过不同活性物种分别活化反应底物，为提升化学转化效率提供了有力策略。尽管Al<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>与块体铝物种常被用作催化剂载体，其本身很少被视为活性中心，尤其在加氢反应中。本研究表明，原子级分散的铝物种可在高温下催化乙炔转化。基于这一发现，我们设计了一种协同催化剂，其特点是通过固相转化耦合气体吸附策略精准构建铝双原子位点与镍纳米团簇的配对结构，从而突破了传统催化中活性与选择性的权衡关系。在温和、经济的反应条件下，该催化剂实现了接近完全的乙炔转化率，乙烯选择性约达90%，并展现出优异的长期稳定性。原位光谱分析与理论计算揭示了协同作用机制：镍纳米团簇将H<sub>2</sub>高效解离为活性氢物种（H*），相邻的铝双原子位点则将H*传递至π吸附的乙炔分子，相较于过度加氢与积碳路径，该过程显著降低了乙烯形成的能垒。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Synergistic catalysis, where distinct active species collaboratively activate different substrates, provides a powerful strategy for achieving chemical transformations with enhanced efficiency. Although Al<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub> and bulk aluminum species are widely employed as catalyst supports, they are seldom regarded as active centers, especially in hydrogenation. Here, we show that atomically dispersed Al species can catalyze acetylene conversion at elevated temperatures. Building on this insight, we have designed a synergistic catalyst featuring precisely controlled Al dual-atom sites paired with Ni nanoclusters, synthesized via a solid-transformation-coupled gas-adsorption strategy to overcome the typical activity-selectivity trade-off. Under mild, cost-effective conditions, this catalyst achieves nearly full acetylene conversion with ~90% ethylene selectivity and excellent long-term stability. In situ spectroscopy and theoretical calculations reveal a cooperative mechanism: Ni nanoclusters efficiently dissociate H<sub>2</sub> into active hydrogen species (H*), while adjacent Al dual-atom sites shuttle the H* species to π-adsorbed acetylene, lowering the energy barrier for ethylene formation compared to over-hydrogenation and coke formation.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: synergistic catalysis, aluminum dual-atom sites, nickel nanoclusters, acetylene selective hydrogenation, ethylene selectivity, solid-transformation-coupled gas-adsorption, cooperative mechanism, in situ spectroscopy

### 87. ❌ Revealing intrinsic 3D spin angular momentum of evanescent acoustic phonons on a single-crystal surface using ultrafast optoacoustics

**作者**: Yi He, Guojie Luo, Hoon Sohn, Osamu Matsuda, Oliver B. Wright, Zhongqing Su
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-05
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70019-9](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70019-9)

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是声子（phonons）的自旋角动量（spin angular momentum），具体涉及表面倏逝声学声子（evanescent acoustic phonons）的三维自旋特性，使用超快光学声学技术进行实验。论文内容完全属于凝聚态物理、声学和材料科学领域，与医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像没有任何关联。所有关键词均与论文主题无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究揭示了单晶表面倏逝声学声子具有内在的三维自旋角动量，并通过超快光学声学实验验证了这一发现，为自旋-轨道相互作用工程提供了基础。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 声波与弹性波自旋角动量的最新进展深化了我们对经典与量子体系中声子的理解。本文研究了单晶表面上的倏逝声学声子，并揭示了一种沿所有轴向均具有非零分量的本征三维自旋角动量——这与各向同性介质截然不同。沿特定晶向，倏逝声学声子表现出自旋-动量锁定特性；而沿其他方向则产生不受约束的自旋角动量及完全三维的自旋纹理。晶格动力学计算表明，三维自旋角动量是倏逝声学声子本征态的基本属性，源于晶体各向异性。实验中采用超快萨格纳克干涉仪产生吉赫兹频段的倏逝声学声子波包，并以微米级空间分辨率与飞秒级时间分辨率对垂直原子速度场进行成像，再结合模拟的面内速度场验证了上述发现。表面结构化的三维自旋角动量分布遵循角动量守恒定律与晶体对称性原则。本研究为传感、信息编码及混合自旋电子-光子系统中自旋-轨道相互作用的调控提供了新途径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Recent advances in spin angular momentum (SAM) of acoustic and elastic waves have deepened our understanding of phonons across classical and quantum regimes. Here, we investigate evanescent acoustic phonons (EAPs) on a single-crystal surface and reveal an intrinsic three-dimensional (3D) spin angular momentum (SAM) with nonzero components along all axes-distinct from isotropic media. EAPs exhibit spin-momentum locking along specific crystallographic directions, while other directions yield unconstrained SAM and fully 3D spin textures. Lattice-dynamics calculations demonstrate that 3D SAM is fundamental to EAP eigenstates, arising from crystal anisotropy. Experiments using an ultrafast Sagnac interferometer generate GHz EAP wave packets and image out-of-plane atomic velocity fields with microscale spatial and femtosecond temporal resolution, which are integrated with simulated in-plane velocity fields to verify findings. The structured 3D SAM distribution over the surface is governed by angular momentum conservation and crystal symmetry. Our findings facilitate engineering spin-orbit interactions for sensing, information encoding, and hybrid spintronic-photonic systems.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: evanescent acoustic phonons, spin angular momentum, 3D spin textures, ultrafast optoacoustics, single-crystal surface, spin-momentum locking, crystal anisotropy, Sagnac interferometer

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是肠道微生物组与心血管疾病风险的关系，通过代谢组学分析发现肠道微生物代谢物与心脏、肾脏功能的亚临床变化相关，并预测心血管疾病风险。论文完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像技术，研究方法是基于代谢组学、遗传学和观察性研究，而非图像处理或分析。

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    It is demonstrated that gut microbiome-related changes can be detected in association with subclinical variations in heart and kidney function, suggesting that the gut microbiome interacts with the cardiorenal axis and participates in an interorgan crosstalk affecting host physiology and risk of CVD.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究发现肠道微生物组通过代谢芳香氨基酸产生代谢物，影响心脏和肾脏功能，并预测未来心血管疾病风险，揭示了肠道微生物组-肾脏-心脏轴的作用机制。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 心血管疾病（CVD）仍然是全球健康面临的重大挑战。我们亟需能够早期识别疾病发生与进展的生物标志物。我们及先前其他研究已表明，肠道微生物组的变化与代谢性疾病及心血管疾病存在关联。本研究进一步证明，肠道微生物组的相关变化可在心脏与肾脏功能的亚临床变异中被检测到。在一个代谢健康的欧洲人群中，与芳香族氨基酸（苯丙氨酸和酪氨酸）的肠道微生物代谢相关的标志物，与循环中的前心房利钠肽及估算的肾小球滤过率存在关联。观察性证据与遗传学证据进一步表明，微生物组相关代谢物是这一肠道微生物-肾脏轴的中介因子，其基线水平在一个外部的加拿大人群中与心血管疾病的发生风险相关。总之，我们的研究表明，肠道微生物组与心肾轴相互作用，并参与影响宿主生理及心血管疾病风险的器官间通讯。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Cardiovascular diseases (CVD) remain a major global health challenge. Early markers of disease initiation and progression are urgently needed. We, and others, have previously shown changes in the gut microbiome in association with metabolic and CVD. Here, we demonstrate that gut microbiome-related changes can be detected in association with subclinical variations in heart and kidney function. Markers related to gut microbial metabolism of aromatic amino acids, phenylalanine and tyrosine, associate with circulating pro-atrial natriuretic peptide and estimated glomerular filtration rate in a metabolically healthy European population. Observational and genetic evidence further identify microbiome-related metabolites as mediators of this gut microbiome-kidney axis, with their baseline levels associating with incident CVD in an external Canadian population. Altogether, our work suggests that the gut microbiome interacts with the cardiorenal axis and participates in an interorgan crosstalk affecting host physiology and risk of CVD.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: gut microbiome, cardiovascular diseases, kidney function, heart function, microbial metabolites, aromatic amino acids, cardiometabolic axis, disease prediction
