!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    This study provides a mechanistic brain-wide account of how a vertebrate brain integrates multiple features to drive sensorimotor decisions, bridging behavioral algorithms with their neural implementation.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究揭示了斑马鱼幼虫大脑如何通过前脑干作为多特征整合中心，将运动一致性、亮度水平和亮度变化三个视觉特征并行计算并汇合，从而驱动感觉运动决策的神经机制。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 动物持续从环境中提取并评估多种感官信息以指导行为。然而，神经环路如何整合多个潜在冲突的输入仍知之甚少。本研究以幼年斑马鱼为模型，利用其对连贯随机点运动的强烈视动反应（optomotor response）及向光性（phototaxis）行为来探讨这一问题。我们证明动物采用了一种基于三种视觉特征的叠加行为算法：运动连贯性、亮度水平以及亮度变化。通过全脑双光子成像，我们定位了这些计算的发生位置，并发现前侧后脑（anterior hindbrain）作为一个多特征整合枢纽。通过对功能已鉴定的神经元进行单细胞神经递质与形态学分析，我们描绘了计算节点内部及节点间潜在的连接模式。这些实验揭示了三条并行且汇聚的计算通路，与我们的行为学结果相符。本研究从机制层面提供了脊椎动物大脑如何整合多特征以驱动感觉运动决策的全脑解释，从而在行为算法与其神经实现之间建立了桥梁。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Animals continuously extract and evaluate diverse sensory information from the environment to guide behavior. Yet, how neural circuits integrate multiple, potentially conflicting, inputs remains poorly understood. Here, we use larval zebrafish to address this question, leveraging their robust optomotor response to coherent random dot motion and phototaxis towards light. We demonstrate that animals employ an additive behavioral algorithm of three visual features: motion coherence, luminance level, and changes in luminance. Using brain-wide two-photon imaging, we identify the loci of these computations, with the anterior hindbrain emerging as a multifeature integration hub. Through single-cell neurotransmitter and morphological analyses of functionally identified neurons, we characterize potential connections within and across computational nodes. These experiments reveal three parallel and converging computational pathways, matching our behavioral results. Our study provides a mechanistic brain-wide account of how a vertebrate brain integrates multiple features to drive sensorimotor decisions, bridging behavioral algorithms with their neural implementation.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: larval zebrafish, visuomotor decision-making, multifeature integration, anterior hindbrain, two-photon imaging, neural circuits, sensorimotor decisions, behavioral algorithms

### 91. ❌ Amorphization-induced plastic deformation in nanodiamonds

**期刊/来源**: nature_communications

| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究纳米金刚石的非晶化诱导塑性变形机制，属于材料科学、纳米力学和凝聚态物理领域，与医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像完全无关。论文内容涉及透射电子显微镜机械测试、纳米尺度力学行为、金刚石变形机制等，没有任何医学或临床相关内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究发现纳米金刚石在压缩应变下通过形成互连的非晶碳网络实现超塑性变形，可承受超过90%的应变而不破裂，且这种效应仅在尺寸小于约13纳米时发生。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 金刚石由sp³共价碳键构成，以其卓越的硬度、导热性和宽带隙而闻名，但其固有的脆性严重限制了其变形与加工能力。本文报道了利用定制设计的原位透射电子显微镜力学样品台，在纳米金刚石中实现的一种非晶化介导的超大塑性。与位错运动或晶相转变等传统机制不同，该变形过程由相互连接的非晶碳网络的形成所主导，该网络能够适应应力并实现晶粒的协同旋转与滑动。这种非晶化介导的塑性使纳米金刚石能够承受超过90%的压缩应变而不发生断裂。研究还发现了一个明显的尺寸依赖性转变：超大塑性仅在约13纳米以下尺寸出现，而更大尺寸的金刚石则以脆性方式变形。这项工作为纳米尺度力学提供了关键见解，并为基于金刚石的纳米制造、应变工程以及先进的量子或电子器件应用带来了令人振奋的机遇。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Diamond, composed of sp³ covalent carbon bonds, is renowned for its exceptional hardness, thermal conductivity, and wide bandgap, yet its intrinsic brittleness severely limits deformation and processing. Here, we report an amorphization-mediated ultralarge plasticity in nanodiamonds using a custom-designed in-situ transmission electron microscopy mechanical holder. Unlike conventional mechanisms such as dislocation motion or crystalline phase transformation, the deformation is governed by the formation of an interconnected amorphous carbon network that accommodates stress and enables cooperative grain rotation and sliding. This amorphization-mediated plasticity allows nanodiamonds to sustain compressive strains exceeding 90% without fracture. A distinct size-dependent transition is identified: ultralarge plasticity occurs only below ~13 nm, while larger diamonds deform in a brittle manner. This work provides critical insights into nanoscale mechanics and offering exciting opportunities for diamond-based nano-manufacturing, strain engineering, and advanced quantum or electronic device applications.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: nanodiamonds, amorphization, plastic deformation, transmission electron microscopy, size-dependent transition, compressive strain, nanoscale mechanics, diamond-based nano-manufacturing

**作者**: Chakreshwara Kuloor, Vishakha Goyal, Zhuang Ma, Fairoosa Poovan, Dilver Peña Fuentes, Wolfgang Baumann, Jun Zhao, Radek Zbořil, Mathias Beller, Rajenahally V. Jagadeesh

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究解决了在温和条件下将伯酰胺选择性氢化为伯胺这一有机合成难题，通过开发一种基于甲氧基取代三膦配体的均相钌催化剂实现了这一转化。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 酰胺的催化氢化反应始终是有机合成中最具挑战性的还原转化之一。尽管过去数十年间已付出巨大努力，目前仍未有通用方案报道能够利用分子氢将相应的伯酰胺转化为各类伯胺。为完成这一极具挑战性的反应，本文报道了一种基于甲氧基取代三膦配体（Triphos<sup>(对甲氧基苯基)</sup>）的特异性均相钌催化剂。在该钌催化剂体系存在下，具有工业应用价值、带有官能团且结构多样的芳香族、杂环及脂肪族伯酰胺（包括脂肪酰胺）均能在相对温和的条件下（典型条件为115°C和10 bar H<sub>2</sub>）选择性氢化，生成相应的伯胺。所得胺类化合物是具有重要价值的化学品，在化学、医学、生物学以及材料与能源技术领域均具有广泛应用。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The catalytic hydrogenation of amides continues to be one of the most difficult reductive transformations in organic synthesis. Despite significant efforts in past decades, there is no general protocol reported allowing the synthesis of various primary amines from the corresponding primary amides using molecular hydrogen. To perform this challenging reaction, here we report a specific homogeneous ruthenium catalyst based on the methoxy-substituted triphos ligand (Triphos<sup>(p-anisole)</sup>). In the presence of this Ru-catalyst system, industrially relevant, functionalized, and structurally diverse aromatic, heterocyclic and aliphatic primary amides including fatty amides have been selectively hydrogenated to produce the corresponding primary amines under comparably mild conditions (typically 115 °C and 10 bar H<sub>2</sub>). The resulting amines are valuable compounds with diverse applications in chemistry, medicine and biology as well as in materials and energy technologies.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: catalytic hydrogenation, primary amides, primary amines, ruthenium catalyst, homogeneous catalysis, mild conditions, Triphos ligand, organic synthesis

### 93. ❌ Bioinspired nanofluidic iontronic device with integrated photoreceptor and photosynaptic functions

**作者**: Wenchao Liu, Lian Duan, Xiangyu Zhang, Xinyi Zhu, Yongxin Ge, Guoheng Xu, Zhixiao Si, Jiqing Dai, Wenbo Chang, Miliang Zhang, Ronghua Lan, Zhijun Hu, Ruotian Chen, Kowit Hengphasatporn, Yasuteru Shigeta, Kai Xiao

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究开发了一种仿生光调控纳米流体离子电子器件，通过碳纳米管/二硫化钼异质结构模拟生物视觉的光感受和光突触功能，实现了准确的方向识别和可靠的指纹检测。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 生物视觉通过光诱导跨膜离子输运获取外部信息，并产生电脉冲。通过光调控离子输运来模拟光感受器与光突触的双重视觉功能是一项重大挑战。本文提出一种仿生光调控纳米流体离子电子器件，可通过工程化的碳纳米管与二硫化钼（CNT/MoS<sub>2</sub>）异质结构模拟生物视觉功能。该仿生器件结合了类光感受器光学传感与类光突触信号处理两大关键功能，并借助偏压调控的瞬态光响应速度实现了动态可调的极性切换行为。理论与实验结果均证明，光调控离子输运源于CNT/MoS<sub>2</sub>纳米管异质界面诱导的非对称光电压产生。此外，我们展示了该器件在不同入射光角度下实现精确方向识别与可靠指纹检测的应用。器件的双向光响应特性凸显了其在自适应视觉模拟系统中的独特优势。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Biological vision acquires external information through light-induced transmembrane ion transport, generating electrical impulses. Emulating the dual visual functions of photoreceptors and photosynapses through light-modulated ion transport presents a significant challenge. Herein, we present a bioinspired light-regulated nanofluidic iontronic device that can mimic biological visual functionalities, realized through an engineered carbon nanotube and molybdenum disulfide (CNT/MoS<sub>2</sub>) heterostructure. This bioinspired device combines two key functionalities of photoreceptor-like optical sensing and photosynaptic signal processing with dynamically adjustable polarity-switching behavior, achieved via bias voltage-modulated transient photoresponse speeds. Both theoretical and experimental results prove that light-modulated ion transport originates from the heterointerface-induced asymmetric photovoltage generation across CNT/MoS<sub>2</sub> nanotube. Furthermore, we demonstrate its implementation for both accurate orientation recognition and reliable fingerprint detection under varying incident light angles. The device's bidirectional photoresponsiveness highlights its unique advantages for adaptive visual simulation systems.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: bioinspired nanofluidic iontronic device, photoreceptor, photosynaptic functions, carbon nanotube/MoS2 heterostructure, light-modulated ion transport, orientation recognition, fingerprint detection, adaptive visual simulation

### 94. ❌ Ternary solvation sheath reconfiguration drives sustainable cryogenic Li||Cl2 batteries

**作者**: Qihao Liu, Guanzhong Ma, Ling Wei, Yanxia Wu, Jiajun Geng, Junwei Han, Xin Qin, LinJie ZHI
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-05
**DOI**: [10.1038/s41467-026-70092-0](https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-026-70092-0)

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是低温锂-氯电池的电解质和界面工程，属于电化学储能领域。全文未涉及医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习医学成像的任何内容，与所有评分关键词完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了低温锂-氯电池因电解质分解导致的界面不稳定问题，通过三元溶剂化鞘重构策略设计了一种新型电解质，在-40°C下实现了1100次循环后99.2%的容量保持率和库仑效率。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 可充电锂| |氯<sub>2</sub>电池在低温储能方面前景广阔，但受限于电解液分解导致的界面不稳定性，尤其在低温条件下。我们发现其失效机制源于一种复杂的溶剂化化学过程，该过程涉及Li<sup>+</sup>、高反应活性的SOCl<sub>2</sub>以及配位氯铝酸盐，共同驱动了寄生副反应。本文提出了一种利用三氟甲磺酸锂重构溶剂化结构的三元溶剂化鞘层重构策略。该方法通过利用强阴离子-阳离子相互作用，重构了锂离子的配位环境，置换出溶剂分子，并引导原位形成一种坚固的双层正极电解质界面相，其内层富含无机成分。这种人工设计的界面相有效抑制了电解液降解，并通过降低Li<sup>+</sup>脱溶剂化能垒增强了电荷转移动力学。因此，采用三元溶剂化鞘层重构电解质的电池可在-40°C下实现稳定循环（1000 mA g⁻<sup>1</sup>），在1100次循环后容量保持率达99.2%，库仑效率达99.2%，并能在-80°C的极低温下可靠运行。本研究为通过溶剂化化学设计功能性界面相、实现可持续储能，建立了一个系统性的框架。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Rechargeable Li | |Cl<sub>2</sub> batteries hold promise for low temperature storage but suffer from interfacial instability due to electrolyte decomposition, particularly at cryogenic temperatures. We identify the failure mechanism as a complex solvation chemistry involving Li<sup>+</sup>, reactive SOCl<sub>2</sub>, and coordinating chloroaluminates that drives parasitic reactions. Here, we demonstrate a Ternary Solvation Sheath Reconfiguration strategy using lithium trifluoromethanesulfonate to engineer the solvation structure. By leveraging strong anion-cation interactions, this approach reconfigures the coordination environment to displace solvent molecules and directs the in-situ formation of a robust, bilayered positive electrode electrolyte interphase featuring an inorganic-rich inner layer. This engineered interphase effectively suppresses electrolyte degradation and enhances charge-transfer kinetics by lowering the Li<sup>+</sup> desolvation barrier. Consequently, cells employing the Ternary Solvation Sheath Reconfiguration electrolyte sustain stable cycling at -40 °C (1000 mA g⁻<sup>1</sup>), maintaining capacity retention of 99.2% and Coulombic efficiency of 99.2% after 1100 cycles, while enabling reliable operation even at -80 °C. This work establishes a systematic framework for designing functional interphases via solvation chemistry for sustainable energy storage.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Li||Cl2 batteries, cryogenic temperatures, solvation chemistry, electrolyte decomposition, ternary solvation sheath, positive electrode electrolyte interphase, capacity retention, Coulombic efficiency

### 95. ❌ Bio-inspired asymmetric Zn-N2O2 single-atom catalysts via natural skeleton for efficient N-alkylation of nitroarenes with alcohols

**作者**: Yu Huang, Yong Li, Xiaogang Yin, Qiudi Zhu, He Mei, Xueqin Chang, Xi Liu, Wu Li, Aiwen Lei, Xianglin Pei
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是化学催化领域，具体涉及单原子催化剂（Zn/CS）在硝基芳烃与醇的N-烷基化反应中的应用，通过生物质壳聚糖骨架构建不对称Zn-N2O2位点。全文内容完全围绕催化剂设计、反应机理和催化性能展开，未涉及任何医学图像分析、医学成像或深度学习在医学成像中的应用。因此，所有关键词与论文主题完全无关。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文通过生物质壳聚糖骨架构建了具有不对称Zn-N2O2位点的单原子催化剂，首次实现了硝基芳烃与醇的借氢反应中异相锌单原子催化剂的高效N-烷基化，展现出优异的催化活性、广泛的底物范围和良好的可重复使用性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 尽管通过借氢策略实现硝基芳烃与醇类N-烷基化反应的非贵金属催化剂已取得显著进展，但在温和反应条件下获得兼具优异活性、可重复使用性及广泛底物适用性的催化剂仍具挑战。单原子催化剂（SACs）凭借其独特的配位/电子结构，有望成为该反应的潜在候选材料。本研究首次创新性地利用生物质壳聚糖（记为Zn/CS）的天然骨架，制备了具有不对称Zn-N<sub>2</sub>O<sub>2</sub>位点的仿生锌单原子催化剂，并实现了非均相锌单原子催化剂在硝基芳烃与醇类借氢反应中的首次应用。结果表明，Zn/CS的天然骨架（类似配体）与纳米孔结构诱导的不对称Zn-N<sub>2</sub>O<sub>2</sub>位点显著提升了硝基芳烃与醇类的N-烷基化效率。值得注意的是，该催化剂在已报道的非均相催化剂中表现出最高的转换频率（TOF），同时具备广泛的底物适用范围（56个实例）和优异的可重复使用性。此外，通过结合理论计算对催化路径/机理进行研究，发现具有缺电子特性的不对称Zn-N<sub>2</sub>O<sub>2</sub>位点能促进Zn/CS与Ph-CH<sub>2</sub>O<sup>-</sup>之间形成Zn-H键和Zn-O键，从而易于生成过渡态Ph-CH<sub>2</sub>O*并驱动整个反应进程。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Although significant developments are made in non-noble metal catalysts for N-alkylation of nitroarenes with alcohols via borrowing hydrogen strategy, obtaining catalysts with superior activity, reusability and broad substrate scope under mild reaction conditions remains challenging. Single-atom catalysts (SACs) hold unique coordination/electron structures, to be the potential candidates for this reaction. In this study, we firstly and creatively fabricate bio-inspired Zn SACs with asymmetric Zn-N<sub>2</sub>O<sub>2</sub> sites by utilizing the natural skeleton of biomass chitosan (denoted as Zn/CS), and achieve the first instance of heterogeneous Zn SACs in borrowing hydrogen reaction between nitroarenes and alcohols. The results reveal that the asymmetric Zn-N<sub>2</sub>O<sub>2</sub> sites induced by natural skeleton (like ligands) and nanoporous structure of Zn/CS significantly promote the N-alkylation efficiency of nitroarenes with alcohols. Notably, the Zn/CS exhibits the highest turnover frequency (TOF) among the reported heterogeneous catalysts, as well as wide substrate scope (56 examples) and excellent reusability. Furthermore, the catalytic pathway/mechanism is investigated by combing theoretical calculations, which reveals that the asymmetric Zn-N<sub>2</sub>O<sub>2</sub> sites with electron-deficient character can facilitate the formation of Zn-H and Zn-O bonds between Zn/CS and Ph-CH<sub>2</sub>O<sup>-</sup>, thus easily generating the transition state Ph-CH<sub>2</sub>O* and driving the whole reaction.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: single-atom catalysts, Zn-N2O2 sites, N-alkylation, nitroarenes, borrowing hydrogen, biomass chitosan, heterogeneous catalysis, asymmetric coordination

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了通过调控聚合物半导体中玻璃相的形成路径来优化其光电性能，发现玻璃态可作为主动设计参数而非被动结构副产物，为下一代光电器件提供了新的加工-结构-性能关系范式。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 有机电子器件中的活性层通常包含大量玻璃态（非晶）区域，其作用相较于晶态区域在很大程度上仍未得到充分探索。本文研究表明，这些玻璃相的热力学状态可作为调控聚合物半导体光电特性的关键调控杠杆。以聚（9,9-二正辛基芴-2,7-二基）（PFO）为模型体系，我们证明通过控制玻璃化动力学以及从不同液态前驱体（包括各向同性相和液晶中间相）形成玻璃态，可获得具有显著不同微观结构和光致发光特性的玻璃态PFO薄膜。这些结果揭示了玻璃形成路径与功能性电子行为之间的直接关联，从而将玻璃态确立为一种主动的设计参数，而非被动的结构副产物。因此，我们的研究结果在聚合物半导体的加工-结构-性能关系中引入了范式转变，并为通过玻璃相工程提升下一代光电器件的效率和稳定性开辟了新途径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Active layers in organic electronic devices often contain extensive glassy (non-crystalline) regions whose roles remain largely uncharted compared to their crystalline counterparts. Here, we demonstrate that the thermodynamic state of these glassy phases constitutes a powerful lever for tuning the optoelectronic properties of polymer semiconductors. Using poly(9,9-di-n-octylfluorenyl-2,7-diyl) (PFO) as a model system, we show that controlled vitrification kinetics and formation from distinct liquid precursors-including isotropic and liquid-crystalline mesophases-yield glassy PFO films with markedly different microstructures and photoluminescence characteristics. These results uncover direct correlations between glass formation pathways and functional electronic behavior, establishing the glassy state as an active design parameter rather than a passive structural byproduct. Our findings thus introduce a paradigm shift in the processing-structure-property relationships of polymer semiconductors and open new avenues for glass-phase engineering toward enhanced efficiency and stability in next-generation optoelectronic devices.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: polymer semiconductors, glassy phase, optoelectronic properties, vitrification kinetics, microstructure, photoluminescence, glass-phase engineering, processing-structure-property relationships

    该研究通过冷冻电镜解析了裸藻光系统I-捕光复合物超复合体的高分辨率结构，揭示了其独特的双层天线排列和色素网络，阐明了次级质体如何重塑光捕获结构以支持光合作用的谱系特异性策略。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 光系统I（PSI）通过捕光复合物（LHCs）捕获光能以驱动电子转移。眼虫（Euglena gracilis）作为一种次级内共生的绿藻，其PSI-LHCs超复合物的结构此前尚未得到解析。本文报道了眼虫PSI-LHCI-LHCII超复合物的2.06 Å冷冻电镜结构，揭示了一个最小的PSI核心，其PsaM侧结合有十个天线蛋白，并排列为两层。每个内层与外层LHC形成面对面配对，而四个LHCI异二聚体通过保守的Loop_23基序稳定，组装成两个四聚体，并由一个中央LHCI-LHCII对连接。值得注意的是，在PsaD亚基中观察到一个约40个残基的插入片段，该片段锚定了LHC-3并稳定了LHC带。此外，眼虫特有的叶绿素分子以及红色叶绿素的独特排列构成了一个特异的色素网络，将激发能导向核心。这些发现揭示了一种谱系特异的捕光策略，凸显了次级质体如何重塑PSI-LHCs结构以支持光合作用。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Photosystem I (PSI) harvests light through light-harvesting complexes (LHCs) to drive electron transfer. Euglena gracilis, a secondary endosymbiotic green alga, yet the architecture of its PSI-LHCs supercomplex has remained unresolved. Here, we report a 2.06 Å cryo-electron microscopy structure of the E. gracilis PSI-LHCI-LHCII supercomplex, revealing a minimal PSI core associated with ten antennas arranged in two layers on the PsaM-facing side. Each inner and outer LHC forms a face-to-face pair, while four LHCI heterodimers, stabilized by conserved Loop_23 motifs, assemble into two tetramers bridged by a central LHCI-LHCII pair. Notably, a ~ 40-residue insertion in PsaD was observed, anchoring LHC-3 and stabilizing LHC belts. Moreover, Euglena-specific chlorophylls and a distinctive arrangement of red chlorophylls establish a distinct pigment network, channeling excitation-energy into the core. These findings uncover a lineage-specific strategy for light-harvesting, highlighting how secondary plastids remodel PSI-LHCs architecture to support photosynthesis.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Photosystem I, light-harvesting complexes, cryo-electron microscopy, Euglena gracilis, chlorophyll arrangement, energy transfer pathways, supercomplex architecture, secondary endosymbiosis

### 100. ❌ Structural insights into insect-selective sodium channel toxins drive AI-enhanced biopesticide design

**作者**: Heng Jiang, Ruibo Gao, Huiqin Xu, Cheng Wang, Shuyue Ma, Yishu Gong, Lianyun Lin, Lina Yang, Xiang Li, Ye Liu, Rongcai Lu, Jun-An Ma, Jinbo Xu, Ke Dong, Filip Van Petegem, Zheng Liu, Shaoying Wu, Zhiguang Yuchi
**期刊/来源**: nature_communications
**发布日期**: 2026-03-05

**评分**: 0.0 / 14.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

!!! info Semantic Scholar TL;DR

    Cryoelectron microscopy structures of the insect sodium channel NavPaS bound to two naturally occurring insect-selective toxins reveal the molecular determinants of insect selectivity and highlight the molecular coevolution of toxin-channel interactions, as corroborated by electrophysiology and toxicity assays.

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    评分失败，无法生成摘要

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 许多以电压门控钠通道为靶点的动物多肽毒素因其对昆虫的强效性和选择性而闻名。理解这些毒素为何能选择性作用于昆虫钠通道而非哺乳动物同源通道，对于开发更安全、更有效的害虫防治剂至关重要。本文报道了昆虫钠通道Na<sub>v</sub>PaS与两种天然昆虫选择性毒素复合物的冷冻电镜（cryo-EM）结构，这两种毒素分别为来自海葵的Av3和来自蝎子的LqhαIT。两种毒素均结合于Na<sub>v</sub>PaS的电压传感结构域4（VSD4），并通过将S4螺旋稳定在失活构象来破坏通道的快失活过程。其中，Av3作用于VSD4与孔道结构域1（PD1）之间的膜嵌入位点，而LqhαIT则结合于经典的神经毒素位点3，这阐明了两种不同的结合模式最终汇聚于共同作用机制的现象。这些结构揭示了昆虫选择性的分子决定因素，并凸显了毒素与通道相互作用的分子协同进化，电生理学和毒性实验数据进一步证实了这一点。基于这些发现，我们应用人工智能驱动的蛋白质设计工具来提升LqhαIT的杀虫效力，通过杀虫生物测定证实，获得了一种效力显著提升一倍的变体。本研究阐明了钠通道调控的多样机制，并为基于结构指导、人工智能驱动的毒素类生物农药设计提供了框架。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Many voltage-gated sodium channel-targeting animal peptide toxins are renowned for their potency and selectivity against insects. Understanding why these toxins selectively target insect sodium channels over their mammalian counterparts is crucial for developing safer and more effective pest control agents. Here, we present the cryoelectron microscopy (cryo-EM) structures of the insect sodium channel Na<sub>v</sub>PaS bound to two naturally occurring insect-selective toxins, Av3 from the sea anemone and LqhαIT from the scorpion. Both toxins bind to the voltage-sensing domain 4 (VSD4) of Na<sub>v</sub>PaS and disrupt fast inactivation by stabilizing the S4 segment in a deactivated conformation. While Av3 engages a membrane-embedded site between VSD4 and pore domain 1 (PD1), LqhαIT binds to the classical neurotoxin site 3, illustrating distinct binding modes that converge on a shared mechanism of action. These structures reveal the molecular determinants of insect selectivity and highlight the molecular coevolution of toxin-channel interactions, as corroborated by electrophysiology and toxicity assays. Leveraging these insights, we apply AI-driven protein design tools to increase the insecticidal potency of LqhαIT, resulting in a variant with a remarkable doubling in efficacy, as we confirm by insecticidal bioassays. This study illuminates the diverse mechanisms of sodium channel modulation and provides a framework for the structure-guided, AI-driven design of toxin-based biopesticides.

</details>
<br>

---
